**v2** "Do you think this is just?You say, 'I am more righteous than God.'[^1]
**v3** For you ask, 'What does it profit me, and what benefit do I gain apart from sin?'
**v4** I will reply to you and to your friends as well.
**v5** Look to the heavens and see; gaze at the clouds high above you.
**v6** If you sin, what do you accomplish against Him?If you multiply your transgressions, what do you do to Him?
**v7** If you are righteous, what do you give Him, or what does He receive from your hand?
**v8** Your wickedness affects only a man like yourself, and your righteousness only a son of man.

**v9** Men cry out under great oppression; they plead for relief from the arm of the mighty.
**v10** But no one asks, 'Where is God my Maker, who gives us songs in the night,
**v11** who teaches us more than the beasts of the earthand makes us wiser than the birds of the air?'
**v12** There they cry out, but He does not answer, because of the pride of evil men.
**v13** Surely God does not listen to empty pleas, and the Almighty does not take note of it.
**v14** How much less, then, when you say that you do not see Him, that your case is before Him and you must wait for Him,
**v15** and further, that in His anger He has not punishedor taken much notice of folly!
**v16** So Job opens his mouth in vainand multiplies words without knowledge."
[^1]: Or 'I am righteous before God.' ( 35:2)

### Chapter 36

#### Elihu Describes God's Power
**v1** And Elihu continued:

**v2** "Bear with me a little longer, and I will show youthat there is more to be said on God's behalf.
**v3** I get my knowledge from afar, and I will ascribe justice to my Maker.
**v4** For truly my words are free of falsehood; one perfect in knowledge is with you.

**v5** Indeed, God is mighty, but He despises no one; He is mighty in strength of understanding.
**v6** He does not keep the wicked alive, but He grants justice to the afflicted.
**v7** He does not take His eyes off the righteous, but He enthrones them with kingsand exalts them forever.

**v8** And if men are bound with chains, caught in cords of affliction,
**v9** then He tells them their deedsand how arrogantly they have transgressed.
**v10** He opens their ears to correctionand commands that they turn from iniquity.
**v11** If they obey and serve Him, then they end their days in prosperityand their years in happiness.
**v12** But if they do not obey, then they perish by the sword [^1] and die without knowledge.

**v13** The godless in heart harbor resentment; even when He binds them, they do not cry for help.
**v14** They die in their youth, among the male shrine prostitutes.
**v15** God rescues the afflicted by their affliction [^2] and opens their ears in oppression.

**v16** Indeed, He drew you from the jaws of distressto a spacious and broad place, to a table full of richness.
**v17** But now you are laden with the judgment due the wicked; judgment and justice have seized you.
**v18** Be careful that no one lures you with riches; do not let a large bribe lead you astray.
**v19** Can your wealth [^3] or all your mighty effortkeep you from distress?
**v20** Do not long for the night, when people vanish from their homes.
**v21** Be careful not to turn to iniquity, for this you have preferred to affliction.

**v22** Behold, God is exalted in His power.Who is a teacher like Him?
**v23** Who has appointed His way for Him, or told Him, 'You have done wrong'?
**v24** Remember to magnify His work, which men have praised in song.
**v25** All mankind has seen it; men behold it from afar.
**v26** Indeed, God is great—beyond our knowledge; the number of His years is unsearchable.
**v27** For He draws up drops of waterwhich distill the rain from the mist,
**v28** which the clouds pour outand shower abundantly on mankind.
**v29** Furthermore, who can understand how the clouds spread out, how the thunder roars from His pavilion?
**v30** See how He scatters His lightning around Himand covers the depths of the sea.
**v31** For by these He judges [^4] the nationsand provides food in abundance.
**v32** He fills His hands with lightningand commands it to strike its mark.
**v33** The thunder declares His presence; even the cattle regard the rising storm.
[^1]: Or they will cross the river of death ( 36:12)
[^2]: Or in their affliction ( 36:15)
[^3]: Or your cry for help ( 36:19)
[^4]: Or governs or nourishes ( 36:31)

### Chapter 37

#### Elihu Proclaims God's Majesty
**v1** "At this my heart also poundsand leaps from its place.
**v2** Listen closely to the thunder of His voiceand the rumbling that comes from His mouth.
**v3** He unleashes His lightning beneath the whole skyand sends it to the ends of the earth.
**v4** Then there comes a roaring sound; He thunders with His majestic voice.He does not restrain the lightningwhen His voice resounds.
**v5** God thunders wondrously with His voice; He does great things we cannot comprehend.
**v6** For He says to the snow, 'Fall on the earth,'and to the gentle rain, 'Pour out a mighty downpour.'
**v7** He seals up the hand of every man, so that all men may know His work.
**v8** The wild animals enter their lairs; they settle down in their dens.
**v9** The tempest comes from its chamber, and the cold from the driving north winds.
**v10** By the breath of God the ice is formedand the watery expanses are frozen.
**v11** He loads the clouds with moisture; He scatters His lightning through them.
**v12** They swirl about, whirling at His direction, accomplishing all that He commandsover the face of all the earth.
**v13** Whether for punishment or for His land, He accomplishes this in His loving devotion.

**v14** Listen to this, O Job; stand still and consider the wonders of God.
**v15** Do you know how God dispatches the cloudsor makes the lightning flash?
**v16** Do you understand how the clouds float, those wonders of Him who is perfect in knowledge?
**v17** You whose clothes get hotwhen the land lies hushed under the south wind,
**v18** can you, like Him, spread out the skies, as strong as a mirror of bronze?

**v19** Teach us what we should say to Him; we cannot draw up our case because of our darkness.
**v20** Should He be told that I want to speak?Would a man ask to be swallowed up [^1]?
**v21** Now no one can gaze at the sunwhen it is bright in the skiesafter the wind has swept them clean.
**v22** Out of the north He comes in golden splendor; awesome majesty surrounds Him.
**v23** The Almighty is beyond our reach; He is exalted in power!In His justice and great righteousness He does not oppress.
**v24** Therefore, men fear Him, for He is not partial to the wise in heart."
[^1]: Or speak without being swallowed up ( 37:20)

### Chapter 38

#### The LORD Challenges Job
**v1** Then the LORD answered Job out of the whirlwind and said:

**v2** "Who is this who obscures My counselby words without knowledge? [^1]
**v3** Now brace yourself [^2] like a man; I will question you, and you shall inform Me. [^3]
**v4** Where were you when I laid the foundations of the earth?Tell Me, if you have understanding.
**v5** Who fixed its measurements? Surely you know!Or who stretched a measuring line across it?
**v6** On what were its foundations set, or who laid its cornerstone, [^4]
**v7** while the morning stars sang togetherand all the sons of God shouted for joy?

**v8** Who enclosed the sea behind doorswhen it burst forth from the womb,
**v9** when I made the clouds its garmentand thick darkness its blanket,
**v10** when I fixed its boundariesand set in place its bars and doors,
**v11** and I declared: 'You may come this far, but no farther; here your proud waves must stop'?

**v12** In your days, have you commanded the morningor assigned the dawn its place,
**v13** that it might spread to the ends of the earthand shake the wicked out of it?
**v14** The earth takes shape like clay under a seal; its hills stand out like the folds of a garment.
**v15** Light is withheld from the wicked, and their upraised arm is broken.

**v16** Have you journeyed to the vents of the seaor walked in the trenches of the deep?
**v17** Have the gates of death been revealed to you?Have you seen the gates of the shadow of death?
**v18** Have you surveyed the extent of the earth?Tell Me, if you know all this.

**v19** Where is the way to the home of light?Do you know where darkness resides,
**v20** so you can lead it back to its border?Do you know the paths to its home?
**v21** Surely you know, for you were already born!And the number of your days is great!

**v22** Have you entered the storehouses of snowor observed the storehouses of hail,
**v23** which I hold in reserve for times of trouble, for the day of war and battle?
**v24** In which direction is the lightning dispersed, or the east wind scattered over the earth?

**v25** Who cuts a channel for the floodor clears a path for the thunderbolt,
**v26** to bring rain on a barren land, on a desert where no man lives,
**v27** to satisfy the parched wastelandand make it sprout with tender grass?
**v28** Does the rain have a father?Who has begotten the drops of dew?
**v29** From whose womb does the ice emerge?Who gives birth to the frost from heaven,
**v30** when the waters become hard as stoneand the surface of the deep is frozen?

**v31** Can you bind the chains of the Pleiadesor loosen the belt of Orion?
**v32** Can you bring forth the constellations in their seasons [^5] or lead out the Bear [^6] and her cubs?
**v33** Do you know the laws of the heavens?Can you set their dominion over the earth?
**v34** Can you command the cloudsso that a flood of water covers you?
**v35** Can you send the lightning bolts on their way?Do they report to you, 'Here we are'?

**v36** Who has put wisdom in the heart [^7] or given understanding to the mind?
**v37** Who has the wisdom to count the clouds?Or who can tilt the water jars of the heavens
**v38** when the dust hardens into a massand the clods of earth stick together?

**v39** Can you hunt the prey for a lionessor satisfy the hunger of young lions
**v40** when they crouch in their densand lie in wait in the thicket?
**v41** Who provides food for the ravenwhen its young cry out to Godas they wander about for lack of food?
[^1]: Cited in Job 42:3 ( 38:2)
[^2]: Hebrew gird up your loins ( 38:3)
[^3]: Cited in Job 42:4 ( 38:3)
[^4]: Or who set its core in place ( 38:6)
[^5]: Or bring forth Mazzaroth in its season ( 38:32)
[^6]: Or Leo or Arcturus ( 38:32)
[^7]: Or Who has given the ibis wisdom, that is, wisdom about the flooding of the Nile ( 38:36)

### Chapter 39

#### The LORD Speaks of His Creation
**v1** "Do you know when mountain goats give birth?Have you watched the doe bear her fawn?
**v2** Can you count the months they are pregnant?Do you know the time they give birth?
**v3** They crouch down and bring forth their young; they deliver their newborn.
**v4** Their young ones thrive and grow up in the open field; they leave and do not return.

**v5** Who set the wild donkey free?Who released the swift donkey from the harness?
**v6** I made the wilderness his homeand the salt flats his dwelling.
**v7** He scorns the tumult of the cityand never hears the shouts of a driver.
**v8** He roams the mountains for pasture, searching for any green thing.

**v9** Will the wild ox consent to serve you?Will he stay by your manger at night?
**v10** Can you hold him to the furrow with a harness?Will he plow the valleys behind you?
**v11** Can you rely on his great strength?Will you leave your hard work to him?
**v12** Can you trust him to bring in your grainand gather it to your threshing floor?

**v13** The wings of the ostrich flap joyfully, but cannot match the pinions [^1] and feathers of the stork.
**v14** For she leaves her eggs on the groundand lets them warm in the sand.
**v15** She forgets that a foot may crush them, or a wild animal may trample them.
**v16** She treats her young harshly, as if not her own, with no concern that her labor was in vain.
**v17** For God has deprived her of wisdom; He has not endowed her with understanding.
**v18** Yet when she proudly spreads her wings, she laughs at the horse and its rider.

**v19** Do you give strength to the horseor adorn his neck with a mane?
**v20** Do you make him leap like a locust, striking terror with his proud snorting?
**v21** He paws in the valley and rejoices in his strength; he charges into battle.
**v22** He laughs at fear, frightened of nothing; he does not turn back from the sword.
**v23** A quiver rattles at his side, along with a flashing spear and lance. [^2]
**v24** Trembling with excitement, he devours the distance; he cannot stand still when the ram's horn sounds.
**v25** At the blast of the horn, he snorts with fervor. [^3] He catches the scent of battle from afar, the shouts of captains and the cry of war.

**v26** Does the hawk take flight by your understandingand spread his wings toward the south?
**v27** Does the eagle soar at your commandand make his nest on high?
**v28** He dwells on a cliff and lodges there; his stronghold is on a rocky crag.
**v29** From there he spies out food; his eyes see it from afar.
**v30** His young ones feast on blood; and where the slain are, there he is."
[^1]: Pinions are the outer parts of a bird's wings, including the flight feathers. ( 39:13)
[^2]: Or javelin ( 39:23)
[^3]: Or he snorts, 'Aha!' ( 39:25)

### Chapter 40

#### Job Humbles Himself before the LORD
**v1** And the LORD said to Job:

**v2** "Will the faultfinder contend with the Almighty?Let him who argues with God give an answer."

**v3** Then Job answered the LORD:

**v4** "Behold, I am insignificant. How can I reply to You?I place my hand over my mouth.
**v5** I have spoken once, but I have no answer—twice, but I have nothing to add."
#### The LORD Challenges Job Again

**v6** Then the LORD answered Job out of the whirlwind and said:

**v7** "Now brace yourself [^1] like a man; I will question you, and you shall inform Me. [^2]

**v8** Would you really annul My justice?Would you condemn Me to justify yourself?
**v9** Do you have an arm like God's?Can you thunder with a voice like His?
**v10** Then adorn yourself with majesty and splendor, and clothe yourself with honor and glory.
**v11** Unleash the fury of your wrath; look on every proud man and bring him low.
**v12** Look on every proud man and humble him; trample the wicked where they stand.
**v13** Bury them together in the dust; imprison them in the grave. [^3]
**v14** Then I will confess to youthat your own right hand can save you.

**v15** Look at Behemoth, which I made along with you.He feeds on grass like an ox.
**v16** See the strength of his loinsand the power in the muscles of his belly.
**v17** His tail sways like a cedar; the sinews of his thighs are tightly knit.
**v18** His bones are tubes of bronze; his limbs are rods of iron.
**v19** He is the foremost of God's works; [^4] only his Maker can draw the sword against him.
**v20** The hills yield him their produce, while all the beasts of the field play nearby.
**v21** He lies under the lotus plants, [^5] hidden among the reeds of the marsh.
**v22** The lotus plants conceal him in their shade; the willows [^6] of the brook surround him.
**v23** Though the river rages, Behemoth is unafraid; he remains secure, though the Jordan surges to his mouth.
**v24** Can anyone capture him as he looks on, or pierce his nose with a snare?
[^1]: Hebrew gird up your loins ( 40:7)
[^2]: Cited in Job 42:4 ( 40:7)
[^3]: Or in the hidden place ( 40:13)
[^4]: Hebrew ways ( 40:19)
[^5]: Or bramble bushes; also in verse 22 ( 40:21)
[^6]: Or poplars ( 40:22)

### Chapter 41

#### The LORD's Power Shown in Leviathan
**v1** "Can you pull in Leviathan with a hookor tie down his tongue with a rope?
**v2** Can you put a cord through his noseor pierce his jaw with a hook?
**v3** Will he beg you for mercyor speak to you softly?
**v4** Will he make a covenant with youto take him as a slave for life?
**v5** Can you pet him like a birdor put him on a leash for your maidens?
**v6** Will traders barter for himor divide him among the merchants?
**v7** Can you fill his hide with harpoonsor his head with fishing spears?
**v8** If you lay a hand on him, you will remember the battle and never repeat it!

**v9** Surely hope of overcoming him is false.Is not the sight of him overwhelming?
**v10** No one is so fierce as to rouse Leviathan.Then who is able to stand against Me?
**v11** Who has given to Me that I should repay him? [^1] Everything under heaven is Mine.

**v12** I cannot keep silent about his limbs, his power and graceful form.
**v13** Who can strip off his outer coat?Who can approach him with a bridle? [^2]
**v14** Who can open his jaws, ringed by his fearsome teeth?
**v15** His rows of scales are his pride, tightly sealed together.
**v16** One scale is so near to anotherthat no air can pass between them.
**v17** They are joined to one another; they clasp and cannot be separated.

**v18** His snorting flashes with light, and his eyes are like the rays of dawn.
**v19** Firebrands stream from his mouth; fiery sparks shoot forth!
**v20** Smoke billows from his nostrilsas from a boiling pot over burning reeds.
**v21** His breath sets coals ablaze, and flames pour from his mouth.
**v22** Strength resides in his neck, and dismay leaps before him.
**v23** The folds of his flesh are tightly joined; they are firm and immovable.
**v24** His chest is as hard as a rock, as hard as a lower millstone!

**v25** When Leviathan rises up, the mighty are terrified; they withdraw before his thrashing.
**v26** The sword that reaches him has no effect, nor does the spear or dart or arrow.
**v27** He regards iron as strawand bronze as rotten wood.
**v28** No arrow can make him flee; slingstones become like chaff to him.
**v29** A club is regarded as straw, and he laughs at the sound of the lance. [^3]
**v30** His undersides are jagged potsherds, spreading out the mud like a threshing sledge.
**v31** He makes the depths seethe like a cauldron; he makes the sea like a jar of ointment.
**v32** He leaves a glistening wake behind him; one would think the deep had white hair!
**v33** Nothing on earth is his equal—a creature devoid of fear!
**v34** He looks down on all the haughty; he is king over all the proud."
[^1]: Cited in Romans 11:35 ( 41:11)
[^2]: Or Who can come within his double mail? ( 41:13)
[^3]: Or javelin ( 41:29)

### Chapter 42

#### Job Submits Himself to the LORD
**v1** Then Job replied to the LORD:

**v2** "I know that You can do all thingsand that no plan of Yours can be thwarted.
**v3** You asked, 'Who is thiswho conceals My counsel without knowledge?'[^1] Surely I spoke of things I did not understand, things too wonderful for me to know.
**v4** You said, 'Listen now, and I will speak.I will question you, and you shall inform Me.'[^2]
**v5** My ears had heard of You, but now my eyes have seen You.
**v6** Therefore I despise myself, and I repent in dust and ashes."
#### The LORD Rebukes Job's Friends

**v7** After the LORD had spoken these words to Job, He said to Eliphaz the Temanite, "My wrath is kindled against you and your two friends. For you have not spoken about Me accurately, as My servant Job has.
**v8** So now, take seven bulls and seven rams, go to My servant Job, and sacrifice a burnt offering for yourselves. Then My servant Job will pray for you, for I will accept his prayer and not deal with you according to your folly. For you have not spoken accurately about Me, as My servant Job has."

**v9** So Eliphaz the Temanite, Bildad the Shuhite, and Zophar the Naamathite went and did as the LORD had told them; and the LORD accepted Job's prayer.
#### The LORD Blesses Job

**v10** After Job had prayed for his friends, the LORD restored his prosperity and doubled his former possessions.
**v11** All his brothers and sisters and prior acquaintances came and dined with him in his house. They consoled him and comforted him over all the adversity that the LORD had brought upon him. And each one gave him a piece of silver [^3] and a gold ring.

**v12** So the LORD blessed Job's latter days more than his first. He owned 14,000 sheep, 6,000 camels, 1,000 yoke of oxen, and 1,000 female donkeys.
**v13** And he also had seven sons and three daughters.
**v14** He named his first daughter Jemimah, his second Keziah, and his third Keren-happuch.
**v15** No women as beautiful as Job's daughters could be found in all the land, and their father granted them an inheritance among their brothers.

**v16** After this, Job lived 140 years and saw his children and their children to the fourth generation.
**v17** And so Job died, old and full of years.
[^1]: Job 38:2 ( 42:3)
[^2]: Job 38:3 and Job 40:7 ( 42:4)
[^3]: Hebrew a kesitah; the value or weight of the kesitah is no longer known. ( 42:11)

## Psalms

### Chapter 1

#### The Two Paths

**v1** Blessed is the manwho does not walk in the counsel of the wicked, or set foot on the path of sinners, or sit in the seat of mockers.
**v2** But his delight is in the Law of the LORD, and on His law he meditates day and night.
**v3** He is like a tree planted by streams of water, yielding its fruit in season, whose leaf does not wither, and who prospers in all he does.

**v4** Not so the wicked!For they are like chaff driven off by the wind.
**v5** Therefore the wicked will not stand in the judgment, nor sinners in the assembly of the righteous.

**v6** For the LORD guards the path of the righteous, but the way of the wicked will perish.
### Chapter 2

#### The Triumphant Messiah
**v1** Why do the nations rage [^1] and the peoples plot in vain?
**v2** The kings of the earth take their standand the rulers gather together, against the LORDand against His Anointed One: [^2]
**v3** "Let us break Their chainsand cast away Their cords."

**v4** The One enthroned in heaven laughs; the Lord taunts them.
**v5** Then He rebukes them in His anger, and terrifies them in His fury:
**v6** "I have installed My King on Zion, upon My holy mountain."

**v7** I will proclaim the decreespoken to Me by the LORD: "You are My Son; today I have become Your Father. [^3]
**v8** Ask Me, and I will make the nations Your inheritance, the ends of the earth Your possession.
**v9** You will break them [^4] with an iron scepter; You will shatter them like pottery. [^5]"

**v10** Therefore be wise, O kings; be admonished, O judges of the earth.
**v11** Serve the LORD with fear, and rejoice with trembling.
**v12** Kiss the Son, lest He be angryand you perish in your rebellion, when His wrath ignites in an instant.Blessed are all who take refuge in Him.
[^1]: Or noisily assemble; see Revelation 11:18. ( 2:1)
[^2]: Cited in Acts 4:25–26 ( 2:2)
[^3]: Literally today I have begotten You; cited in Acts 13:33, Hebrews 1:5, and Hebrews 5:5 ( 2:7)
[^4]: LXX You will rule them or You will shepherd them ( 2:9)
[^5]: Cited in Revelation 2:27; see also Revelation 12:5 and Revelation 19:15. ( 2:9)

### Chapter 3

#### Deliver Me, O LORD!

**v1** O LORD, how my foes have increased!How many rise up against me!
**v2** Many say of me,"God will not deliver him." Selah [^1]
**v3** But You, O LORD, are a shield around me, my glory, and the One who lifts my head.
**v4** To the LORD I cry aloud, and He answers me from His holy mountain.Selah
**v5** I lie down and sleep; I wake again, for the LORD sustains me.
**v6** I will not fear the myriadsset against me on every side.

**v7** Arise, O LORD!Save me, O my God!Strike all my enemies on the jaw; break the teeth of the wicked.
**v8** Salvation belongs to the LORD; may Your blessing be on Your people.Selah
[^1]: Selah or Interlude is probably a musical or literary term; here and throughout the Psalms. ( 3:2)

### Chapter 4

#### Answer Me When I Call!

**v1** Answer me when I call, O God of my righteousness!You have relieved my distress; show me grace and hear my prayer.

**v2** How long, O men, will my honor be maligned?How long will you love vanity and seek after lies [^1]?Selah
**v3** Know that the LORD has set apart the godly for Himself; the LORD hears when I call to Him.

**v4** Be angry, yet do not sin; [^2] on your bed, search your heart and be still.Selah
**v5** Offer the sacrifices of the righteousand trust in the LORD.

**v6** Many ask, "Who can show us the good?" Shine the light of Your face upon us, O LORD.
**v7** You have filled my heart with more joythan when grain and new wine abound.
**v8** I will lie down and sleep in peace, for You alone, O LORD, make me dwell in safety.
[^1]: Or false gods ( 4:2)
[^2]: Or In your anger do not sin or Tremble and do not sin; cited in Ephesians 4:26 ( 4:4)

### Chapter 5

#### Give Ear to My Words

**v1** Give ear to my words, O LORD; consider my groaning.
**v2** Attend to the sound of my cry, my King and my God, for to You I pray.

**v3** In the morning, O LORD, You hear my voice; at daybreak I lay my plea before Youand wait in expectation.

**v4** For You are not a God who delights in wickedness; no evil can dwell with You.
**v5** The boastful cannot stand in Your presence; You hate all workers of iniquity.
**v6** You destroy those who tell lies; the LORD abhors the man of bloodshed and deceit.

**v7** But I will enter Your houseby the abundance of Your loving devotion; [^1] in reverence I will bow downtoward Your holy temple.

**v8** Lead me, O LORD, in Your righteousnessbecause of my enemies; make straight Your way before me.
**v9** For not a word they speak can be trusted; destruction lies within them.Their throats are open graves; their tongues practice deceit. [^2]

**v10** Declare them guilty, O God; let them fall by their own devices.Drive them out for their many transgressions, for they have rebelled against You.

**v11** But let all who take refuge in You rejoice; let them ever shout for joy.May You shelter them, that those who love Your name may rejoice in You.
**v12** For surely You, O LORD, bless the righteous; You surround them with the shield of Your favor.
[^1]: Forms of the Hebrew chesed are translated here and in most cases throughout the Scriptures as loving devotion; the range of meaning includes love, goodness, kindness, faithfulness, and mercy, as well as loyalty to a covenant. ( 5:7)
[^2]: Or flattery; cited in Romans 3:13 ( 5:9)

### Chapter 6

#### Do Not Rebuke Me in Your Anger

**v1** O LORD, do not rebuke me in Your angeror discipline me in Your wrath.
**v2** Be merciful to me, O LORD, for I am frail; heal me, O LORD, for my bones are in agony.
**v3** My soul is deeply distressed.How long, O LORD, how long?

**v4** Turn, O LORD, and deliver my soul; save me because of Your loving devotion.
**v5** For there is no mention of You in death; who can praise You from Sheol?

**v6** I am weary from groaning; all night I flood my bed with weepingand drench my couch with tears.
**v7** My eyes fail from grief; they grow dim because of all my foes.

**v8** Depart from me, all you workers of iniquity, for the LORD has heard my weeping.
**v9** The LORD has heard my cry for mercy; the LORD accepts my prayer.
**v10** All my enemies will be ashamed and dismayed; they will turn back in sudden disgrace.
[^1]: Sheminith is probably a musical term; here and in 1 Chronicles 15:21 and Psalms 12:1. ( 6:0)

### Chapter 7

#### I Take Refuge in You

**v1** O LORD my God, I take refuge in You; save me and deliver me from all my pursuers,
**v2** or they will shred my soul like a lionand tear me to pieces with no one to rescue me.

**v3** O LORD my God, if I have done this, if injustice is on my hands,
**v4** if I have rewarded my ally [^2] with evil, if I have plundered my foe without cause,
**v5** then may my enemy pursue me and overtake me; may he trample me to the groundand leave my honor in the dust.Selah
**v6** Arise, O LORD, in Your anger; rise up against the fury of my enemies.Awake, my God, and ordain judgment.
**v7** Let the assembled peoples gather around You; take Your seat over them on high.
**v8** The LORD judges the peoples; vindicate me, O LORD, according to my righteousness and integrity.
**v9** Put an end to the evil of the wicked, but establish the righteous, O righteous God who searches hearts and minds. [^3]

**v10** My shield is with God, who saves the upright in heart.
**v11** God is a righteous judgeand a God who feels indignation each day.
**v12** If one does not repent, God will sharpen His sword; He has bent and strung His bow.
**v13** He has prepared His deadly weapons; He ordains His arrows with fire.

**v14** Behold, the wicked man travails with evil; he conceives trouble and births falsehood.
**v15** He has dug a hole and hollowed it out; he has fallen into a pit of his own making.
**v16** His trouble recoils on himself, and his violence falls on his own head.

**v17** I will thank the LORD for His righteousnessand sing praise to the name of the LORD Most High.
[^1]: Shiggaion is probably a musical or liturgical term. ( 7:0)
[^2]: Hebrew the one at peace with me ( 7:4)
[^3]: Hebrew hearts and kidneys ( 7:9)

### Chapter 8

#### How Majestic Is Your Name!

**v1** O LORD, our Lord, how majestic is Your name in all the earth!You have set Your gloryabove the heavens.
**v2** From the mouths of children and infants You have ordained praise [^2] on account of Your adversaries, to silence the enemy and avenger.

**v3** When I behold Your heavens, the work of Your fingers, the moon and the stars, which You have set in place—

**v4** what is man that You are mindful of him, or the son of man that You care for him?
**v5** You made him a little lower than the angels; [^3] You crowned him with glory and honor.
**v6** You made him ruler of the works of Your hands; You have placed everything under his feet: [^4]
**v7** all sheep and oxen, and even the beasts of the field,
**v8** the birds of the air and the fish of the sea, all that swim the paths of the seas.

**v9** O LORD, our Lord, how majestic is Your name in all the earth!
[^1]: Gittith is probably a musical or liturgical term; here and in Psalms 81 and 84. ( 8:0)
[^2]: Literally You have ordained strength; LXX You have prepared praise; cited in Matthew 21:16 ( 8:2)
[^3]: Or than God or than the heavenly beings; see also LXX. ( 8:5)
[^4]: Cited in 1 Corinthians 15:27 and Hebrews 2:6–8 ( 8:6)

### Chapter 9

#### I Will Give Thanks to the LORD

**v1** I will give thanks to the LORD with all my heart; I will recount all Your wonders.
**v2** I will be glad and rejoice in You; I will sing praise to Your name, O Most High.

**v3** When my enemies retreat, they stumble and perish before You.
**v4** For You have upheld my just cause; You sit on Your throne judging righteously.
**v5** You have rebuked the nations; You have destroyed the wicked; You have erased their name forever and ever.
**v6** The enemy has come to eternal ruin, and You have uprooted their cities; the very memory of them has vanished.

**v7** But the LORD abides forever; He has established His throne for judgment.
**v8** He judges the world with justice; He governs the people with equity.
**v9** The LORD is a refuge for the oppressed, a stronghold in times of trouble.
**v10** Those who know Your name trust in You, for You, O LORD, have not forsaken those who seek You.

**v11** Sing praises to the LORD, who dwells in Zion; proclaim His deeds among the nations.
**v12** For the Avenger of bloodshed remembers; He does not ignore the cry of the afflicted.

**v13** Be merciful to me, O LORD; see how my enemies afflict me!Lift me up from the gates of death,
**v14** that I may declare all Your praises—that within the gates of Daughter Zion I may rejoice in Your salvation.

**v15** The nations have fallen into a pit of their making; their feet are caught in the net they have hidden.
**v16** The LORD is known by the justice He brings; the wicked are ensnared by the work of their hands.Higgaion Selah [^2]
**v17** The wicked will return to Sheol—all the nations who forget God.
**v18** For the needy will not always be forgotten; nor the hope of the oppressed forever dashed.

**v19** Rise up, O LORD, do not let man prevail; let the nations be judged in Your presence.
**v20** Lay terror upon them, O LORD; let the nations know they are but men.Selah
[^1]: Psalms 9 and 10 together follow an acrostic pattern, each stanza beginning with the successive letters of the Hebrew alphabet. In the LXX they form one psalm. ( 9:0)
[^2]: Higgaion Selah or quiet interlude is probably a musical or liturgical term. ( 9:16)

### Chapter 10

#### The Perils of the Pilgrim
**v1** Why, O LORD, do You stand far off?Why do You hide in times of trouble?
**v2** In pride the wicked pursue the needy; let them be caught in the schemes they devise.

**v3** For the wicked man boasts in the cravings of his heart; he blesses the greedy and reviles the LORD.
**v4** In his pride the wicked man does not seek Him; in all his schemes there is no God.
**v5** He is secure in his ways at all times; Your lofty judgments are far from him; he sneers at all his foes.
**v6** He says to himself, "I will not be moved; from age to age I am free of distress."

**v7** His mouth is full of cursing, deceit, [^1] and violence; trouble and malice are under his tongue.
**v8** He lies in wait near the villages; in ambush he slays the innocent; his eyes watch in stealth for the helpless.
**v9** He lies in wait like a lion in a thicket; he lurks to seize the oppressed; he catches the lowly in his net.
**v10** They are crushed and beaten down; [^2] the helpless fall prey to his strength.
**v11** He says to himself, "God has forgotten; He hides His face and never sees."

**v12** Arise, O LORD! Lift up Your hand, O God!Do not forget the helpless.
**v13** Why has the wicked man renounced God?He says to himself, "You will never call me to account."
**v14** But You have regarded trouble and grief; You see to repay it by Your hand.The victim entrusts himself to You; You are the helper of the fatherless.
**v15** Break the arm of the wicked and evildoer; call him to account for his wickednessuntil none is left to be found.

**v16** The LORD is King forever and ever; the nations perish from His land.
**v17** You have heard, O LORD, the desire of the humble; You will strengthen their hearts.You will incline Your ear,
**v18** to vindicate the fatherless and oppressed, that the men of the earthmay strike terror no more.
[^1]: LXX bitterness; cited in Romans 3:14 ( 10:7)
[^2]: Or He crouches and lies low ( 10:10)

### Chapter 11

#### In the LORD I Take Refuge

**v1** In the LORD I take refuge.How then can you say to me: "Flee like a bird to your mountain!
**v2** For behold, the wicked bend their bows.They set their arrow on the stringto shoot from the shadows at the upright in heart.
**v3** If the foundations are destroyed, what can the righteous do?"

**v4** The LORD is in His holy temple; the LORD is on His heavenly throne.His eyes are watching closely; they examine the sons of men.
**v5** The LORD tests the righteous and the wicked; His soul hates the lover of violence.
**v6** On the wicked He will rain down fiery coals and sulfur; a scorching wind will be their portion.

**v7** For the LORD is righteous; He loves justice.The upright will see His face.
### Chapter 12

#### The Godly Are No More

**v1** Help, O LORD, for the godly are no more; the faithful have vanished from among men.
**v2** They lie to one another; they speak with flattering lips and a double heart.
**v3** May the LORD cut off all flattering lipsand every boastful tongue.
**v4** They say, "With our tongues we will prevail.We own our lips—who can be our master?"

**v5** "For the cause of the oppressedand for the groaning of the needy, I will now arise," says the LORD." I will bring safety to him who yearns."

**v6** The words of the LORD are flawless, like silver refined in a furnace, like gold purified sevenfold. [^2]
**v7** You, O LORD, will keep us; You will forever guard us from this generation.
**v8** The wicked wander freely, and vileness is exalted among men.
[^1]: Sheminith is probably a musical term; here and in 1 Chronicles 15:21 and Psalms 6:1. ( 12:0)
[^2]: Probable reading; MT like silver refined in a furnace of clay, purified sevenfold ( 12:6)

### Chapter 13

#### How Long, O LORD?

**v1** How long, O LORD?Will You forget me forever?How long will You hide Your face from me?
**v2** How long must I wrestle in my soul, with sorrow in my heart each day?How long will my enemy dominate me?

**v3** Consider me and respond, O LORD my God.Give light to my eyes, lest I sleep in death,
**v4** lest my enemy say, "I have overcome him,"and my foes rejoice when I fall.

**v5** But I have trusted in Your loving devotion; my heart will rejoice in Your salvation.
**v6** I will sing to the LORD, for He has been good to me.
### Chapter 14

#### The Fool Says There Is No God

**v1** The fool [^1] says in his heart,"There is no God." They are corrupt; their acts are vile.There is no one who does good.

**v2** The LORD looks down from heavenupon the sons of mento see if any understand, if any seek God.
**v3** All have turned away, they have together become corrupt; [^2] there is no one who does good, not even one. [^3]

**v4** Will the workers of iniquity never learn?They devour my people like bread; they refuse to call upon the LORD.
**v5** There they are, overwhelmed with dread, for God is in the company of the righteous.
**v6** You sinners frustrate the plans of the oppressed, yet the LORD is their shelter.

**v7** Oh, that the salvation of Israel would come from Zion!When the LORD restores His captive people, let Jacob rejoice, let Israel be glad!
[^1]: The Hebrew words rendered fool throughout the Psalms denote one who is morally deficient. ( 14:1)
[^2]: LXX worthless ( 14:3)
[^3]: Cited in Romans 3:10–12 ( 14:3)

### Chapter 15

#### Who May Dwell on Your Holy Mountain?

**v1** O LORD, who may abide in Your tent?Who may dwell on Your holy mountain?

**v2** He who walks with integrityand practices righteousness, who speaks the truth from his heart,
**v3** who has no slander on his tongue, who does no harm to his neighbor, who casts no scorn on his friend,
**v4** who despises the vilebut honors those who fear the LORD, who does not revise a costly oath,
**v5** who lends his money without interestand refuses a bribe against the innocent.He who does these thingswill never be shaken.
### Chapter 16

#### The Presence of the LORD

**v1** Preserve me, O God, for in You I take refuge.

**v2** I said to the LORD, "You are my Lord; apart from You I have no good thing."
**v3** As for the saints in the land, they are the excellencein whom all my delight resides.
**v4** Sorrows will multiplyto those who chase other gods.I will not pour out their libations of blood, or speak their names with my lips.

**v5** The LORD is my chosen portion and my cup; You have made my lot secure.
**v6** The lines of my boundary have fallen in pleasant places; surely my inheritance is delightful.
**v7** I will bless the LORD who counsels me; even at night my conscience instructs me. [^2]

**v8** I have set [^3] the LORD always before me.Because He is at my right hand, I will not be shaken.
**v9** Therefore my heart is glad and my tongue rejoices; my body also will dwell securely. [^4]
**v10** For You will not abandon my soul to Sheol, nor will You let Your Holy One see decay. [^5]
**v11** You have made known to me the path of life; You will fill me with joy in Your presence, [^6] with eternal pleasures at Your right hand.
[^1]: Miktam is probably a musical or liturgical term; used for Psalms 16 and Psalms 56–60. ( 16:0)
[^2]: Or my heart instructs me; Hebrew my kidneys instruct me ( 16:7)
[^3]: LXX I foresaw ( 16:8)
[^4]: LXX will dwell in hope ( 16:9)
[^5]: Cited in Acts 13:35 ( 16:10)
[^6]: Cited in Acts 2:25–28 ( 16:11)

### Chapter 17

#### Hear My Righteous Plea

**v1** Hear, O LORD, my righteous plea; listen to my cry.Give ear to my prayer—it comes from lips free of deceit.
**v2** May my vindication come from Your presence; may Your eyes see what is right.

**v3** You have tried my heart; You have visited me in the night.You have tested me and found no evil; I have resolved not to sin with my mouth.
**v4** As for the deeds of men—by the word of Your lips I have avoided the ways of the violent.
**v5** My steps have held to Your paths; my feet have not slipped.

**v6** I call on You, O God, for You will answer me.Incline Your ear to me; hear my words.
**v7** Show the wonders of Your loving devotion, You who save by Your right handthose who seek refuge from their foes.
**v8** Keep me as the apple of [^1] Your eye; hide me in the shadow of Your wings
**v9** from the wicked who assail me, from my mortal enemies who surround me.

**v10** They have closed their callous hearts; their mouths speak with arrogance.
**v11** They have tracked us down, and now surround us; their eyes are set to cast us to the ground,
**v12** like a lion greedy for prey, like a young lion lurking in ambush.

**v13** Arise, O LORD, confront them!Bring them to their knees; deliver me from the wicked by Your sword,
**v14** from such men, O LORD, by Your hand—from men of the worldwhose portion is in this life.May You fill the bellies of Your treasured ones [^2] and satisfy their sons, so they leave their abundance to their children.

**v15** As for me, I will behold Your face in righteousness; when I awake, I will be satisfied in Your presence.
[^1]: Literally as the pupil, the daughter of ( 17:8)
[^2]: Or May what You have stored up for the wicked fill their bellies ( 17:14)

### Chapter 18

#### The LORD Is My Rock

**v1** I love You, O LORD, my strength.

**v2** The LORD is my rock, my fortress, and my deliverer.My God is my rock, in whom I take refuge, my shield, and the horn of my salvation, my stronghold.
**v3** I will call upon the LORD, who is worthy to be praised; so shall I be saved from my enemies.

**v4** The cords of death encompassed me; the torrents of chaos overwhelmed me.
**v5** The cords of Sheol entangled me; the snares of death confronted me.
**v6** In my distress I called upon the LORD; I cried to my God for help.From His temple He heard my voice, and my cry for His help reached His ears.

**v7** Then the earth shook and quaked, and the foundations of the mountains trembled; they were shaken because He burned with anger.
**v8** Smoke rose from His nostrils, and consuming fire came from His mouth; glowing coals blazed forth.
**v9** He parted the heavens and came downwith dark clouds beneath His feet.
**v10** He mounted a cherub and flew; He soared on the wings of the wind.
**v11** He made darkness His hiding place, and storm clouds a canopy around Him.
**v12** From the brightness of His presence His clouds advanced—hailstones and coals of fire. [^1]

**v13** The LORD thundered from heaven; the voice of the Most High resounded—hailstones and coals of fire. [^2]
**v14** He shot His arrows and scattered the foes; He hurled lightning and routed them.
**v15** The channels of the sea appeared, and the foundations of the world were exposed, at Your rebuke, O LORD, at the blast of the breath of Your nostrils.

**v16** He reached down from on high and took hold of me; He drew me out of deep waters.
**v17** He rescued me from my powerful enemy, from foes too mighty for me.
**v18** They confronted me in my day of calamity, but the LORD was my support.
**v19** He brought me out into the open; He rescued me because He delighted in me.

**v20** The LORD has rewarded me according to my righteousness; He has repaid me according to the cleanness of my hands.
**v21** For I have kept the ways of the LORDand have not wickedly departed from my God.
**v22** For all His ordinances are before me; I have not disregarded His statutes.
**v23** And I have been blameless before Himand kept myself from iniquity.
**v24** So the LORD has repaid me according to my righteousness, according to the cleanness of my hands in His sight.

**v25** To the faithful You show Yourself faithful, to the blameless You show Yourself blameless;
**v26** to the pure You show Yourself pure, but to the crooked You show Yourself shrewd.
**v27** For You save an afflicted people, but You humble those with haughty eyes.

**v28** For You, O LORD, light my lamp; my God lights up my darkness.
**v29** For in You I can charge an army, and with my God I can scale a wall.
**v30** As for God, His way is perfect; the word of the LORD is flawless.He is a shield to all who take refuge in Him.

**v31** For who is God besides the LORD?And who is the Rock except our God?
**v32** It is God who arms me with strengthand makes my way clear.
**v33** He makes my feet like those of a deerand stations me upon the heights.
**v34** He trains my hands for battle; my arms can bend a bow of bronze.

**v35** You have given me Your shield of salvation; Your right hand upholds me, and Your gentleness exalts me. [^3]
**v36** You broaden the path beneath meso that my ankles do not give way.
**v37** I pursued my enemies and overtook them; I did not turn back until they were consumed.
**v38** I crushed them so they could not rise; they have fallen under my feet.

**v39** You have armed me with strength for battle; You have subdued my foes beneath me.
**v40** You have made my enemies retreat before me; I destroyed those who hated me.
**v41** They cried for help, but there was no one to save them—to the LORD, but He did not answer.
**v42** I ground them as dust in the face of the wind; I trampled them [^4] like mud in the streets.

**v43** You have delivered me from the strife of the people; You have made me the head of nations; a people I had not known shall serve me.
**v44** When they hear me, they obey me; foreigners cower before me.
**v45** Foreigners lose heartand come trembling from their strongholds.

**v46** The LORD lives, and blessed be my Rock!And may the God of my salvation be exalted—
**v47** the God who avenges meand subdues nations beneath me,
**v48** who delivers me from my enemies.You exalt me above my foes; You rescue me from violent men.
**v49** Therefore I will praise You, O LORD, among the nations; I will sing praises to Your name. [^5]

**v50** Great salvation He brings to His king.He shows loving devotion to His anointed, to David and his descendants forever.
[^1]: Or bolts of lightning; also in verse 13 ( 18:12)
[^2]: Most Hebrew manuscripts; some Hebrew manuscripts and LXX do not include—hailstones and coals of fire; see 2 Samuel 22:14. ( 18:13)
[^3]: Or and Your help exalts me or and You stoop down to make me great ( 18:35)
[^4]: Some Hebrew manuscripts, LXX, and Syriac (see also 2 Samuel 22:43); MT I poured them out ( 18:42)
[^5]: Cited in Romans 15:9 ( 18:49)

### Chapter 19

#### The Heavens Declare the Glory of God

**v1** The heavens declare the glory of God; the skies proclaim the work of His hands.
**v2** Day after day they pour forth speech; night after night they reveal knowledge.
**v3** Without speech or language, without a sound to be heard, [^1]
**v4** their voice [^2] has gone out into all the earth, their words to the ends of the world. [^3] In the heavens He has pitcheda tent for the sun.
**v5** Like a bridegroom emerging from his chamber, like a champion rejoicing to run his course,
**v6** it rises at one end of the heavensand runs its circuit to the other; nothing is deprived of its warmth.

**v7** The Law of the LORD is perfect, reviving the soul; the testimony of the LORD is trustworthy, making wise the simple.
**v8** The precepts of the LORD are right, bringing joy to the heart; the commandments of the LORD are radiant, giving light to the eyes.
**v9** The fear of the LORD is pure, enduring forever; the judgments of the LORD are true, being altogether righteous.
**v10** They are more precious than gold, than much pure gold; they are sweeter than honey, than honey from the comb.
**v11** By them indeed Your servant is warned; in keeping them is great reward.

**v12** Who can discern his own errors?Cleanse me from my hidden faults.
**v13** Keep Your servant also from willful sins; may they not rule over me.Then I will be blamelessand cleansed of great transgression.
**v14** May the words of my mouthand the meditation of my heartbe pleasing in Your sight, O LORD, my Rock and my Redeemer.
[^1]: Or There is no speech or language where their voice is not heard ( 19:3)
[^2]: LXX, Syriac, and Vulgate; Hebrew their measuring line ( 19:4)
[^3]: Cited in Romans 10:18 ( 19:4)

### Chapter 20

#### The Day of Trouble

**v1** May the LORD answer you in the day of trouble; may the name of the God of Jacob protect you.
**v2** May He send you help from the sanctuaryand sustain you from Zion.
**v3** May He remember all your giftsand look favorably on your burnt offerings.Selah
**v4** May He give you the desires of your heartand make all your plans succeed.
**v5** May we shout for joy at your victoryand raise a banner in the name of our God.May the LORD grant all your petitions.

**v6** Now I know that the LORD saves His anointed; He answers him from His holy heavenwith the saving power of His right hand.
**v7** Some trust in chariots and others in horses, but we trust in the name of the LORD our God.
**v8** They collapse and fall, but we rise up and stand firm.
**v9** O LORD, save [^1] the king.Answer us on the day we call.
[^1]: Or give victory to ( 20:9)

### Chapter 21

#### After the Battle

**v1** O LORD, the king rejoices in Your strength.How greatly he exults in Your salvation!
**v2** You have granted his heart's desireand have not withheld the request of his lips.Selah
**v3** For You welcomed him with rich blessings; You placed on his head a crown of pure gold.
**v4** He asked You for life, and You granted it—length of days, forever and ever.

**v5** Great is his glory in Your salvation; You bestow on him splendor and majesty.
**v6** For You grant him blessings forever; You cheer him with joy in Your presence.
**v7** For the king trusts in the LORD; through the loving devotion of the Most High, he will not be shaken.

**v8** Your hand will apprehend all Your enemies; Your right hand will seize those who hate You.
**v9** You will place them in a fiery furnaceat the time of Your appearing.In His wrath the LORD will engulf them, and the fire will consume them.
**v10** You will wipe their descendants from the earth, and their offspring from the sons of men.

**v11** Though they intend You harm, the schemes they devise will not prevail.
**v12** For You will put them to flightwhen Your bow is trained upon them.

**v13** Be exalted, O LORD, in Your strength; we will sing and praise Your power.
### Chapter 22

#### The Psalm of the Cross

**v1** My God, my God, why have You forsaken me? [^1] Why are You so far from saving me, so far from my words of groaning?
**v2** I cry out by day, O my God, but You do not answer, and by night, but I have no rest.

**v3** Yet You are holy, enthroned on the praises of Israel.
**v4** In You our fathers trusted; they trusted and You delivered them.
**v5** They cried out to You and were set free; they trusted in You and were not disappointed.

**v6** But I am a worm and not a man, scorned by men and despised by the people.
**v7** All who see me mock me; they sneer and shake their heads:
**v8** "He trusts in the LORD, let the LORD deliver him; let the LORD rescue him, since He delights in him."[^2]

**v9** Yet You brought me forth from the womb; You made me secure at my mother's breast.
**v10** From birth I was cast upon You; from my mother's womb You have been my God.
**v11** Be not far from me, for trouble is nearand there is no one to help.

**v12** Many bulls surround me; strong bulls of Bashan encircle me.
**v13** They open their jaws against melike lions that roar and maul.
**v14** I am poured out like water, and all my bones are disjointed.My heart is like wax; it melts away within me.
**v15** My strength [^3] is dried up like a potsherd, and my tongue sticks to the roof of my mouth.You lay me in the dust of death.

**v16** For dogs surround me; a band of evil men encircles me; they have pierced my hands and feet. [^4]
**v17** I can count all my bones; they stare and gloat over me.
**v18** They divide my garments among themand cast lots for my clothing. [^5]

**v19** But You, O LORD, be not far off; O my Strength, come quickly to help me.
**v20** Deliver my soul from the sword, my precious life from the power of wild dogs.
**v21** Save me from the mouth of the lion; at the horns of the wild oxen You have answered me!

**v22** I will proclaim Your name to my brothers; I will praise You in the assembly. [^6]
**v23** You who fear the LORD, praise Him!All descendants of Jacob, honor Him!All offspring of Israel, revere Him!
**v24** For He has not despised or detestedthe torment of the afflicted.He has not hidden His face from him, but has attended to his cry for help.

**v25** My praise for You resounds in the great assembly; I will fulfill my vows before those who fear You.
**v26** The poor will eat and be satisfied; those who seek the LORD will praise Him.May your hearts live forever!

**v27** All the ends of the earthwill remember and turn to the LORD.All the families of the nationswill bow down before Him.
**v28** For dominion belongs to the LORDand He rules over the nations.
**v29** All the rich of the earth will feast and worship; all who go down to the dust will kneel before Him—even those unable to preserve their lives.
**v30** Posterity will serve Him; they will declare the Lord to a new generation.
**v31** They will come and proclaim His righteousnessto a people yet unborn—all that He has done.
[^1]: Cited in Matthew 27:46 and Mark 15:34 ( 22:1)
[^2]: Cited in Matthew 27:43 ( 22:8)
[^3]: MT; or My mouth, a possible reading of the original Hebrew text ( 22:15)
[^4]: DSS, LXX, Vulgate, and Syriac; most MT like a lion at my hands and feet ( 22:16)
[^5]: Cited in John 19:24; see also Matthew 27:35, Mark 15:24, and Luke 23:34 ( 22:18)
[^6]: LXX I will sing Your praises in the assembly; cited in Hebrews 2:12. ( 22:22)

### Chapter 23

#### The LORD Is My Shepherd
**v1** The LORD is my shepherd; [^1] I shall not want.
**v2** He makes me lie down in green pastures; He leads me beside quiet waters.
**v3** He restores my soul; He guides me in the paths of righteousnessfor the sake of His name.
**v4** Even though I walk through the valley of the shadow of death, [^2] I will fear no evil, for You are with me; Your rod and Your staff, they comfort me.

**v5** You prepare a table before mein the presence of my enemies.You anoint my head with oil; my cup overflows.
**v6** Surely goodness and mercy will follow meall the days of my life, and I will dwell in the house of the LORDforever. [^3]
[^1]: See Revelation 7:17. ( 23:1)
[^2]: Or the valley of deep darkness ( 23:4)
[^3]: Literally for a length of days ( 23:6)

### Chapter 24

#### The Earth Is the LORD's

**v1** The earth is the LORD's, and the fullness thereof, [^1] the world and all who dwell therein.
**v2** For He has founded it upon the seasand established it upon the waters.

**v3** Who may ascend the hill of the LORD?Who may stand in His holy place?
**v4** He who has clean hands and a pure heart, who does not lift up his soul to an idol [^2] or swear deceitfully.
**v5** He will receive blessing from the LORDand vindication from the God of his salvation.
**v6** Such is the generation of those who seek Him, who seek Your face, O God of Jacob. [^3] Selah
**v7** Lift up your heads, O gates!Be lifted up, O ancient doors, that the King of Glory may enter!
**v8** Who is this King of Glory?The LORD strong and mighty, the LORD mighty in battle.
**v9** Lift up your heads, O gates!Be lifted up, O ancient doors, that the King of Glory may enter!
**v10** Who is He, this King of Glory?The LORD of Hosts—He is the King of Glory.Selah
[^1]: Cited in 1 Corinthians 10:26 ( 24:1)
[^2]: Or to falsehood or to vanity ( 24:4)
[^3]: LXX, Syriac, and two Hebrew manuscripts; MT who seek your face, O Jacob ( 24:6)

### Chapter 25

#### To You I Lift Up My Soul

**v1** To You, O LORD, I lift up my soul;
**v2** in You, my God, I trust.Do not let me be put to shame; do not let my enemies exult over me.
**v3** Surely none who wait for You will be put to shame; but those who engage in treachery without cause will be disgraced.

**v4** Show me Your ways, O LORD; teach me Your paths.
**v5** Guide me in Your truth and teach me, for You are the God of my salvation; all day long I wait for You.
**v6** Remember, O LORD, Your compassion and loving devotion, for they are from age to age.
**v7** Remember not the sins of my youth, nor my rebellious acts; remember me according to Your loving devotion, because of Your goodness, O LORD.

**v8** Good and upright is the LORD; therefore He shows sinners the way.
**v9** He guides the humble in what is rightand teaches them His way.
**v10** All the LORD's ways are loving and faithfulto those who keep His covenant and His decrees.
**v11** For the sake of Your name, O LORD, forgive my iniquity, for it is great.

**v12** Who is the man who fears the LORD?He will instruct him in the path chosen for him.
**v13** His soul will dwell in prosperity, and his descendants will inherit the land.
**v14** The LORD confides in those who fear Him, and reveals His covenant to them.
**v15** My eyes are always on the LORD, for He will free my feet from the mesh.

**v16** Turn to me and be gracious, for I am lonely and afflicted.
**v17** The troubles of my heart increase; free me from my distress.
**v18** Consider my affliction and trouble, and take away all my sins.
**v19** Consider my enemies, for they are many, and they hate me with vicious hatred.

**v20** Guard my soul and deliver me; let me not be put to shame, for I take refuge in You.
**v21** May integrity and uprightness preserve me, because I wait for You. [^2]

**v22** Redeem Israel, O God, from all its distress.
[^1]: This psalm is an acrostic poem, each verse beginning with the successive letters of the Hebrew alphabet. ( 25:0)
[^2]: Or because my hope is in You; LXX because I wait for You, O Lord ( 25:21)

### Chapter 26

#### Vindicate Me, O LORD

**v1** Vindicate me, O LORD!For I have walked with integrity; I have trusted in the LORD without wavering.
**v2** Test me, O LORD, and try me; examine my heart [^1] and mind.
**v3** For Your loving devotion is before my eyes, and I have walked in Your truth.

**v4** I do not sit with deceitful men, nor keep company with hypocrites.
**v5** I hate the mob of evildoers, and refuse to sit with the wicked.
**v6** I wash my hands in innocencethat I may go about Your altar, O LORD,
**v7** to raise my voice in thanksgivingand declare all Your wonderful works.

**v8** O LORD, I love the house where You dwell, the place where Your glory resides.
**v9** Do not take my soul away with sinners, or my life with men of bloodshed,
**v10** in whose hands are wicked schemes, whose right hands are full of bribes.

**v11** But I will walk with integrity; redeem me and be merciful to me.
**v12** My feet stand on level ground; in the congregations I will bless the LORD.
[^1]: Hebrew my kidneys ( 26:2)

### Chapter 27

#### The LORD Is My Salvation
**v1** The LORD is my light and my salvation—whom shall I fear?The LORD is the stronghold of my life—whom shall I dread?
**v2** When the wicked came upon me to devour my flesh, my enemies and foes stumbled and fell.
**v3** Though an army encamps around me, my heart will not fear; though a war breaks out against me, I will keep my trust.

**v4** One thing I have asked of the LORD; this is what I desire:to dwell in the house of the LORDall the days of my life, to gaze on the beauty of the LORDand seek Him in His temple.
**v5** For in the day of trouble He will hide me in His shelter; He will conceal me under the cover of His tent; He will set me high upon a rock.
**v6** Then my head will be held highabove my enemies around me.At His tabernacle I will offer sacrifices with shouts of joy; I will sing and make music to the LORD.

**v7** Hear, O LORD, my voice when I call; be merciful and answer me.
**v8** My heart said, "Seek His face." Your face, O LORD, I will seek.
**v9** Hide not Your face from me, nor turn away Your servant in anger.You have been my helper; do not leave me or forsake me, O God of my salvation.

**v10** Though my father and mother forsake me, the LORD will receive me.
**v11** Teach me Your way, O LORD, and lead me on a level path, because of my oppressors.
**v12** Do not hand me over to the will of my foes, for false witnesses rise up against me, breathing out violence.

**v13** Still I am certain to seethe goodness of the LORDin the land of the living.
**v14** Wait patiently for the LORD; be strong and courageous.Wait patiently for the LORD!
### Chapter 28

#### The LORD Is My Strength
**v1** To You, O LORD, I call; be not deaf to me, O my Rock.For if You remain silent, I will be like those descending to the Pit.
**v2** Hear my cry for mercywhen I call to You for help, when I lift up my handstoward Your holy sanctuary. [^1]

**v3** Do not drag me away with the wicked, and with the workers of iniquity, who speak peace to their neighborswhile malice is in their hearts.
**v4** Repay them according to their deedsand for their works of evil.Repay them for what their hands have done; bring back on them what they deserve.
**v5** Since they show no regard for the works of the LORDor what His hands have done, He will tear them downand never rebuild them.

**v6** Blessed be the LORD, for He has heard my cry for mercy.
**v7** The LORD is my strength and my shield; my heart trusts in Him, and I am helped.Therefore my heart rejoices, and I give thanks to Him with my song.

**v8** The LORD is the strength of His people, a stronghold of salvation for His anointed.
**v9** Save Your people and bless Your inheritance; shepherd them and carry them forever.
[^1]: Or Your innermost sanctuary or Your Most Holy Place ( 28:2)

### Chapter 29

#### Ascribe Glory to the LORD

**v1** Ascribe to the LORD, O heavenly beings, [^1] ascribe to the LORD glory and strength.
**v2** Ascribe to the LORD the glory due His name; worship the LORD in the splendor of His holiness. [^2]

**v3** The voice of the LORD is over the waters; the God of glory thunders; the LORD is heard over many waters.
**v4** The voice of the LORD is powerful; the voice of the LORD is majestic.
**v5** The voice of the LORD breaks the cedars; the LORD shatters the cedars of Lebanon.
**v6** He makes Lebanon skip like a calf, and Sirion [^3] like a young wild ox.

**v7** The voice of the LORDstrikes with flames of fire.
**v8** The voice of the LORD shakes the wilderness; the LORD shakes the Wilderness of Kadesh.
**v9** The voice of the LORD twists the oaks [^4] and strips the forests bare.And in His temple all cry, "Glory!"

**v10** The LORD sits enthroned over the flood; the LORD is enthroned as King forever.
**v11** The LORD gives His people strength; the LORD blesses His people with peace.
[^1]: Or sons of God or sons of might ( 29:1)
[^2]: Or in holy attire ( 29:2)
[^3]: That is, Mount Hermon ( 29:6)
[^4]: Or LORD makes the deer to calve ( 29:9)

### Chapter 30

#### You Turned My Mourning into Dancing

**v1** I will exalt You, O LORD, for You have lifted me upand have not allowed my foesto rejoice over me.
**v2** O LORD my God, I cried to You for help, and You healed me.
**v3** O LORD, You pulled me up from Sheol; You spared me from descending into the Pit.

**v4** Sing to the LORD, O you His saints, and praise His holy name. [^1]
**v5** For His anger is fleeting, but His favor lasts a lifetime.Weeping may stay the night, but joy comes in the morning.

**v6** In prosperity I said,"I will never be shaken."
**v7** O LORD, You favored me; You made my mountain stand strong.When You hid Your face, I was dismayed.
**v8** To You, O LORD, I called, and I begged my Lord for mercy:
**v9** "What gain is there in my bloodshed, [^2] in my descent to the Pit? [^3] Will the dust praise You?Will it proclaim Your faithfulness?
**v10** Hear me, O LORD, and have mercy; O LORD, be my helper."

**v11** You turned my mourning into dancing; You peeled off my sackcloth and clothed me with joy,
**v12** that my heart may sing Your praises and not be silent.O LORD my God, I will give thanks forever.
[^1]: Or and praise the memorial of His holiness; see Exodus 3:15. ( 30:4)
[^2]: Or in my destruction ( 30:9)
[^3]: Or to corruption ( 30:9)

### Chapter 31

#### Into Your Hands I Commit My Spirit

**v1** In You, O LORD, I have taken refuge; let me never be put to shame; save me by Your righteousness.
**v2** Incline Your ear to me; come quickly to my rescue.Be my rock of refuge, the stronghold of my deliverance.

**v3** For You are my rock and my fortress; lead me and guide me for the sake of Your name.
**v4** You free me from the net laid out for me, for You are my refuge.
**v5** Into Your hands I commit my spirit; [^1] You have redeemed me, O LORD, God of truth.

**v6** I hate [^2] those who cling to worthless idols, but in the LORD I trust.
**v7** I will be glad and rejoice in Your loving devotion, for You have seen my affliction; You have known the anguish of my soul.
**v8** You have not delivered me to the enemy; You have set my feet in the open.

**v9** Be merciful to me, O LORD, for I am in distress; my eyes fail from sorrow, my soul and body as well.
**v10** For my life is consumed with griefand my years with groaning; my iniquity has drained my strength, and my bones are wasting away.
**v11** Among all my enemies I am a disgrace, and among my neighbors even more.I am dreaded by my friends—they flee when they see me on the street.
**v12** I am forgotten like a dead man, out of mind.I am like a broken vessel.
**v13** For I hear the slander of many; there is terror on every side.They conspire against meand plot to take my life.

**v14** But I trust in You, O LORD; I say, "You are my God."
**v15** My times are in Your hands; deliver me from my enemiesand from those who pursue me.
**v16** Make Your face shine on Your servant; save me by Your loving devotion.

**v17** O LORD, let me not be ashamed, for I have called on You.Let the wicked be put to shame; let them lie silent in Sheol.
**v18** May lying lips be silenced—lips that speak with arrogance against the righteous, full of pride and contempt.

**v19** How great is Your goodnesswhich You have laid up for those who fear You, which You have bestowed before the sons of menon those who take refuge in You!
**v20** You hide them in the secret place of Your presencefrom the schemes of men.You conceal them in Your shelterfrom accusing tongues.

**v21** Blessed be the LORD, for He has shown me His loving devotionin a city under siege.
**v22** In my alarm I said,"I am cut off from Your sight!" But You heard my plea for mercywhen I called to You for help.

**v23** Love the LORD, all His saints.The LORD preserves the faithful, but fully repays the arrogant.
**v24** Be strong and courageous, all you who hope in the LORD.
[^1]: Cited in Luke 23:46 ( 31:5)
[^2]: MT; one Hebrew manuscript, LXX, and Syriac You hate ( 31:6)

### Chapter 32

#### The Joy of Forgiveness

**v1** Blessed is he whose transgressions are forgiven, whose sins are covered. [^2]
**v2** Blessed is the manwhose iniquity the LORD does not count against him, [^3] in whose spirit there is no deceit.

**v3** When I kept silent, my bones became brittlefrom my groaning all day long.
**v4** For day and night Your hand was heavy upon me; my strength was drained [^4] as in the summer heat.Selah
**v5** Then I acknowledged my sin to Youand did not hide my iniquity.I said, "I will confess my transgressions to the LORD,"and You forgave the guilt of my sin.Selah
**v6** Therefore let all the godly pray to Youwhile You may be found.Surely when great waters rise, they will not come near.
**v7** You are my hiding place.You protect me from trouble; You surround me with songs of deliverance.Selah
**v8** I will instruct you and teach you the way you should go; I will give you counsel and watch over you.
**v9** Do not be like the horse or mule, which have no understanding; they must be controlled with bit and bridleto make them come to you.
**v10** Many are the sorrows of the wicked, but loving devotion surrounds him who trusts in the LORD.

**v11** Be glad in the LORD and rejoice, O righteous ones; shout for joy, all you upright in heart.
[^1]: Maskil is probably a musical or liturgical term; used for Psalms 32, 42, 44–45, 52–55, 74, 78, 88–89, and 142. ( 32:0)
[^2]: LXX Blessed is he whose lawless acts are forgiven, whose sins are covered; cited in Romans 4:7 ( 32:1)
[^3]: LXX Blessed is the man whose sin the LORD does not count against him; cited in Romans 4:8 ( 32:2)
[^4]: Or my vitality was turned ( 32:4)

### Chapter 33

#### Praise to the Creator
**v1** Rejoice in the LORD, O righteous ones; it is fitting for the upright to praise Him.
**v2** Praise the LORD with the harp; make music to Him with ten strings.
**v3** Sing to Him a new song; play skillfully with a shout of joy.

**v4** For the word of the LORD is upright, and all His work is trustworthy.
**v5** The LORD loves righteousness and justice; the earth is full of His loving devotion.

**v6** By the word of the LORD the heavens were made, and all the stars by the breath of His mouth.
**v7** He piles up the waters of the sea; He puts the depths into storehouses.
**v8** Let all the earth fear the LORD; let all the people of the world revere Him.
**v9** For He spoke, and it came to be; He commanded, and it stood firm.

**v10** The LORD frustrates the plans of the nations; He thwarts the devices of the peoples.
**v11** The counsel of the LORD stands forever, the purposes of His heart to all generations.
**v12** Blessed is the nation whose God is the LORD, the people He has chosen as His inheritance!

**v13** The LORD looks down from heaven; He sees all the sons of men.
**v14** From His dwelling place He gazeson all who inhabit the earth.
**v15** He shapes the hearts of each; He considers all their works.
**v16** No king is saved by his vast army; no warrior is delivered by his great strength.
**v17** A horse is a vain hope for salvation; even its great strength cannot save.

**v18** Surely the eyes of the LORD are on those who fear Him, on those whose hope is in His loving devotion
**v19** to deliver them from deathand keep them alive in famine.

**v20** Our soul waits for the LORD; He is our help and our shield.
**v21** For our hearts rejoice in Him, since we trust in His holy name.
**v22** May Your loving devotion rest on us, O LORD, as we put our hope in You.
### Chapter 34

#### Taste and See That the LORD Is Good

**v1** I will bless the LORD at all times; His praise will always be on my lips.
**v2** My soul boasts in the LORD; let the oppressed hear and rejoice.
**v3** Magnify the LORD with me; let us exalt His name together.

**v4** I sought the LORD, and He answered me; He delivered me from all my fears.
**v5** Those who look to Him are radiant with joy; their faces shall never be ashamed.
**v6** This poor man called out, and the LORD heard him; He saved him from all his troubles.
**v7** The angel of the LORD encamps around those who fear Him, and he delivers them.

**v8** Taste and see that the LORD is good; blessed is the man who takes refuge in Him!
**v9** Fear the LORD, you His saints, for those who fear Him lack nothing.
**v10** Young lions go lacking and hungry, but those who seek the LORD lack no good thing.
**v11** Come, children, listen to me; I will teach you the fear of the LORD.

**v12** Who is the man who delights in life, who desires to see good days?
**v13** Keep your tongue from eviland your lips from deceitful speech.
**v14** Turn away from evil and do good; seek peace and pursue it.
**v15** The eyes of the LORD are on the righteous, and His ears are inclined to their cry. [^3]
**v16** But the face of the LORD is against those who do evil, [^4] to wipe out all memory of them from the earth.

**v17** The righteous cry out, and the LORD hears; He delivers them from all their troubles.
**v18** The LORD is near to the brokenhearted; He saves the contrite in spirit.

**v19** Many are the afflictions of the righteous, but the LORD delivers him from them all.
**v20** He protects all his bones; not one of them will be broken. [^5]

**v21** Evil will slay the wicked, and the haters of the righteous will be condemned.
**v22** The LORD redeems His servants, and none who take refuge in Him will be condemned.
[^1]: Abimelech is another name for Achish; see 1 Samuel 21–29 and 1 Kings 2:39. ( 34:0)
[^2]: This psalm is an acrostic poem, each verse beginning with the successive letters of the Hebrew alphabet. ( 34:0)
[^3]: LXX to their prayer ( 34:15)
[^4]: Cited in 1 Peter 3:10–12 ( 34:16)
[^5]: Cited in John 19:36 ( 34:20)

### Chapter 35

#### Contend with My Opponents, O LORD

**v1** Contend with my opponents, O LORD; fight against those who fight against me.
**v2** Take up Your shield and buckler; arise and come to my aid.
**v3** Draw the spear and javelin [^1] against my pursuers; say to my soul: "I am your salvation."

**v4** May those who seek my lifebe disgraced and put to shame; may those who plan to harm mebe driven back and confounded.
**v5** May they be like chaff in the wind, as the angel of the LORD drives them away.
**v6** May their path be dark and slick, as the angel of the LORD pursues.
**v7** For without cause they laid their net for me; without reason they dug a pit for my soul.
**v8** May ruin befall them by surprise; may the net they hid ensnare them; may they fall into the hazard they created.

**v9** Then my soul will rejoice in the LORDand exult in His salvation.
**v10** All my bones will exclaim,"Who is like You, O LORD, who delivers the afflicted from the aggressor, the poor and needy from the robber?"

**v11** Hostile witnesses come forward; they make charges I know nothing about.
**v12** They repay me evil for good, to the bereavement of my soul.
**v13** Yet when they were ill, I put on sackcloth; I humbled myself with fasting, but my prayers returned unanswered. [^2]
**v14** I paced aboutas for my friend or brother; I was bowed down with grief, like one mourning for his mother.
**v15** But when I stumbled, they assembled in glee; they gathered together against me.Assailants I did not knowslandered me without ceasing.
**v16** Like godless jesters at a feast, [^3] they gnashed their teeth at me.

**v17** How long, O Lord, will You look on?Rescue my soul from their ravages, my precious life from these lions.
**v18** Then I will give You thanks in the great assembly; I will praise You among many people.
**v19** Let not my enemies gloat over me without cause, nor those who hate me without reason wink in malice. [^4]
**v20** For they do not speak peace, but they devise deceitful schemesagainst those who live quietly in the land.
**v21** They gape at me and say,"Aha, aha! Our eyes have seen!"

**v22** O LORD, You have seen it; be not silent.O Lord, be not far from me.
**v23** Awake and rise to my defense, to my cause, my God and my Lord!
**v24** Vindicate me by Your righteousness, O LORD my God, and do not let them gloat over me.
**v25** Let them not say in their hearts,"Aha, just what we wanted!" Let them not say,"We have swallowed him up!"

**v26** May those who gloat in my distressbe ashamed and confounded; may those who exalt themselves over mebe clothed in shame and reproach.
**v27** May those who favor my vindicationshout for joy and gladness; may they always say, "Exalted be the LORDwho delights in His servant's well-being."

**v28** Then my tongue will proclaim Your righteousnessand Your praises all day long.
[^1]: Or and close the way ( 35:3)
[^2]: Literally returned to my bosom ( 35:13)
[^3]: Or Like a godless circle of mockers, ( 35:16)
[^4]: See John 15:25. ( 35:19)

### Chapter 36

#### The Transgression of the Wicked

**v1** An oracle is in my heartregarding the transgression of the wicked man:There is no fear of Godbefore his eyes. [^1]
**v2** For his eyes are too full of conceitto detect or hate his own sin.
**v3** The words of his mouth are wicked and deceitful; he has ceased to be wise and well-doing.
**v4** Even on his bed he plots wickedness; he sets himself on a path that is not good; he fails to reject evil.

**v5** Your loving devotion, O LORD, reaches to the heavens, Your faithfulness to the clouds.
**v6** Your righteousness is like the highest mountains; Your judgments are like the deepest sea.O LORD, You preserve man and beast.
**v7** How precious is Your loving devotion, O God, that the children of men take refugein the shadow of Your wings!
**v8** They feast on the abundance of Your house, and You give them drink from Your river of delights.
**v9** For with You is the fountain of life; in Your light we see light.

**v10** Extend Your loving devotion to those who know You, and Your righteousness to the upright in heart.
**v11** Let not the foot of the proud come against me, nor the hand of the wicked drive me away.
**v12** There the evildoers lie fallen, thrown down and unable to rise.
[^1]: Cited in Romans 3:18 ( 36:1)

### Chapter 37

#### Delight Yourself in the LORD
**v1** Do not fret over those who do evil; do not envy those who do wrong.
**v2** For they wither quickly like grassand wilt like tender plants.

**v3** Trust in the LORD and do good; dwell in the land and cultivate faithfulness.
**v4** Delight yourself in the LORD, and He will give you the desires of your heart.

**v5** Commit your way to the LORD; trust in Him, and He will do it.
**v6** He will bring forth your righteousness like the dawn, your justice like the noonday sun.

**v7** Be still before the LORDand wait patiently for Him; do not fret when men prosper in their ways, when they carry out wicked schemes.

**v8** Refrain from anger and abandon wrath; do not fret—it can only bring harm.
**v9** For the evildoers will be cut off, but those who hope in the LORD will inherit the land.

**v10** Yet a little while, and the wicked will be no more; though you look for them, they will not be found.
**v11** But the meek will inherit the land [^2] and delight in abundant prosperity.

**v12** The wicked scheme against the righteousand gnash their teeth at them,
**v13** but the Lord laughs, seeing that their day is coming.

**v14** The wicked have drawn the swordand bent the bowto bring down the poor and needy, to slay those whose ways are upright.
**v15** But their swords will pierce their own hearts, and their bows will be broken.

**v16** Better is the little of the righteousthan the abundance of many who are wicked.
**v17** For the arms of the wicked will be broken, but the LORD upholds the righteous.

**v18** The LORD knows the days of the blameless, and their inheritance will last forever.
**v19** In the time of evil they will not be ashamed, and in the days of famine they will be satisfied.

**v20** But the wicked and enemies of the LORDwill perish like the glory of the fields.They will vanish; like smoke they will fade away.

**v21** The wicked borrow and do not repay, but the righteous are gracious and giving.
**v22** Surely those He blesses will inherit the land, but the cursed will be destroyed.

**v23** The steps of a man are ordered by the LORDwho takes delight in his journey.
**v24** Though he falls, he will not be overwhelmed, for the LORD is holding his hand. [^3]

**v25** I once was young and now am old, yet never have I seen the righteous abandonedor their children begging for bread.
**v26** They are ever generous and quick to lend, and their children are a blessing.

**v27** Turn away from evil and do good, so that you will abide forever.
**v28** For the LORD loves justiceand will not forsake His saints.They are preserved forever, but the offspring of the wicked will be cut off.
**v29** The righteous will inherit the landand dwell in it forever.
