**v30** The mouth of the righteous man utters wisdom, and his tongue speaks justice.
**v31** The law of his God is in his heart; his steps do not falter.

**v32** Though the wicked lie in wait for the righteous, and seek to slay them,
**v33** the LORD will not leave them in their poweror let them be condemned under judgment.

**v34** Wait for the LORD and keep His way, and He will raise you up to inherit the land.When the wicked are cut off, you will see it.

**v35** I have seen a wicked, ruthless manflourishing like a well-rooted native tree,
**v36** yet he passed away and was no more; though I searched, he could not be found.

**v37** Consider the blameless and observe the upright, for posterity awaits the man of peace. [^4]
**v38** But the transgressors will all be destroyed; the future of the wicked will be cut off.

**v39** The salvation of the righteous is from the LORD; He is their stronghold in time of trouble.
**v40** The LORD helps and delivers them; He rescues and saves them from the wicked, because they take refuge in Him.
[^1]: This psalm is an acrostic poem, each stanza beginning with the successive letters of the Hebrew alphabet. ( 37:0)
[^2]: Or the earth; see Matthew 5:5. ( 37:11)
[^3]: Or upholds him with His hand ( 37:24)
[^4]: Or for there is a future for the man of peace ( 37:37)

### Chapter 38

#### Do Not Rebuke Me in Your Anger

**v1** O LORD, do not rebuke me in Your angeror discipline me in Your wrath.
**v2** For Your arrows have pierced me deeply, and Your hand has pressed down on me.

**v3** There is no soundness in my bodybecause of Your anger; there is no rest in my bonesbecause of my sin.
**v4** For my iniquities have overwhelmed me; they are a burden too heavy to bear.
**v5** My wounds are foul and festeringbecause of my sinful folly.
**v6** I am bent and brought low; all day long I go about mourning.
**v7** For my loins are full of burning pain, and no soundness remains in my body.
**v8** I am numb and badly crushed; I groan in anguish of heart.

**v9** O Lord, my every desire is before You; my groaning is not hidden from You.
**v10** My heart pounds, my strength fails, and even the light of my eyes has faded.
**v11** My beloved and friends shun my disease, and my kinsmen stand at a distance.
**v12** Those who seek my life lay snares; those who wish me harm speak destruction, plotting deceit all day long.

**v13** But like a deaf man, I do not hear; and like a mute man, I do not open my mouth.
**v14** I am like a man who cannot hear, whose mouth offers no reply.
**v15** I wait for You, O LORD; You will answer, O Lord my God.
**v16** For I said, "Let them not gloat over me—those who taunt me when my foot slips."

**v17** For I am ready to fall, and my pain is ever with me.
**v18** Yes, I confess my iniquity; I am troubled by my sin.
**v19** Many are my enemies without cause, [^1] and many hate me without reason. [^2]
**v20** Those who repay my good with evilattack me for pursuing the good.

**v21** Do not forsake me, O LORD; be not far from me, O my God.
**v22** Come quickly to help me, O Lord my Savior.
[^1]: One DSS manuscript; MT My enemies are vigorous and strong ( 38:19)
[^2]: See John 15:25 ( 38:19)

### Chapter 39

#### I Will Watch My Ways

**v1** I said, "I will watch my waysso that I will not sin with my tongue; I will guard my mouth with a muzzleas long as the wicked are present."
**v2** I was speechless and still; I remained silent, even from speaking good, and my sorrow was stirred.
**v3** My heart grew hot within me; as I mused, the fire burned.Then I spoke with my tongue:

**v4** "Show me, O LORD, my endand the measure of my days.Let me know how fleeting my life is.
**v5** You, indeed, have made my days as handbreadths, and my lifetime as nothing before You.Truly each man at his bestexists as but a breath.Selah
**v6** Surely every man goes about like a phantom; surely he bustles in vain; he heaps up richesnot knowing who will haul them away.

**v7** And now, O Lord, for what do I wait?My hope is in You.
**v8** Deliver me from all my transgressions; do not make me the reproach of fools.
**v9** I have become mute; I do not open my mouthbecause of what You have done.
**v10** Remove Your scourge from me; I am perishing by the force of Your hand.
**v11** You discipline and correct a man for his iniquity, consuming like a moth what he holds dear; surely each man is but a vapor.Selah
**v12** Hear my prayer, O LORD, and give ear to my cry for help; do not be deaf to my weeping.For I am a foreigner dwelling with You, a stranger like all my fathers.
**v13** Turn Your gaze away from me, that I may again be cheeredbefore I depart and am no more."
### Chapter 40

#### I Waited Patiently for the LORD

**v1** I waited patiently for the LORD; He inclined to me and heard my cry.
**v2** He lifted me up from the pit of despair, out of the miry clay; He set my feet upon a rock, and made my footsteps firm.
**v3** He put a new song in my mouth, a hymn of praise to our God.Many will see and fearand put their trust in the LORD.

**v4** Blessed is the manwho has made the LORD his trust, who has not turned to the proud, nor to those who lapse into falsehood. [^1]
**v5** Many, O LORD my God, are the wonders You have done, and the plans You have for us—none can compare to You—if I proclaim and declare them, they are more than I can count.

**v6** Sacrifice and offering You did not desire, but my ears You have opened. [^2] Burnt offerings and sin offerings You did not require.
**v7** Then I said, "Here I am, I have come—it is written about me in the scroll:
**v8** I delight to do Your will, O my God; [^3] Your law is within my heart."

**v9** I proclaim righteousness in the great assembly; behold, I do not seal my lips, as You, O LORD, do know.
**v10** I have not covered up Your righteousness in my heart; I have declared Your faithfulness and salvation; I have not concealed Your loving devotion and faithfulnessfrom the great assembly.

**v11** O LORD, do not withhold Your mercy from me; Your loving devotion and faithfulness will always guard me.
**v12** For evils without number surround me; my sins have overtaken me, so that I cannot see.They are more than the hairs of my head, and my heart has failed within me.
**v13** Be pleased, O LORD, to deliver me; hurry, O LORD, to help me.

**v14** May those who seek my lifebe ashamed and confounded; may those who wish me harmbe repelled and humiliated.
**v15** May those who say to me, "Aha, aha!"be appalled at their own shame.
**v16** May all who seek Yourejoice and be glad in You; may those who love Your salvationalways say, "The LORD be magnified!"

**v17** But I am poor and needy; may the Lord think of me.You are my helper and deliverer; O my God, do not delay.
[^1]: Or who turn aside to false gods or who run after lies ( 40:4)
[^2]: Hebrew; some LXX manuscripts but a body You prepared for me ( 40:6)
[^3]: Cited in Hebrews 10:5–7 ( 40:8)

### Chapter 41

#### Victory over Betrayal

**v1** Blessed is the one who cares for the poor; the LORD will deliver him in the day of trouble.
**v2** The LORD will protect and preserve him; He will bless him in the landand refuse to give him overto the will of his foes.
**v3** The LORD will sustain him on his bed of illnessand restore him from his bed of sickness.

**v4** I said, "O LORD, be gracious to me; heal me, for I have sinned against You."
**v5** My enemies say with malice: "When will he die and be forgotten?"
**v6** My visitor speaks falsehood; he gathers slander in his heart; he goes out and spreads it abroad.
**v7** All who hate me whisper against me; they imagine the worst for me:
**v8** "A vile disease has been poured into him; he will never get up from where he lies!"
**v9** Even my close friend whom I trusted, the one who shared my bread, has lifted up his heel against me. [^1]

**v10** But You, O LORD, be gracious to me and raise me up, that I may repay them.
**v11** By this I know that You delight in me, for my enemy does not triumph over me.
**v12** In my integrity You uphold meand set me in Your presence forever.

**v13** Blessed be the LORD, the God of Israel, from everlasting to everlasting.Amen and Amen.
[^1]: Cited in John 13:18 ( 41:9)

### Chapter 42

#### As the Deer Pants for the Water


**v1** As the deer pants for streams of water, so my soul longs after You, O God.
**v2** My soul thirsts for God, the living God.When shall I come and appear in God's presence? [^2]
**v3** My tears have been my foodboth day and night, while men ask me all day long,"Where is your God?"
**v4** These things come to mind as I pour out my soul:how I walked with the multitude, leading the festive procession to the house of Godwith shouts of joy and praise.

**v5** Why are you downcast, O my soul?Why the unease within me?Put your hope in God, for I will yet praise Himfor the salvation of His presence.

**v6** O my God, my soul despairs within me.Therefore I remember Youfrom the land of Jordan and the peaks of Hermon—even from Mount Mizar.
**v7** Deep calls to deepin the roar of Your waterfalls; all Your breakers and waveshave rolled over me.
**v8** The LORD decrees His loving devotion by day, and at night His song is with meas a prayer to the God of my life.

**v9** I say to God my Rock,"Why have You forgotten me?Why must I walk in sorrowbecause of the enemy's oppression?"
**v10** Like the crushing of my bones, my enemies taunt me, while they say to me all day long,"Where is your God?"

**v11** Why are you downcast, O my soul?Why the unease within me?Put your hope in God, for I will yet praise Him, my Savior and my God.
[^1]: In many Hebrew manuscripts Psalms 42 and 43 constitute one psalm. Maskil is probably a musical or liturgical term; used for Psalms 32, 42, 44–45, 52–55, 74, 78, 88–89, and 142. ( 42:0)
[^2]: Or and see the face of God? ( 42:2)

### Chapter 43

#### Send Out Your Light
**v1** Vindicate me, O God, and plead my caseagainst an ungodly nation; deliver me from deceitful and unjust men.
**v2** For You are the God of my refuge.Why have You rejected me?Why must I walk in sorrowbecause of the enemy's oppression?

**v3** Send out Your light and Your truth; let them lead me.Let them bring me to Your holy mountainand to the place where You dwell.
**v4** Then I will go to the altar of God, to God, my greatest joy.I will praise You with the harp, O God, my God.

**v5** Why are you downcast, O my soul?Why the unease within me?Put your hope in God, for I will yet praise Him, my Savior and my God.
### Chapter 44

#### Redeem Us, O God

**v1** We have heard with our ears, O God; our fathers have told usthe work You did in their days, in the days of old.
**v2** With Your hand You drove out the nationsand planted our fathers there; You crushed the peoplesand cast them out.
**v3** For it was not by their sword that they took the land; their arm did not bring them victory.It was by Your right hand, Your arm, and the light of Your face, because You favored them.

**v4** You are my King, O God, who ordains victories for Jacob.
**v5** Through You we repel our foes; through Your name we trample our enemies.
**v6** For I do not trust in my bow, nor does my sword save me. [^2]
**v7** For You save us from our enemies; You put those who hate us to shame.
**v8** In God we have boasted all day long, and Your name we will praise forever.Selah
**v9** But You have rejected and humbled us; You no longer go forth with our armies.
**v10** You have made us retreat from the foe, and those who hate us have plundered us.
**v11** You have given us up as sheep to be devoured; You have scattered us among the nations.
**v12** You sell Your people for nothing; no profit do You gain from their sale.

**v13** You have made us a reproach to our neighbors, a mockery and derision to those around us.
**v14** You have made us a byword among the nations, a laughingstock [^3] among the peoples.
**v15** All day long my disgrace is before me, and shame has covered my face,
**v16** at the voice of the scorner and reviler, because of the enemy, bent on revenge.

**v17** All this has come upon us, though we have not forgotten Youor betrayed Your covenant.
**v18** Our hearts have not turned back; our steps have not strayed from Your path.
**v19** But You have crushed us in the lair of jackals; [^4] You have covered us with deepest darkness.

**v20** If we had forgotten the name of our Godor spread out our hands to a foreign god,
**v21** would not God have discovered, since He knows the secrets of the heart?
**v22** Yet for Your sake we face death all day long; we are considered as sheep to be slaughtered. [^5]

**v23** Wake up, O Lord! Why are You sleeping?Arise! Do not reject us forever.
**v24** Why do You hide Your faceand forget our affliction and oppression?
**v25** For our soul has sunk to the dust; our bodies cling to the earth.
**v26** Rise up; be our help!Redeem us on account of Your loving devotion.
[^1]: Maskil is probably a musical or liturgical term; used for Psalms 32, 42, 44–45, 52–55, 74, 78, 88–89, and 142. ( 44:0)
[^2]: Or give me victory; similarly in verse 7 ( 44:6)
[^3]: Literally a shaking of the head ( 44:14)
[^4]: Or serpents or dragons ( 44:19)
[^5]: Cited in Romans 8:36 ( 44:22)

### Chapter 45

#### My Heart Is Stirred by a Noble Theme

**v1** My heart is stirred by a noble themeas I recite my verses to the king; [^2] my tongue is the pen of a skillful writer.
**v2** You are the most handsome of men; grace has anointed your lips; therefore God has blessed you forever.
**v3** Strap your sword at your side, O mighty warrior; appear in your majesty and splendor.
**v4** In your splendor ride forth in victoryon behalf of truth and humility and justice; may your right hand show your awesome deeds.
**v5** Your arrows pierce the hearts of the king's foes; the nations fall beneath your feet.

**v6** Your throne, O God, endures forever and ever, and justice is the scepter of Your kingdom.
**v7** You have loved righteousnessand hated wickedness; therefore God, your God, has anointed youabove your companions with the oil of joy. [^3]

**v8** All your garments are fragrantwith myrrh and aloes and cassia; from palaces of ivory the harps make you glad.
**v9** The daughters of kings are among your honored women; the queen stands at your right hand, adorned with the gold of Ophir.

**v10** Listen, O daughter! Consider and incline your ear:Forget your people and your father's house,
**v11** and the king will desire your beauty; bow to him, for he is your lord.
**v12** The Daughter of Tyre will come with a gift; men of wealth will seek your favor.

**v13** All glorious is the princess in her chamber; her gown is embroidered with gold.
**v14** In colorful garments she is led to the king; her virgin companions are brought before you.
**v15** They are led in with joy and gladness; they enter the palace of the king.

**v16** Your sons will succeed your fathers; you will make them princes throughout the land.
**v17** I will commemorate your name through all generations; therefore the nations will praise you forever and ever.
[^1]: Maskil is probably a musical or liturgical term; used for Psalms 32, 42, 44–45, 52–55, 74, 78, 88–89, and 142. ( 45:0)
[^2]: Or King; here and throughout Psalm 45 ( 45:1)
[^3]: Cited in Hebrews 1:8–9 ( 45:7)

### Chapter 46

#### God Is Our Refuge and Strength

**v1** God is our refuge and strength, an ever-present help in times of trouble.
**v2** Therefore we will not fear, though the earth is transformedand the mountains are toppledinto the depths of the seas,
**v3** though their waters roar and foamand the mountains quake in the surge.Selah
**v4** There is a river whose streams delight the city of God, the holy place where the Most High dwells.
**v5** God is within her; she will not be moved.God will help her when morning dawns.
**v6** Nations rage, kingdoms crumble; the earth melts when He lifts His voice.
**v7** The LORD of Hosts is with us; the God of Jacob is our fortress.Selah
**v8** Come, see the works of the LORD, who brings devastation upon the earth.
**v9** He makes wars to cease throughout the earth; He breaks the bow and shatters the spear; He burns the shields [^2] in the fire.

**v10** "Be still and know that I am God; I will be exalted among the nations, I will be exalted over the earth."

**v11** The LORD of Hosts is with us; the God of Jacob is our fortress.Selah
[^1]: Alamoth is probably a musical or liturgical term; here and in 1 Chronicles 15:20. ( 46:0)
[^2]: Or chariots ( 46:9)

### Chapter 47

#### Clap Your Hands, All You Peoples

**v1** Clap your hands, all you peoples; shout unto God with a voice of triumph.

**v2** How awesome is the LORD Most High, the great King over all the earth!
**v3** He subdues nations beneath us, and peoples under our feet.
**v4** He chooses our inheritance for us, the pride of Jacob, whom He loves.Selah
**v5** God has ascended amid shouts of joy, the LORD with the sound of the horn.
**v6** Sing praises to God, sing praises; sing praises to our King, sing praises!
**v7** For God is King of all the earth; sing to Him a psalm of praise. [^1]

**v8** God reigns over the nations; God is seated on His holy throne.
**v9** The nobles of the nations have assembledas the people of the God of Abraham; for the shields of the earth belong to God; He is highly exalted.
[^1]: Or sing a Maskil of praise or sing praises with understanding ( 47:7)

### Chapter 48

#### Broken Bondage

**v1** Great is the LORD, and greatly to be praisedin the city of our God, His holy mountain.
**v2** Beautiful in loftiness, the joy of all the earth, like the peaks of Zaphon [^1] is Mount Zion, the city of the great King.
**v3** God is in her citadels; He has shown Himself to be a fortress.

**v4** For behold, the kings assembled; they all advanced together.
**v5** They saw and were astounded; they fled in terror.
**v6** Trembling seized them there, anguish like a woman in labor.
**v7** With a wind from the east You wrecked the ships of Tarshish. [^2]

**v8** As we have heard, so we have seenin the city of the LORD of Hosts, in the city of our God:God will establish her forever.Selah
**v9** Within Your temple, O God, we contemplate Your loving devotion.
**v10** Your name, O God, like Your praise, reaches to the ends of the earth; Your right hand is full of righteousness.
**v11** Mount Zion is glad, the daughters [^3] of Judah rejoice, on account of Your judgments.

**v12** March around Zion, encircle her, count her towers,
**v13** consider her ramparts, tour her citadels, that you may tell the next generation.
**v14** For this God is our God forever and ever; He will be our guide even till death. [^4]
[^1]: Or in the far north; the most sacred mountain of the Canaanites was Zaphon ( 48:2)
[^2]: Or a fleet of trading ships ( 48:7)
[^3]: Or the villages ( 48:11)
[^4]: Or He will guide us beyond death ( 48:14)

### Chapter 49

#### The Evanescence of Wealth

**v1** Hear this, all you peoples; listen, all inhabitants of the world,
**v2** both low and high, rich and poor alike.
**v3** My mouth will impart wisdom, and the meditation of my heart will bring understanding.
**v4** I will incline my ear to a proverb; I will express my riddle with the harp:

**v5** Why should I fear in times of trouble, when wicked usurpers surround me?
**v6** They trust in their wealthand boast in their great riches.
**v7** No man can possibly redeem his brother [^1] or pay his ransom to God.
**v8** For the redemption of his soul is costly, and never can payment suffice,
**v9** that he should live on foreverand not see decay.

**v10** For it is clear that wise men die, and the foolish and the senseless both perishand leave their wealth to others.
**v11** Their graves [^2] are their eternal homes—their dwellings for endless generations—even though their lands were their namesakes.
**v12** But a man, despite his wealth, cannot endure; he is like the beasts that perish.

**v13** This is the fate of the foolish [^3] and their followers who endorse their sayings.Selah
**v14** Like sheep they are destined for Sheol.Death will be their shepherd.The upright will rule them in the morning, and their form will decay in Sheol, far from their lofty abode.
**v15** But God will redeem my life from Sheol, for He will surely take me to Himself.Selah
**v16** Do not be afraid when a man grows rich, when the splendor of his house increases.
**v17** For when he dies, he will carry nothing away; his abundance will not follow him down.
**v18** Though in his lifetime he blesses his soul—and men praise you when you prosper—
**v19** he will join the generation of his fathers, who will never see the light of day.
**v20** A man who has riches without understandingis like the beasts that perish.
[^1]: Or redeem another ( 49:7)
[^2]: LXX, Syriac, and Aramaic Targum; Hebrew Their inward thoughts ( 49:11)
[^3]: Or the way of the foolish ( 49:13)

### Chapter 50

#### The Mighty One Calls

**v1** The Mighty One, God the LORD, speaks and summons the earthfrom where the sun rises to where it sets.
**v2** From Zion, perfect in beauty, God shines forth.
**v3** Our God approaches and will not be silent!Consuming fire precedes Him, and a tempest rages around Him.
**v4** He summons the heavens above, and the earth, that He may judge His people:
**v5** "Gather to Me My saints, who made a covenant with Me by sacrifice."
**v6** And the heavens proclaim His righteousness, for God Himself is Judge. [^1] Selah
**v7** "Hear, O My people, and I will speak, O Israel, and I will testify against you:I am God, your God.
**v8** I do not rebuke you for your sacrifices, and your burnt offerings are ever before Me.
**v9** I have no need for a bull from your stallor goats from your pens,
**v10** for every beast of the forest is Mine—the cattle on a thousand hills.
**v11** I know every bird in the mountains, and the creatures of the field are Mine.
**v12** If I were hungry, I would not tell you, for the world is Mine, and the fullness thereof.
**v13** Do I eat the flesh of bulls, or drink the blood of goats?
**v14** Sacrifice a thank offering to God, and fulfill your vows to the Most High.
**v15** Call upon Me in the day of trouble; I will deliver you, and you will honor Me."

**v16** To the wicked, however, God says,"What right have you to recite My statutesand to bear My covenant on your lips?
**v17** For you hate My instructionand cast My words behind you.
**v18** When you see a thief, you befriend him, and throw in your lot with adulterers.
**v19** You unleash your mouth for eviland harness your tongue to deceit.
**v20** You sit and malign your brother; you slander your own mother's son.
**v21** You have done these things, and I kept silent; you thought I was [^2] just like you.But now I rebuke you and accuse you to your face. [^3]

**v22** Now consider this, you who forget God, lest I tear you to pieces, with no one to rescue you:
**v23** He who sacrifices a thank offering honors Me, and to him who rightly orders his way, I will show the salvation of God."
[^1]: Or He is a God of justice ( 50:6)
[^2]: Or you thought the 'I AM' was ( 50:21)
[^3]: Literally and I set it in order before your eyes ( 50:21)

### Chapter 51

#### Create in Me a Clean Heart, O God

**v1** Have mercy on me, [^1] O God, according to Your loving devotion; according to Your great compassion, blot out my transgressions.
**v2** Wash me clean of my iniquityand cleanse me from my sin.
**v3** For I know my transgressions, and my sin is always before me.
**v4** Against You, You only, have I sinnedand done what is evil in Your sight, so that You may be proved right when You speakand blameless when You judge. [^2]
**v5** Surely I was brought forth in iniquity; I was sinful when my mother conceived me.

**v6** Surely You desire truth in the inmost being; You teach me wisdom in the inmost place.
**v7** Purify me with hyssop, and I will be clean; wash me, and I will be whiter than snow.
**v8** Let me hear joy and gladness; let the bones You have crushed rejoice.
**v9** Hide Your face from my sinsand blot out all my iniquities.

**v10** Create in me a clean heart, O God, and renew a right spirit within me.
**v11** Cast me not away from Your presence; take not Your Holy Spirit from me.
**v12** Restore to me the joy of Your salvation, and sustain me with a willing spirit.
**v13** Then I will teach transgressors Your ways, and sinners will return to You.

**v14** Deliver me from bloodguilt, O God, the God of my salvation, and my tongue will sing of Your righteousness.
**v15** O Lord, open my lips, and my mouth will declare Your praise.
**v16** For You do not delight in sacrifice, or I would bring it; You take no pleasure in burnt offerings.
**v17** The sacrifices of God are a broken spirit; a broken and a contrite heart, O God, You will not despise.

**v18** In Your good pleasure, cause Zion to prosper; build up the walls of Jerusalem.
**v19** Then You will delight in righteous sacrifices, in whole burnt offerings; then bulls will be offered on Your altar.
[^1]: Or Be gracious to me ( 51:1)
[^2]: LXX and victorious when You judge; cited in Romans 3:4 ( 51:4)

### Chapter 52

#### Why Do You Boast of Evil?

**v1** Why do you boast of evil, O mighty man?The loving devotion of God endures all day long.
**v2** Your tongue devises destructionlike a sharpened razor, O worker of deceit.
**v3** You love evil more than good, falsehood more than speaking truth.Selah
**v4** You love every word that devours, O deceitful tongue.
**v5** Surely God will bring you down to everlasting ruin; He will snatch you up and tear you away from your tent; He will uproot you from the land of the living.Selah
**v6** The righteous will see and fear; they will mock the evildoer, saying,
**v7** "Look at the manwho did not make God his refuge, but trusted in the abundance of his wealthand strengthened himself by destruction."

**v8** But I am like an olive treeflourishing in the house of God; I trust in the loving devotion of Godforever and ever.
**v9** I will praise You forever, because You have done it.I will wait on Your name—for it is good—in the presence of Your saints.
[^1]: Maskil is probably a musical or liturgical term; used for Psalms 32, 42, 44–45, 52–55, 74, 78, 88–89, and 142. ( 52:0)

### Chapter 53

#### The Fool Says There Is No God

**v1** The fool says in his heart,"There is no God." They are corrupt; their ways are vile.There is no one who does good.

**v2** God looks down from heavenupon the sons of mento see if any understand, if any seek God.
**v3** All have turned away, they have together become corrupt; [^3] there is no one who does good, not even one. [^4]

**v4** Will the workers of iniquity never learn?They devour my people like bread; they refuse to call upon God.
**v5** There they are, overwhelmed with dread, where there was nothing to fear.For God has scattered the bonesof those who besieged you.You put them to shame, for God has despised them.

**v6** Oh, that the salvation of Israel would come from Zion!When God restores His captive people, [^5] let Jacob rejoice, let Israel be glad!
[^1]: Mahalath is probably a musical or liturgical term; see also Psalms 88:1. ( 53:0)
[^2]: Maskil is probably a musical or liturgical term; used for Psalms 32, 42, 44–45, 52–55, 74, 78, 88–89, and 142. ( 53:0)
[^3]: LXX worthless ( 53:3)
[^4]: Cited in Romans 3:10–12 ( 53:3)
[^5]: Or the fortunes of His people ( 53:6)

### Chapter 54

#### Save Me by Your Name

**v1** Save me, O God, by Your name, and vindicate me by Your might!
**v2** Hear my prayer, O God; listen to the words of my mouth.
**v3** For strangers rise up against me, and ruthless men seek my life—men with no regard for God.Selah
**v4** Surely God is my helper; the Lord is the sustainer of my soul.
**v5** He will reward my enemies with evil.In Your faithfulness, destroy them.
**v6** Freely I will sacrifice to You; I will praise Your name, O LORD, for it is good.
**v7** For He has delivered me from every trouble, and my eyes have looked in triumph on my foes.
[^1]: Maskil is probably a musical or liturgical term; used for Psalms 32, 42, 44–45, 52–55, 74, 78, 88–89, and 142. ( 54:0)

### Chapter 55

#### Cast Your Burden upon the LORD

**v1** Listen to my prayer, O God, and do not ignore my plea.
**v2** Attend to me and answer me.I am restless in my complaint, and distraught
**v3** at the voice of the enemy, at the pressure of the wicked.For they bring down disaster upon meand resent me in their anger.

**v4** My heart pounds within me, and the terrors of death assail me.
**v5** Fear and trembling grip me, and horror has overwhelmed me.
**v6** I said, "Oh, that I had wings like a dove!I would fly away and find rest.
**v7** How far away I would flee!In the wilderness I would remain.Selah
**v8** I would hurry to my shelter, far from this raging tempest."

**v9** O Lord, confuse and confound their speech, for I see violence and strife in the city.
**v10** Day and night they encircle the walls, while malice and trouble lie within.
**v11** Destruction is within; oppression and deceit never leave the streets.

**v12** For it is not an enemy who insults me; that I could endure.It is not a foe who rises against me; from him I could hide.
**v13** But it is you, a man like myself, my companion and close friend.
**v14** We shared sweet fellowship together; we walked with the crowd into the house of God.

**v15** Let death seize them by surprise; let them go down to Sheol alive, for evil is with them in their homes.
**v16** But I call to God, and the LORD saves me.
**v17** Morning, noon, and night, I cry out in distress, and He hears my voice.
**v18** He redeems my soul in peacefrom the battle waged against me, even though many oppose me.
**v19** God will hear and humiliate them—the One enthroned for the ages—Selahbecause they do not changeand they have no fear of God.

**v20** My companion attacks his friends; he violates his covenant.
**v21** His speech is smooth as butter, but war is in his heart.His words are softer than oil, yet they are swords unsheathed.

**v22** Cast your burden upon the LORDand He will sustain you; He will never let the righteous be shaken.
**v23** But You, O God, will bring them downto the Pit of destruction; men of bloodshed and deceitwill not live out half their days.But I will trust in You.
[^1]: Maskil is probably a musical or liturgical term; used for Psalms 32, 42, 44–45, 52–55, 74, 78, 88–89, and 142. ( 55:0)

### Chapter 56

#### Be Merciful to Me, O God

**v1** Be merciful to me, O God, for men are hounding me; all day they press their attack.
**v2** My enemies pursue me all day long, for many proudly assail me.

**v3** When I am afraid, I put my trust in You.
**v4** In God, whose word I praise—in God I trust.I will not be afraid.What can man do to me?

**v5** All day long they twist my words; all their thoughts are on my demise.
**v6** They conspire, they lurk, they watch my stepswhile they wait to take my life.
**v7** In spite of such sin, will they escape? [^2] In Your anger, O God, cast down the nations.

**v8** You have taken account of my wanderings. [^3] Put my tears in Your bottle—are they not in Your book?
**v9** Then my enemies will retreaton the day I cry for help.By this I will know that God is on my side.

**v10** In God, whose word I praise, in the LORD, whose word I praise,
**v11** in God I trust; I will not be afraid.What can man do to me?

**v12** Your vows are upon me, O God; I will render thank offerings to You.
**v13** For You have delivered my soul from death, and my feet from stumbling, that I may walk before Godin the light of life.
[^1]: Miktam is probably a musical or liturgical term; used for Psalms 16 and 56–60. ( 56:0)
[^2]: Or do not let them escape; MT does not include do not. ( 56:7)
[^3]: Or sorrows ( 56:8)

### Chapter 57

#### In You My Soul Takes Refuge

**v1** Have mercy on me, O God, have mercy, for in You my soul takes refuge.In the shadow of Your wings I will take shelteruntil the danger has passed.
**v2** I cry out to God Most High, [^2] to God who fulfills His purpose for me.
**v3** He reaches down from heaven and saves me; He rebukes those who trample me.Selah God sends forth His loving devotion and His truth.
**v4** My soul is among the lions; I lie down with ravenous beasts—with men whose teeth are spears and arrows, whose tongues are sharp swords.

**v5** Be exalted, O God, above the heavens; may Your glory cover all the earth.

**v6** They spread a net for my feet; my soul was despondent.They dug a pit before me, but they themselves have fallen into it!Selah
**v7** My heart is steadfast, O God, my heart is steadfast.I will sing and make music.
**v8** Awake, my glory! [^3] Awake, O harp and lyre!I will awaken the dawn.

**v9** I will praise You, O Lord, among the nations; I will sing Your praises among the peoples.
**v10** For Your loving devotion reaches to the heavens, and Your faithfulness to the clouds.
**v11** Be exalted, O God, above the heavens; may Your glory cover all the earth.
[^1]: Miktam is probably a musical or liturgical term; used for Psalms 16 and 56–60. ( 57:0)
[^2]: Hebrew Elohim-Elyon ( 57:2)
[^3]: Or Awake, my soul! ( 57:8)

### Chapter 58

#### God Judges the Earth

**v1** Do you indeed speak justly, O rulers?Do you judge uprightly, O sons of men?
**v2** No, in your hearts you devise injustice; with your hands you mete out violence on the earth.

**v3** The wicked are estranged from the womb; the liars go astray from birth.
**v4** Their venom is like the venom of a snake, like a cobra that shuts its ears,
**v5** refusing to hear the tune of the charmerwho skillfully weaves his spell.

**v6** O God, shatter their teeth in their mouths; O LORD, tear out the fangs of the lions.
**v7** May they vanishlike water that runs off; when they draw the bow, may their arrows be blunted. [^2]
**v8** Like a slug that dissolves in its slime, like a woman's stillborn child, may they never see the sun.

**v9** Before your pots can feel the burning thorns—whether green or dry—He will sweep them away.
**v10** The righteous will rejoicewhen they see they are avenged; they will wash their feetin the blood of the wicked.
**v11** Then men will say,"There is surely a reward for the righteous!There is surely a God who judges the earth!"
[^1]: Miktam is probably a musical or liturgical term; used for Psalms 16 and 56–60. ( 58:0)
[^2]: Or when they are trodden down, may they wither like grass ( 58:7)

### Chapter 59

#### Deliver Me from My Enemies

**v1** Deliver me from my enemies, O my God; protect me from those who rise against me.
**v2** Deliver me from workers of iniquity, and save me from men of bloodshed.
**v3** See how they lie in wait for me.Fierce men conspire against mefor no transgression or sin of my own, O LORD.
**v4** For no fault of my own, they move swiftly to attack me.Arise to help me, and take notice.
**v5** O LORD God of Hosts, the God of Israel, rouse Yourself to punish all the nations; show no mercy to the wicked traitors.Selah
**v6** They return in the evening, snarling like dogsand prowling around the city.
**v7** See what they spew from their mouths—sharp words from their lips: "For who can hear us?"
**v8** But You, O LORD, laugh at them; You scoff at all the nations.

**v9** I will keep watch for You, O my strength, because You, O God, are my fortress.
**v10** My God of loving devotion will come to meet me; God will let me stare down my foes.

**v11** Do not kill them, or my people will forget.Scatter them by Your power, and bring them down, O Lord, our shield.
**v12** By the sins of their mouthsand the words of their lips, let them be trapped in their pride, in the curses and lies they utter.
**v13** Consume them in wrath; consume them till they are no more, so it may be known to the ends of the earththat God rules over Jacob.Selah
**v14** They return in the evening, snarling like dogsand prowling around the city.
**v15** They scavenge for food, and growl if they are not satisfied.

**v16** But I will sing of Your strengthand proclaim Your loving devotion in the morning.For You are my fortress, my refuge in times of trouble.
**v17** To You, O my strength, I sing praises, for You, O God, are my fortress, my God of loving devotion.
[^1]: Miktam is probably a musical or liturgical term; used for Psalms 16 and 56–60. ( 59:0)

### Chapter 60

#### Victory with God

**v1** You have rejected us, O God; You have broken us; You have been angry; restore us!
**v2** You have shaken the landand torn it open.Heal its fractures, for it is quaking.
**v3** You have shown Your people hardship; we are staggered from the wine You made us drink.

**v4** You have raised a banner for those who fear You, that they may flee the bow. [^4] Selah
**v5** Respond and save us with Your right hand, that Your beloved may be delivered.

**v6** God has spoken from His sanctuary: [^5]"I will triumph!I will parcel out Shechemand apportion the Valley of Succoth.
**v7** Gilead is Mine, and Manasseh is Mine; Ephraim is My helmet, Judah is My scepter.
**v8** Moab is My washbasin; upon Edom I toss My sandal; over Philistia I shout in triumph."

**v9** Who will bring me to the fortified city?Who will lead me to Edom?
**v10** Have You not rejected us, O God?Will You no longer march out, O God, with our armies?
**v11** Give us aid against the enemy, for the help of man is worthless.
**v12** With God we will perform with valor, and He will trample our enemies.
[^1]: Miktam is probably a musical or liturgical term; used for Psalms 16 and 56–60. ( 60:0)
[^2]: That is, Mesopotamia; Aram-naharaim means Aram of the two rivers, likely the region between the Euphrates and Balih Rivers in northwestern Mesopotamia. ( 60:0)
[^3]: That is, the land northeast of Damascus ( 60:0)
[^4]: Or that it may be displayed because of truth ( 60:4)
[^5]: Or in His holiness ( 60:6)

### Chapter 61

#### You Have Heard My Vows

**v1** Hear my cry, O God; attend to my prayer.
**v2** From the ends of the earth I call out to Youwhenever my heart is faint.Lead me to the rockthat is higher than I.
**v3** For You have been my refuge, a tower of strength against the enemy.
**v4** Let me dwell in Your tent foreverand take refuge in the shelter of Your wings.Selah
**v5** For You have heard my vows, O God; You have given me the inheritancereserved for those who fear Your name.

**v6** Increase the days of the king's life; may his years span many generations.
**v7** May he sit enthroned in God's presence forever; appoint Your loving devotionand Your faithfulness to guard him.
**v8** Then I will ever sing praise to Your nameand fulfill my vows day by day.
### Chapter 62

#### Waiting on God

**v1** In God alone my soul finds rest; my salvation comes from Him.
**v2** He alone is my rock and my salvation.He is my fortress; I will never be shaken.

**v3** How long will you threaten a man?Will all of you throw him downlike a leaning wallor a tottering fence?
**v4** They fully intend to cast him down from his lofty perch; they delight in lies; with their mouths they bless, but inwardly they curse.Selah
**v5** Rest in God alone, O my soul, for my hope comes from Him.
**v6** He alone is my rock and my salvation; He is my fortress; I will not be shaken.
**v7** My salvation and my honor rest on God, my strong rock; my refuge is in God.
**v8** Trust in Him at all times, O people; pour out your hearts before Him.God is our refuge.Selah
**v9** Lowborn men are but a vapor; the exalted are but a lie.Weighed on the scale, they go up; together they are but a vapor.
**v10** Place no trust in extortionor false hope in stolen goods.If your riches increase, do not set your heart upon them.

**v11** God has spoken once; I have heard this twice:that power belongs to God,
**v12** and loving devotion to You, O Lord.For You will repay each manaccording to his deeds. [^1]
[^1]: Cited in Romans 2:6 ( 62:12)

### Chapter 63

#### Thirsting for God

**v1** O God, You are my God.Earnestly I seek You; my soul thirsts for You.My body yearns for Youin a dry and weary land without water.

**v2** So I have seen You in the sanctuaryand beheld Your power and glory.
**v3** Because Your loving devotion is better than life, my lips will glorify You.
**v4** So I will bless You as long as I live; in Your name I will lift my hands.

**v5** My soul is satisfied as with the richest of foods; with joyful lips my mouth will praise You.
**v6** When I remember You on my bed, I think of You through the watches of the night.
**v7** For You are my help; I will sing for joy in the shadow of Your wings.
**v8** My soul clings to You; Your right hand upholds me.

**v9** But those who seek my life to destroy itwill go into the depths of the earth.
**v10** They will fall to the power of the sword; they will become a portion for foxes.
**v11** But the king will rejoice in God; all who swear by Him will exult, for the mouths of liars will be shut.
### Chapter 64

#### The Hurtful Tongue

**v1** Hear, O God, my voice of complaint; preserve my life from dread of the enemy.
**v2** Hide me from the scheming of the wicked, from the mob of workers of iniquity,
**v3** who sharpen their tongues like swordsand aim their bitter words like arrows,
**v4** ambushing the innocent in seclusion, shooting suddenly, without fear.

**v5** They hold fast to their evil purpose; they speak of hiding their snares." Who will see them?" they say.
**v6** They devise injustice and say,"We have perfected a secret plan." For the inner man and the heart are mysterious.

**v7** But God will shoot them with arrows; suddenly they will be wounded.
**v8** They will be made to stumble, their own tongues turned against them.All who see will shake their heads.
**v9** Then all mankind will fearand proclaim the work of God; so they will ponder what He has done.

**v10** Let the righteous rejoice in the LORDand take refuge in Him; let all the upright in heart exult.
### Chapter 65

#### Praise Awaits God in Zion

**v1** Praise awaits You, O God, in Zion; to You our vows will be fulfilled.
**v2** O You who listen to prayer, all people will come to You.
**v3** When iniquities prevail against me, You atone for our transgressions.
**v4** Blessed is the one You chooseand bring near to dwell in Your courts!We are filled with the goodness of Your house, the holiness of Your temple.

**v5** With awesome deeds of righteousness You answer us, O God of our salvation, the hope of all the ends of the earthand of the farthest seas.
**v6** You formed the mountains by Your power, having girded Yourself with might.
**v7** You stilled the roaring of the seas, the pounding of their waves, and the tumult of the nations.
**v8** Those who live far away fear Your wonders; You make the dawn and sunset shout for joy. [^1]

**v9** You attend to the earth and water it; [^2] with abundance You enrich it.The streams of God are full of water, for You prepare our grainby providing for the earth. [^3]
**v10** You soak its furrows and level its ridges; You soften it with showers and bless its growth.
**v11** You crown the year with Your bounty, and Your paths overflow with plenty.
**v12** The pastures of the wilderness overflow; the hills are robed with joy.
**v13** The pastures are clothed with flocks, and the valleys are decked with grain.They shout in triumph; indeed, they sing.
[^1]: Or where morning dawns and evening fades You call forth songs of joy. ( 65:8)
[^2]: Or and make it overflow ( 65:9)
[^3]: Or to provide the people with grain, for so You have ordained it ( 65:9)

### Chapter 66

#### Make a Joyful Noise

**v1** Make a joyful noise to God, all the earth!
**v2** Sing the glory of His name; make His praise glorious.
**v3** Say to God, "How awesome are Your deeds!So great is Your powerthat Your enemies cower before You.
**v4** All the earth bows down to You; they sing praise to You; they sing praise to Your name." Selah
**v5** Come and see the works of God; how awesome are His deeds toward mankind.
**v6** He turned the sea into dry land; they passed through the waters on foot; there we rejoiced in Him.
**v7** He rules forever by His power; His eyes watch the nations.Do not let the rebellious exalt themselves.Selah
**v8** Bless our God, O peoples; let the sound of His praise be heard.
**v9** He preserves our livesand keeps our feet from slipping.

**v10** For You, O God, have tested us; You have refined us like silver.
**v11** You led us into the net; You laid burdens on our backs.
**v12** You let men ride over our heads; we went through fire and water, but You brought us into abundance.

**v13** I will enter Your house with burnt offerings; I will fulfill my vows to You—
**v14** the vows that my lips promisedand my mouth spoke in my distress.
**v15** I will offer You fatlings as burnt offerings, with the fragrant smoke of rams; I will offer bulls and goats.Selah
**v16** Come and listen, all you who fear God, and I will declare what He has done for me.
**v17** I cried out to Him with my mouthand praised Him with my tongue. [^1]
**v18** If I had cherished iniquity in my heart, the Lord would not have listened.
**v19** But God has surely heard; He has attended to the sound of my prayer.

**v20** Blessed be God, who has not rejected my prayeror withheld from me His loving devotion!
[^1]: Or and His praise was on my tongue ( 66:17)

### Chapter 67

#### May God Cause His Face to Shine upon Us

**v1** May God be gracious to us and bless us, and cause His face to shine upon us, Selah
**v2** that Your ways may be known on earth, Your salvation among all nations.

**v3** Let the peoples praise You, O God; let all the peoples praise You.
**v4** Let the nations be glad and sing for joy, for You judge the peoples justlyand lead the nations of the earth.Selah
**v5** Let the peoples praise You, O God; let all the peoples praise You.

**v6** The earth has yielded its harvest; God, our God, blesses us.
**v7** God blesses us, that all the ends of the earth shall fear Him.
### Chapter 68

#### God's Enemies Are Scattered

**v1** God arises. His enemies are scattered, and those who hate Him flee His presence.
**v2** As smoke is blown away, You will drive them out; as wax melts before the fire, the wicked will perish in the presence of God.
**v3** But the righteous will be gladand rejoice before God; they will celebrate with joy.

**v4** Sing to God!Sing praises to His name.Exalt Him who rides on the clouds [^1]—His name is the LORD—and rejoice before Him.
**v5** A father of the fatherlessand a defender of widowsis God in His holy habitation.
**v6** God settles the lonely in families; He leads the prisoners out to prosperity, but the rebellious dwell in a sun-scorched land.

**v7** O God, when You went out before Your people, when You marched through the wasteland, Selah
**v8** the earth shook and the heavens poured down rainbefore God, the One on Sinai, before God, the God of Israel.
**v9** You sent abundant rain, O God; You refreshed Your weary inheritance.
**v10** Your flock settled therein; O God, from Your bounty You provided for the poor.

**v11** The Lord gives the command; a great company of women proclaim it:
**v12** "Kings and their armies flee in haste; she who waits at home divides the plunder.
**v13** Though you lie down among the sheepfolds, the wings of the dove are covered with silver, and her feathers with shimmering gold."
**v14** When the Almighty [^2] scattered the kings in the land, it was like the snow falling on Zalmon.

**v15** A mountain of God is Mount Bashan; a mountain of many peaks is Mount Bashan.
**v16** Why do you gaze in envy, O mountains of many peaks?This is the mountain God chose for His dwelling, where the LORD will surely dwell forever.

**v17** The chariots of God are tens of thousands—thousands of thousands are they; the Lord is in His sanctuaryas He was at Sinai. [^3]
**v18** You have ascended on high; You have led captives away.You have received gifts from men, [^4] even from the rebellious, that the LORD God may dwell there.
**v19** Blessed be the Lord, who daily bears our burden, the God of our salvation.Selah
**v20** Our God is a God of deliverance; the Lord GOD is our rescuer from death.
**v21** Surely God will crush the heads of His enemies, the hairy crowns of those who persist in guilty ways.
**v22** The Lord said, "I will retrieve them from Bashan, I will bring them up from the depths of the sea,
**v23** that your foot may be dippedin the blood of your foes—the tongues of your dogs in the same."

**v24** They have seen Your procession, O God—the march of my God and King into the sanctuary.
**v25** The singers lead the way, the musicians follow after, among the maidens playing tambourines.
**v26** Bless God in the great congregation; bless the LORD from the fountain of Israel.
**v27** There is Benjamin, the youngest, ruling them, the princes of Judah in their company, the princes of Zebulun and of Naphtali.

**v28** Summon Your power, O God; [^5] show Your strength, O God, which You have exerted on our behalf.
**v29** Because of Your temple at Jerusalemkings will bring You gifts.
**v30** Rebuke the beast in the reeds, the herd of bulls among the calves of the nations, until it submits, bringing bars of silver.Scatter the nations who delight in war.
**v31** Envoys will arrive from Egypt; Cush [^6] will stretch out her hands to God.

**v32** Sing to God, O kingdoms of the earth; sing praises to the Lord—Selah
**v33** to Him who rides upon the highest heavens of old; behold, His mighty voice resounds.
**v34** Ascribe the power to God, whose majesty is over Israel, whose strength is in the skies.
**v35** O God, You are awesome in Your sanctuary; the God of Israel Himselfgives strength and power to His people.Blessed be God!
[^1]: Or rides through the deserts ( 68:4)
[^2]: Hebrew Shaddai ( 68:14)
[^3]: Or the Lord has come from Sinai in His holiness ( 68:17)
[^4]: Cited in Ephesians 4:8 ( 68:18)
[^5]: LXX and Syriac; most Hebrew manuscripts Your God has summoned your power ( 68:28)
[^6]: That is, the upper Nile region ( 68:31)

### Chapter 69

#### The Waters Are up to My Neck

**v1** Save me, O God, for the waters are up to my neck.
**v2** I have sunk into the miry depths, where there is no footing; I have drifted into deep waters, where the flood engulfs me.
**v3** I am weary from my crying; my throat is parched.My eyes fail, looking for my God.
**v4** Those who hate me without causeoutnumber the hairs of my head; many are those who would destroy me—my enemies for no reason. [^1] Though I did not steal, I must repay.

**v5** You know my folly, O God, and my guilt is not hidden from You.
**v6** May those who hope in You not be ashamed through me, O Lord GOD of Hosts; may those who seek You not be dishonored through me, O God of Israel.
**v7** For I have endured scorn for Your sake, and shame has covered my face.
**v8** I have become a stranger to my brothersand a foreigner to my mother's sons,
**v9** because zeal for Your house has consumed me, [^2] and the insults of those who insult You have fallen on me. [^3]
**v10** I wept and fasted, but it brought me reproach.
**v11** I made sackcloth my clothing, and I was sport to them.
**v12** Those who sit at the gate mock me, and I am the song of drunkards.

**v13** But my prayer to You, O LORD, is for a time of favor.In Your abundant loving devotion, O God, answer me with Your sure salvation.
**v14** Rescue me from the mireand do not let me sink; deliver me from my foesand out of the deep waters.
**v15** Do not let the floods engulf meor the depths swallow me up; let not the Pit close its mouth over me.
**v16** Answer me, O LORD, for Your loving devotion is good; turn to me in keeping with Your great compassion.
**v17** Hide not Your face from Your servant, for I am in distress.Answer me quickly!
**v18** Draw near to my soul and redeem me; ransom me because of my foes.

**v19** You know my reproach, my shame and disgrace.All my adversaries are before You.
**v20** Insults have broken my heart, and I am in despair.I looked for sympathy, but there was none, for comforters, but I found no one.
**v21** They poisoned my food with galland gave me vinegar to quench my thirst.

**v22** May their table become a snare; may it be a retribution and a trap. [^4]
**v23** May their eyes be darkened so they cannot see, and their backs be bent forever. [^5]
**v24** Pour out Your wrath upon them, and let Your burning anger overtake them.
**v25** May their place be deserted; let there be no one to dwell in their tents. [^6]
**v26** For they persecute the one You struckand recount the pain of those You wounded.
**v27** Add iniquity to their iniquity; let them not share in Your righteousness.
**v28** May they be blotted out of the Book of Lifeand not listed with the righteous.

**v29** But I am in pain and distress; let Your salvation protect me, O God.
**v30** I will praise God's name in songand exalt Him with thanksgiving.
**v31** And this will please the LORD more than an ox, more than a bull with horns and hooves.
**v32** The humble will see and rejoice.You who seek God, let your hearts be revived!
**v33** For the LORD listens to the needyand does not despise His captive people.

**v34** Let heaven and earth praise Him, the seas and everything that moves in them.
**v35** For God will save Zionand rebuild the cities of Judah, that they may dwell there and possess it.
**v36** The descendants of His servants will inherit it, and those who love His name will settle in it.
[^1]: See John 15:25 ( 69:4)
[^2]: Cited in John 2:17 ( 69:9)
[^3]: Cited in Romans 15:3 ( 69:9)
[^4]: A slight revocalization of the Hebrew (see also LXX, Syriac, and Vulgate); literally may their prosperity be a trap; cited in Romans 11:9 ( 69:22)
[^5]: LXX; Hebrew and may their loins tremble continually; cited in Romans 11:10 ( 69:23)
[^6]: Cited in Acts 1:20 ( 69:25)

### Chapter 70

#### Hurry, O LORD, to Help Me!
**v1** Make haste, O God, to deliver me!Hurry, O LORD, to help me!

**v2** May those who seek my lifebe ashamed and confounded; may those who wish me harmbe repelled and humiliated.
**v3** May those who say, "Aha, aha!"retreat because of their shame.

**v4** May all who seek Yourejoice and be glad in You; may those who love Your salvation always say,"Let God be magnified!"
**v5** But I am poor and needy; hurry to me, O God.You are my help and my deliverer; O LORD, do not delay.
### Chapter 71

#### Be My Rock of Refuge
**v1** In You, O LORD, I have taken refuge; let me never be put to shame.
**v2** In Your justice, rescue and deliver me; incline Your ear and save me.
**v3** Be my rock of refuge, where I can always go.Give the command to save me, for You are my rock and my fortress.
**v4** Deliver me, O my God, from the hand of the wicked, from the grasp of the unjust and ruthless.

**v5** For You are my hope, O Lord GOD, my confidence from my youth.
**v6** I have leaned on You since birth; You pulled me from my mother's womb.My praise is always for You.
**v7** I have become a portent to many, but You are my strong refuge.
**v8** My mouth is filled with Your praiseand with Your splendor all day long.

**v9** Do not discard me in my old age; do not forsake me when my strength fails.
**v10** For my enemies speak against me, and those who lie in wait for my life conspire,
**v11** saying, "God has forsaken him; pursue him and seize him, for there is no one to rescue him."

**v12** Be not far from me, O God.Hurry, O my God, to help me.
**v13** May the accusers of my soulbe ashamed and consumed; may those who seek my harmbe covered with scorn and disgrace.

**v14** But I will always hopeand will praise You more and more.
**v15** My mouth will declare Your righteousnessand Your salvation all day long, though I cannot know their full measure.
**v16** I will come in the strength of the Lord GOD; I will proclaim Your righteousness—Yours alone.

**v17** O God, You have taught me from my youth, and to this day I proclaim Your marvelous deeds.
**v18** Even when I am old and gray, do not forsake me, O God, until I proclaim Your power to the next generation, Your might to all who are to come.
**v19** Your righteousness reaches to the heavens, O God, You who have done great things.Who, O God, is like You?

**v20** Though You have shown me many troubles and misfortunes, You will revive me once again.Even from the depths of the earth You will bring me back up.
**v21** You will increase my honorand comfort me once again.

**v22** So I will praise You with the harpfor Your faithfulness, O my God; I will sing praise to You with the lyre, O Holy One of Israel.
**v23** When I sing praise to Youmy lips will shout for joy, along with my soul, which You have redeemed.
**v24** My tongue will indeed proclaim Your righteousness all day long, for those who seek my harmare disgraced and confounded.
### Chapter 72

#### Endow the King with Your Justice

**v1** Endow the king with Your justice, O God, and the son of the king with Your righteousness.
**v2** May he judge Your people with righteousnessand Your afflicted with justice.

**v3** May the mountains bring peace to the people, and the hills bring righteousness.
**v4** May he vindicate the afflicted among the people; may he save the children of the needyand crush the oppressor.
**v5** May they fear him [^1] as long as the sun shines, as long as the moon remains, through all generations.
**v6** May he be like rain that falls on freshly cut grass, like spring showers that water the earth.
**v7** May the righteous flourish in his daysand prosperity abounduntil the moon is no more.

**v8** May he rule from sea to sea, and from the Euphrates [^2] to the ends of the earth.
**v9** May the nomads bow before him, and his enemies lick the dust.
**v10** May the kings of Tarshish and distant shores bring tribute; may the kings of Sheba and Seba offer gifts.
**v11** May all kings bow down to himand all nations serve him.

**v12** For he will deliver the needy who cry outand the afflicted who have no helper.
**v13** He will take pity on the poor and needyand save the lives of the oppressed.
**v14** He will redeem them from oppression and violence, for their blood is precious in his sight.

**v15** Long may he live!May gold from Sheba be given him.May people ever pray for him; may they bless him all day long.
**v16** May there be an abundance of grain in the land; may it sway atop the hills.May its fruit trees flourish like the forests of Lebanon, the people of its cities like the grass of the field.
**v17** May his name endure forever; may his name continue [^3] as long as the sun shines.In him may all nations be blessed; may they call him blessed.

**v18** Blessed be the LORD God, the God of Israel, who alone does marvelous deeds.
**v19** And blessed be His glorious name forever; may all the earth be filled with His glory.Amen and amen.

**v20** Thus conclude the prayers of David son of Jesse.
[^1]: LXX He shall endure ( 72:5)
[^2]: Hebrew the River ( 72:8)
[^3]: Or increase ( 72:17)

### Chapter 73

#### Surely God Is Good to Israel


**v1** Surely God is good to Israel, to those who are pure in heart.
**v2** But as for me, my feet had almost stumbled; my steps had nearly slipped.
**v3** For I envied the arrogantwhen I saw the prosperity of the wicked.

**v4** They have no struggle in their death; their bodies are well-fed.
**v5** They are free of the burdens others carry; they are not afflicted like other men.
**v6** Therefore pride is their necklace; a garment of violence covers them.
**v7** From their prosperity proceeds iniquity; [^1] the imaginations of their hearts run wild.
**v8** They mock and speak with malice; with arrogance they threaten oppression.
**v9** They set their mouths against the heavens, and their tongues strut across the earth.

**v10** So their people [^2] return to this placeand drink up waters in abundance.
**v11** The wicked say, "How can God know?Does the Most High have knowledge?"
**v12** Behold, these are the wicked—always carefree as they increase their wealth.

**v13** Surely in vain I have kept my heart pure; in innocence I have washed my hands.
**v14** For I am afflicted all day longand punished every morning.
**v15** If I had said, "I will speak this way,"then I would have betrayed Your children.
**v16** When I tried to understand all this, it was troublesome in my sight
**v17** until I entered God's sanctuary; then I discerned their end.

**v18** Surely You set them on slick ground; You cast them down into ruin.
**v19** How suddenly they are laid waste, completely swept away by terrors!
**v20** Like one waking from a dream, so You, O Lord, awaken and despise their form.

**v21** When my heart was grievedand I was pierced within,
**v22** I was senseless and ignorant; I was a brute beast before You.

**v23** Yet I am always with You; You hold my right hand.
**v24** You guide me with Your counsel, and later receive me in glory.
**v25** Whom have I in heaven but You?And on earth I desire no one besides You.
**v26** My flesh and my heart may fail, but God is the strength [^3] of my heartand my portion forever.

**v27** Those far from You will surely perish; You destroy all who are unfaithful to You.
**v28** But as for me, it is good to draw near to God.I have made the Lord GOD my refuge, that I may proclaim all Your works.
[^1]: Literally Their eye bulges with fatness; Syriac From their callous heart proceeds iniquity ( 73:7)
[^2]: Or His people ( 73:10)
[^3]: Hebrew rock ( 73:26)

### Chapter 74

#### Why Have You Rejected Us Forever?

**v1** Why have You rejected us forever, O God?Why does Your anger smolderagainst the sheep of Your pasture?
**v2** Remember Your congregation, which You purchased long agoand redeemed as the tribe of Your inheritance—Mount Zion, where You dwell.
**v3** Turn Your steps to the everlasting ruins, to everything in the sanctuary the enemy has destroyed.

**v4** Your foes have roared within Your meeting place; they have unfurled their banners as signs,
**v5** like men wielding axes in a thicket of trees
**v6** and smashing all the carvings with hatchets and picks.
**v7** They have burned Your sanctuary to the ground; they have defiled the dwelling place of Your Name.

**v8** They said in their hearts,"We will crush them completely." They burned down every placewhere God met us in the land.
**v9** There are no signs for us to see.There is no longer any prophet.And none of us knows how long this will last.
**v10** How long, O God, will the enemy taunt You?Will the foe revile Your name forever?
**v11** Why do You withdraw Your strong right hand?Stretch it out to destroy them! [^2]

**v12** Yet God is my King from ancient times, working salvation on the earth.
**v13** You divided the sea by Your strength; You smashed the heads of the dragons of the sea;
**v14** You crushed the heads of Leviathan; You fed him to the creatures of the desert.
**v15** You broke open the fountain and the flood; You dried up the ever-flowing rivers.
**v16** The day is Yours, and also the night; You established the moon [^3] and the sun.
**v17** You set all the boundaries of the earth; You made the summer and winter.

**v18** Remember how the enemy has mocked You, O LORD, how a foolish people has spurned Your name.
**v19** Do not deliver the soul of Your dove to beasts; do not forget the lives of Your afflicted forever.
**v20** Consider Your covenant, for haunts of violence fill the dark places of the land.
**v21** Do not let the oppressed retreat in shame; may the poor and needy praise Your name.

**v22** Rise up, O God; defend Your cause!Remember how the fool mocks You all day long.
**v23** Do not disregard the clamor of Your adversaries, the uproar of Your enemies that ascends continually.
[^1]: Maskil is probably a musical or liturgical term; used for Psalms 32, 42, 44–45, 52–55, 74, 78, 88–89, and 142. ( 74:0)
[^2]: Literally From the midst of Your bosom destroy them! or From the midst of Your bosom remove it! ( 74:11)
[^3]: Literally the light ( 74:16)

### Chapter 75

#### God's Righteous Judgment

**v1** We give thanks to You, O God; we give thanks, for Your Name is near.The people declare Your wondrous works.

**v2** "When I choose a time, I will judge fairly.
**v3** When the earth and all its dwellers quake, it is I who bear up its pillars.Selah
**v4** I say to the proud, 'Do not boast,'and to the wicked, 'Do not lift up your horn.
**v5** Do not lift up your horn against heavenor speak with an outstretched neck.'"

**v6** For exaltation comes neither from east nor west, nor out of the desert,
**v7** but it is God who judges; He brings down one and exalts another.
**v8** For a cup is in the hand of the LORD, full of foaming wine mixed with spices.He pours from His cup, and all the wicked of the earthdrink it down to the dregs.

**v9** But I will proclaim Him [^1] forever; I will sing praise to the God of Jacob.

**v10** "All the horns of the wicked I will cut off, but the horns of the righteous will be exalted."
[^1]: Or proclaim it ( 75:9)

### Chapter 76

#### God's Name Is Great in Israel

**v1** God is known in Judah; His name is great in Israel.
**v2** His tent is in Salem, [^1] His dwelling place in Zion.
**v3** There He shattered the flaming arrows, the shield and sword and weapons of war.Selah
**v4** You are resplendent with light, more majestic than mountains filled with game.
**v5** The valiant lie plundered; they sleep their last sleep.No men of might could lift a hand.
**v6** At Your rebuke, O God of Jacob, both horse and rider lie stunned.

**v7** You alone are to be feared.When You are angry, who can stand before You?
**v8** From heaven You pronounced judgment, and the earth feared and was still
**v9** when God rose up to judge, to save all the lowly of the earth.Selah
**v10** Even the wrath of man shall praise You; with the survivors of wrath You will clothe Yourself. [^2]

**v11** Make and fulfill your vows to the LORD your God; let all the neighboring lands bring tributeto Him who is to be feared.
**v12** He breaks the spirits of princes; He is feared by the kings of the earth.
[^1]: That is, Jerusalem ( 76:2)
[^2]: Or Surely Your wrath against men brings You praise, and the survivors of Your wrath will be restrained. ( 76:10)

### Chapter 77

#### In the Day of Trouble I Sought the Lord

**v1** I cried out to God; I cried aloud to God to hear me.
**v2** In the day of trouble I sought the Lord; through the night my outstretched hands did not grow weary; my soul refused to be comforted.
**v3** I remembered You, O God, and I groaned; I mused and my spirit grew faint.Selah
**v4** You have kept my eyes from closing; I am too troubled to speak.
**v5** I considered the days of old, the years long in the past.
**v6** At night I remembered my song; in my heart I mused, and my spirit pondered:

**v7** "Will the Lord spurn us foreverand never show His favor again?
**v8** Is His loving devotion gone forever?Has His promise failed for all time?
**v9** Has God forgotten to be gracious?Has His anger shut off His compassion?" Selah
**v10** So I said, "I am grievedthat the right hand of the Most High has changed."[^1]

**v11** I will remember the works of the LORD; yes, I will remember Your wonders of old.
**v12** I will reflect on all You have doneand ponder Your mighty deeds.
**v13** Your way, O God, is holy.What god is so great as our God?
**v14** You are the God who works wonders; You display Your strength among the peoples.
**v15** With power You redeemed Your people, the sons of Jacob and Joseph.Selah
**v16** The waters saw You, O God; the waters saw You and swirled; even the depths were shaken.
**v17** The clouds poured down water; the skies resounded with thunder; Your arrows flashed back and forth.
**v18** Your thunder resounded in the whirlwind; the lightning lit up the world; the earth trembled and quaked.

**v19** Your path led through the sea, Your way through the mighty waters, but Your footprints were not to be found. [^2]
**v20** You led Your people like a flockby the hand of Moses and Aaron.
[^1]: Or "To this I will appeal: to the years of the right hand of the Most High." ( 77:10)
[^2]: Or were unknown ( 77:19)

### Chapter 78

#### I Will Open My Mouth in Parables

**v1** Give ear, O my people, to my instruction; listen to the words of my mouth.

**v2** I will open my mouth in parables; I will utter things hidden from the beginning, [^2]
**v3** that we have heard and knownand our fathers have relayed to us.
**v4** We will not hide them from their childrenbut will declare to the next generationthe praises of the LORD and His mightand the wonders He has performed.

**v5** For He established a testimony in Jacoband appointed a law in Israel, which He commanded our fathersto teach to their children,
**v6** that the coming generation would know them—even children yet to be born—to arise and tell their own children
**v7** that they should put their confidence in God, not forgetting His works, but keeping His commandments.
**v8** Then they will not be like their fathers, a stubborn and rebellious generation, whose heart was not loyal, whose spirit was not faithful to God.

**v9** The archers of Ephraimturned back on the day of battle.
**v10** They failed to keep God's covenantand refused to live by His law.
**v11** They forgot what He had done, the wonders He had shown them.
**v12** He worked wonders before their fathersin the land of Egypt, in the region of Zoan.
**v13** He split the sea and brought them through; He set the waters upright like a wall.
**v14** He led them with a cloud by dayand with a light of fire all night.
**v15** He split the rocks in the wildernessand gave them drink as abundant as the seas.
**v16** He brought streams from the stoneand made water flow down like rivers.

**v17** But they continued to sin against Him, rebelling in the desert against the Most High.
**v18** They willfully tested Godby demanding the food they craved.
**v19** They spoke against God, saying,"Can God really prepare a table in the wilderness?
**v20** When He struck the rock, water gushed outand torrents raged.But can He also give breador supply His people with meat?"

**v21** Therefore the LORD heardand was filled with wrath; so a fire was kindled against Jacob, and His anger flared against Israel,
**v22** because they did not believe Godor rely on His salvation.

**v23** Yet He commanded the clouds aboveand opened the doors of the heavens.
**v24** He rained down manna for them to eat; He gave them grain from heaven. [^3]
**v25** Man ate the bread of angels; He sent them food in abundance.
**v26** He stirred the east wind from the heavensand drove the south wind by His might.
**v27** He rained meat on them like dust, and winged birds like the sand of the sea.
**v28** He felled them in the midst of their camp, all around their dwellings.
**v29** So they ate and were well filled, for He gave them what they craved.

**v30** Yet before they had filled their desire, with the food still in their mouths,
**v31** God's anger flared against them, and He put to death their strongestand subdued the young men of Israel.

**v32** In spite of all this, they kept on sinning; despite His wonderful works, they did not believe.
**v33** So He ended their days in futility, [^4] and their years in sudden terror.
**v34** When He slew them, they would seek Him; they repented and searched for God.
**v35** And they remembered that God was their Rock, that God Most High [^5] was their Redeemer.

**v36** But they deceived Him with their mouths, and lied to Him with their tongues.
**v37** Their hearts were disloyal to Him, and they were unfaithful to His covenant.

**v38** And yet He was compassionate; He forgave their iniquity and did not destroy them.He often restrained His angerand did not unleash His full wrath.
**v39** He remembered that they were but flesh, a passing breeze that does not return.

**v40** How often they disobeyed Him in the wildernessand grieved Him in the desert!
**v41** Again and again they tested Godand provoked the Holy One of Israel.
**v42** They did not remember His power [^6]—the day He redeemed them from the adversary,
**v43** when He performed His signs in Egyptand His wonders in the fields of Zoan.

**v44** He turned their rivers to blood, and from their streams they could not drink.
**v45** He sent swarms of flies that devoured them, and frogs that devastated them.
**v46** He gave their crops to the grasshopper, the fruit of their labor to the locust.
**v47** He killed their vines with hailstonesand their sycamore-figs with sleet. [^7]
**v48** He abandoned their cattle to the hailand their livestock to bolts of lightning.

**v49** He unleashed His fury against them, wrath, indignation, and calamity—a band of destroying angels.
**v50** He cleared a path for His anger; He did not spare them from deathbut delivered their lives to the plague.
**v51** He struck all the firstborn of Egypt, the virility in the tents of Ham.

**v52** He led out His people like sheepand guided them like a flock in the wilderness.
**v53** He led them safely, so they did not fear, but the sea engulfed their enemies.
**v54** He brought them to His holy land, to the mountain His right hand had acquired.
**v55** He drove out nations before themand apportioned their inheritance; He settled the tribes of Israel in their tents.

**v56** But they tested and disobeyed God Most High, for they did not keep His decrees.
**v57** They turned back and were faithless like their fathers, twisted like a faulty bow.
**v58** They enraged Him with their high placesand provoked His jealousy with their idols.

**v59** On hearing it, God was furiousand rejected Israel completely.
**v60** He abandoned the tabernacle of Shiloh, the tent He had pitched among men.
**v61** He delivered His strength to captivity, and His splendor to the hand of the adversary.
**v62** He surrendered His people to the swordbecause He was enraged by His heritage.
**v63** Fire consumed His young men, and their maidens were left without wedding songs.
**v64** His priests fell by the sword, but their widows could not lament.

**v65** Then the Lord awoke as from sleep, like a mighty warrior overcome by wine.
**v66** He beat back His foes; He put them to everlasting shame.
**v67** He rejected the tent of Josephand refused the tribe of Ephraim.
**v68** But He chose the tribe of Judah, Mount Zion, which He loved.
**v69** He built His sanctuary like the heights, like the earth He has established forever.

**v70** He chose David His servantand took him from the sheepfolds;
**v71** from tending the ewes He brought himto be shepherd of His people Jacob, of Israel His inheritance.
**v72** So David shepherded them with integrity of heartand guided them with skillful hands.
[^1]: Maskil is probably a musical or liturgical term; used for Psalms 32, 42, 44–45, 52–55, 74, 78, 88–89, and 142. ( 78:0)
[^2]: Or from ancient times; see also LXX; cited in Matthew 13:35 ( 78:2)
[^3]: Cited in John 6:31 ( 78:24)
[^4]: Or in vapor ( 78:33)
[^5]: Hebrew El-Elyon ( 78:35)
[^6]: Or His hand ( 78:42)
[^7]: Or frost or driving rain ( 78:47)

### Chapter 79

#### A Prayer for Deliverance

**v1** The nations, O God, have invaded Your inheritance; they have defiled Your holy templeand reduced Jerusalem to rubble.
**v2** They have given the corpses of Your servantsas food to the birds of the air, the flesh of Your saints to the beasts of the earth.
**v3** They have poured out their blood like waterall around Jerusalem, and there is no one to bury the dead.
**v4** We have become a reproach to our neighbors, a scorn and derision to those around us.

**v5** How long, O LORD?Will You be angry forever?Will Your jealousy burn like fire?
**v6** Pour out Your wrath on the nationsthat do not acknowledge You, on the kingdomsthat refuse to call on Your name,
**v7** for they have devoured Jacoband devastated his homeland.

**v8** Do not hold past sins against us; let Your compassion come quickly, for we are brought low.
**v9** Help us, O God of our salvation, for the glory of Your name; deliver us and atone for our sins, for the sake of Your name.
**v10** Why should the nations ask,"Where is their God?" Before our eyes, make known among the nations Your vengeance for the bloodshed of Your servants.

**v11** May the groans of the captives reach You; by the strength of Your arm preserve those condemned to death.
**v12** Pay back into the laps of our neighborssevenfold the reproach they hurled at You, O Lord.
**v13** Then we Your people, the sheep of Your pasture, will thank You forever; from generation to generationwe will declare Your praise.
### Chapter 80

#### Hear Us, O Shepherd of Israel

**v1** Hear us, O Shepherd of Israel, who leads Joseph like a flock; You who sit enthroned between the cherubim, shine forth
**v2** before Ephraim, Benjamin, and Manasseh.Rally Your mighty powerand come to save us.
**v3** Restore us, O God, and cause Your face to shine upon us, that we may be saved.

**v4** O LORD God of Hosts, how long will Your anger smolderagainst the prayers of Your people?
**v5** You fed them with the bread of tearsand made them drink the full measure of their tears.
**v6** You make us contend with our neighbors; our enemies mock us.
**v7** Restore us, O God of Hosts, and cause Your face to shine upon us, that we may be saved.

**v8** You uprooted a vine from Egypt; You drove out the nations and transplanted it.
**v9** You cleared the ground for it, and it took root and filled the land.
**v10** The mountains were covered by its shade, and the mighty cedars with its branches.
**v11** It sent out its branches to the Sea, [^1] and its shoots toward the River. [^2]

**v12** Why have You broken down its walls, so that all who pass by pick its fruit?
**v13** The boar from the forest ravages it, and the creatures of the field feed upon it.
**v14** Return, O God of Hosts, we pray!Look down from heaven and see!Attend to this vine—
**v15** the root Your right hand has planted, the son You have raised up for Yourself.

**v16** Your vine has been cut down and burned; they perish at the rebuke of Your countenance.
**v17** Let Your hand be upon the man at Your right hand, on the son of man You have raised up for Yourself.
**v18** Then we will not turn away from You; revive us, and we will call on Your name.
**v19** Restore us, O LORD God of Hosts; cause Your face to shine upon us, that we may be saved.
[^1]: That is, the Mediterranean Sea, also called the Great Sea ( 80:11)
[^2]: That is, the Euphrates ( 80:11)

### Chapter 81

#### Sing for Joy to God Our Strength

**v1** Sing for joy to God our strength; make a joyful noise to the God of Jacob.
**v2** Lift up a song, strike the tambourine, play the sweet-sounding harp and lyre.
**v3** Sound the ram's horn at the New Moon, and at the full moon on the day of our Feast.
**v4** For this is a statute for Israel, an ordinance of the God of Jacob.
**v5** He ordained it as a testimony for Joseph [^2] when he went out over the land of Egypt, where I heard an unfamiliar language:

**v6** "I relieved his shoulder of the burden; his hands were freed from the basket.
**v7** You called out in distress, and I rescued you; I answered you from the cloud of thunder; I tested you at the waters of Meribah. [^3] Selah
**v8** Hear, O My people, and I will warn you:O Israel, if only you would listen to Me!
**v9** There must be no strange god among you, nor shall you bow to a foreign god.
**v10** I am the LORD your God, who brought you up out of Egypt.Open wide your mouth, and I will fill it.

**v11** But My people would not listen to Me, and Israel would not obey Me.
**v12** So I gave them up to their stubborn heartsto follow their own devices.
**v13** If only My people would listen to Me, if Israel would follow My ways,
**v14** how soon I would subdue their enemiesand turn My hand against their foes!
**v15** Those who hate the LORD would feign obedience, and their doom would last forever.
