**v16** But I would feed you the finest wheat; with honey from the rock I would satisfy you."
[^1]: Gittith is probably a musical or liturgical term; here and in Psalms 8 and 84. ( 81:0)
[^2]: Or in Joseph ( 81:5)
[^3]: Meribah means quarreling; see Exodus 17:7. ( 81:7)

### Chapter 82

#### God Presides in the Divine Assembly

**v1** God presides in the divine assembly; He renders judgment among the gods:

**v2** "How long will you judge unjustly [^1] and show partiality to the wicked?Selah
**v3** Defend the cause of the weak and fatherless; uphold the rights of the afflicted and oppressed.
**v4** Rescue the weak and needy; save them from the hand of the wicked.
**v5** They do not know or understand; they wander in the darkness; all the foundations of the earth are shaken.
**v6** I have said, 'You are gods; you are all sons of the Most High.'[^2]
**v7** But like mortals you will die, and like rulers you will fall."

**v8** Arise, O God, judge the earth, for all the nations are Your inheritance.
[^1]: Or How long will you defend the unjust ( 82:2)
[^2]: Cited in John 10:34 ( 82:6)

### Chapter 83

#### O God, Be Not Silent

**v1** O God, be not silent; be not speechless; [^1] be not still, O God.
**v2** See how Your enemies rage, how Your foes have reared their heads.
**v3** With cunning they scheme against Your peopleand conspire against those You cherish,
**v4** saying, "Come, let us erase them as a nation; may the name of Israel be remembered no more."

**v5** For with one mind they plot together; they form an alliance against You—
**v6** the tents of Edom and the Ishmaelites, of Moab and the Hagrites,
**v7** of Gebal, Ammon, and Amalek, of Philistia with the people of Tyre.
**v8** Even Assyria has joined them, lending strength to the sons of Lot.Selah
**v9** Do to them as You did to Midian, as to Sisera and Jabin at the River Kishon,
**v10** who perished at Endorand became like dung on the ground.
**v11** Make their nobles like Oreb and Zeeb, and all their princes like Zebah and Zalmunna,
**v12** who said, "Let us possess for ourselvesthe pastures of God."

**v13** Make them like tumbleweed, O my God, like chaff before the wind.
**v14** As fire consumes a forest, as a flame sets the mountains ablaze,
**v15** so pursue them with Your tempest, and terrify them with Your storm.
**v16** Cover their faces with shame, that they may seek Your name, O LORD.

**v17** May they be ever ashamed and terrified; may they perish in disgrace.
**v18** May they know that You alone, whose name is the LORD, are Most High over all the earth.
[^1]: Or deaf ( 83:1)

### Chapter 84

#### Better Is One Day in Your Courts

**v1** How lovely is Your dwelling place, O LORD of Hosts!
**v2** My soul longs, even faints, for the courts of the LORD; my heart and my flesh cry outfor the living God.

**v3** Even the sparrow has found a home, and the swallow a nest for herself, where she places her young near Your altars, O LORD of Hosts, my King and my God.
**v4** How blessed are those who dwell in Your house!They are ever praising You.Selah
**v5** Blessed are those whose strength is in You, whose hearts are set on pilgrimage.
**v6** As they pass through the Valley of Baca, [^2] they make it a place of springs; even the autumn rain covers it with pools. [^3]
**v7** They go from strength to strength, until each appears before God in Zion.

**v8** O LORD God of Hosts, hear my prayer; give ear, O God of Jacob.Selah
**v9** Take notice of our shield, O God, and look with favor on the face of Your anointed.
**v10** For better is one day in Your courtsthan a thousand elsewhere.I would rather be a doorkeeper in the house of my Godthan dwell in the tents of the wicked.
**v11** For the LORD God is a sun and a shield; the LORD gives grace and glory; He withholds no good thingfrom those who walk with integrity.

**v12** O LORD of Hosts, how blessed is the man who trusts in You!
[^1]: Gittith is probably a musical or liturgical term; here and in Psalms 8 and 81. ( 84:0)
[^2]: Or Valley of Poplars ( 84:6)
[^3]: Or with blessings ( 84:6)

### Chapter 85

#### You Showed Favor to Your Land

**v1** You showed favor to Your land, O LORD; You restored Jacob from captivity. [^1]
**v2** You forgave the iniquity of Your people; You covered all their sin.Selah
**v3** You withheld all Your fury; You turned from Your burning anger.

**v4** Restore us, O God of our salvation, and put away Your displeasure toward us.
**v5** Will You be angry with us forever?Will You draw out Your anger to all generations?
**v6** Will You not revive us again, that Your people may rejoice in You?
**v7** Show us Your loving devotion, O LORD, and grant us Your salvation.

**v8** I will listen to what God the LORD will say; for He will surely speak peace to His people and His saints; He will not let them return to folly.
**v9** Surely His salvation is near to those who fear Him, that His glory may dwell in our land.

**v10** Loving devotion and faithfulness have joined together; righteousness and peace have kissed.
**v11** Faithfulness sprouts from the earth, and righteousness looks down from heaven.
**v12** The LORD will indeed provide what is good, and our land will yield its increase.
**v13** Righteousness will go before Himto prepare the way for His steps.
[^1]: Or restored the fortunes of Jacob ( 85:1)

### Chapter 86

#### Tried but Trusting

**v1** Incline Your ear, O LORD, and answer me, for I am poor and needy.
**v2** Preserve my soul, for I am godly.You are my God; save Your servant who trusts in You.
**v3** Be merciful to me, O Lord, for I call to You all day long.
**v4** Bring joy to Your servant, for to You, O Lord, I lift up my soul.

**v5** For You, O Lord, are kind and forgiving, rich in loving devotion to all who call on You.
**v6** Hear my prayer, O LORD, and attend to my plea for mercy.
**v7** In the day of my distress I call on You, because You answer me.

**v8** O Lord, there is none like You among the gods, nor any works like Yours.
**v9** All the nations You have madewill come and bow before You, O Lord, and they will glorify Your name.
**v10** For You are great and perform wonders; You alone are God.

**v11** Teach me Your way, O LORD, that I may walk in Your truth.Give me an undivided heart, that I may fear Your name.
**v12** I will praise You, O Lord my God, with all my heart; I will glorify Your name forever.
**v13** For great is Your loving devotion to me; You have delivered me from the depths of Sheol.

**v14** The arrogant rise against me, O God; a band of ruthless men seeks my life; they have no regard for You.
**v15** But You, O Lord, are a compassionate and gracious God, slow to anger, abounding in loving devotion and faithfulness.

**v16** Turn to me and have mercy; grant Your strength to Your servant; save the son of Your maidservant.
**v17** Show me a sign of Your goodness, that my enemies may see and be ashamed; for You, O LORD, have helped me and comforted me.
### Chapter 87

#### The LORD Loves the Gates of Zion

**v1** He has founded His cityon the holy mountains. [^1]
**v2** The LORD loves the gates of Zionmore than all the dwellings of Jacob.
**v3** Glorious things are ascribed to you, O city of God.Selah
**v4** "I will mention Rahab [^2] and Babylonamong those who know Me—along with Philistia, Tyre, and Cush [^3]—when I say, 'This one was born in Zion.'"

**v5** And it will be said of Zion: "This one and that one were born in her, and the Most High Himself will establish her."

**v6** The LORD will record in the register of the peoples: "This one was born in Zion." Selah
**v7** Singers and pipers will proclaim,"All my springs of joy are in You."
[^1]: Literally His foundation is on the holy mountains ( 87:1)
[^2]: Rahab is a poetic name for Egypt. ( 87:4)
[^3]: That is, the upper Nile region ( 87:4)

### Chapter 88

#### I Cry Out before You

**v1** O LORD, the God of my salvation, day and night I cry out before You.
**v2** May my prayer come before You; incline Your ear to my cry.
**v3** For my soul is full of troubles, and my life draws near to Sheol.
**v4** I am counted among those descending to the Pit.I am like a man without strength.

**v5** I am forsaken among the dead, like the slain who lie in the grave, whom You remember no more, who are cut off from Your care.

**v6** You have laid me in the lowest Pit, in the darkest of the depths.
**v7** Your wrath weighs heavily upon me; all Your waves have submerged me.Selah
**v8** You have removed my friends from me; You have made me repulsive to them; I am confined and cannot escape.
**v9** My eyes grow dim with grief.I call to You daily, O LORD; I spread out my hands to You.
**v10** Do You work wonders for the dead?Do departed spirits rise up to praise You?Selah
**v11** Can Your loving devotion be proclaimed in the grave, Your faithfulness in Abaddon [^3]?
**v12** Will Your wonders be known in the darkness, or Your righteousness in the land of oblivion?

**v13** But to You, O LORD, I cry for help; in the morning my prayer comes before You.
**v14** Why, O LORD, do You reject me?Why do You hide Your face from me?

**v15** From my youth I was afflicted and near death.I have borne Your terrors; I am in despair.
**v16** Your wrath has swept over me; Your terrors have destroyed me.
**v17** All day long they engulf me like water; they enclose me on every side.
**v18** You have removed my beloved and my friend; darkness is my closest companion.
[^1]: Mahalath Leannoth is probably a musical or liturgical term; see also Psalms 53:1. ( 88:0)
[^2]: Maskil is probably a musical or liturgical term; used for Psalms 32, 42, 44–45, 52–55, 74, 78, 88–89, and 142. ( 88:0)
[^3]: Abaddon means Destruction. ( 88:11)

### Chapter 89

#### I Will Sing of His Love Forever

**v1** I will sing of the loving devotion of the LORD forever; with my mouth I will proclaim Your faithfulness to all generations.
**v2** For I have said, "Loving devotion is built up forever; in the heavens You establish Your faithfulness."

**v3** You said, "I have made a covenant with My chosen one, I have sworn to David My servant:
**v4** 'I will establish your offspring foreverand build up your throne for all generations.'"Selah
**v5** The heavens praise Your wonders, O LORD—Your faithfulness as well—in the assembly of the holy ones.
**v6** For who in the skies can compare with the LORD?Who among the heavenly beings [^2] is like the LORD?
**v7** In the council of the holy ones, God is greatly feared, and awesome above all who surround Him.

**v8** O LORD God of Hosts, who is like You?O mighty LORD, Your faithfulness surrounds You.
**v9** You rule the raging sea; when its waves mount up, You still them.
**v10** You crushed Rahab like a carcass; You scattered Your enemies with Your mighty arm.
**v11** The heavens are Yours, and also the earth.The earth and its fullness You founded.
**v12** North and south You created; Tabor and Hermon shout for joy at Your name.

**v13** Mighty is Your arm; strong is Your hand.Your right hand is exalted.
**v14** Righteousness and justice are the foundation of Your throne; loving devotion and faithfulness go before You.

**v15** Blessed are those who know the joyful sound, who walk, O LORD, in the light of Your presence.
**v16** They rejoice in Your name all day long, and in Your righteousness they exult.
**v17** For You are the glory of their strength, and by Your favor our horn is exalted.
**v18** Surely our shield belongs to the LORD, and our king to the Holy One of Israel.

**v19** You once spoke in a vision; to Your godly ones You said,"I have bestowed help on a warrior; I have exalted one chosen from the people.
**v20** I have found My servant David; with My sacred oil I have anointed him.
**v21** My hand will sustain him; surely My arm will strengthen him.

**v22** No enemy will exact tribute; no wicked man will oppress him.
**v23** I will crush his foes before himand strike down those who hate him.
**v24** My faithfulness and loving devotion will be with him, and through My name his horn will be exalted.
**v25** I will set his hand over the sea, and his right hand upon the rivers.
**v26** He will call to Me, 'You are my Father, my God, the Rock of my salvation.'

**v27** I will indeed appoint him as My firstborn, the highest of the kings of the earth.
**v28** I will forever preserve My loving devotion for him, and My covenant with him will stand fast.
**v29** I will establish his line forever, his throne as long as the heavens endure.

**v30** If his sons forsake My lawand do not walk in My judgments,
**v31** if they violate My statutesand fail to keep My commandments,
**v32** I will attend to their transgression with the rod, and to their iniquity with stripes.

**v33** But I will not withdraw My loving devotion from him, nor ever betray My faithfulness.
**v34** I will not violate My covenantor alter the utterance of My lips.
**v35** Once and for all I have sworn by My holiness—I will not lie to David—
**v36** his offspring shall endure forever, and his throne before Me like the sun,
**v37** like the moon, established forever, a faithful witness in the sky." Selah
**v38** Now, however, You have spurned and rejected him; You are enraged by Your anointed one.
**v39** You have renounced the covenant with Your servantand sullied his crown in the dust.
**v40** You have broken down all his walls; You have reduced his strongholds to rubble.
**v41** All who pass by plunder him; he has become a reproach to his neighbors.

**v42** You have exalted the right hand of his foes; You have made all his enemies rejoice.
**v43** You have bent the edge of his swordand have not sustained him in battle.
**v44** You have ended his splendorand cast his throne to the ground.
**v45** You have cut short the days of his youth; You have covered him with shame.Selah
**v46** How long, O LORD?Will You hide Yourself forever?Will Your wrath keep burning like fire?
**v47** Remember the briefness of my lifespan!For what futility You have created all men!
**v48** What man can live and never see death?Can he deliver his soul from the power of Sheol?Selah
**v49** Where, O Lord, is Your loving devotion of old, which You faithfully swore to David?
**v50** Remember, O Lord, the reproach of Your servants, which I bear in my heart from so many people—
**v51** how Your enemies have taunted, O LORD, and have mocked every step of Your anointed one!

**v52** Blessed be the LORD forever!Amen and amen.
[^1]: Maskil is probably a musical or liturgical term; used for Psalms 32, 42, 44–45, 52–55, 74, 78, 88–89, and 142. ( 89:0)
[^2]: Or the sons of God or the sons of might ( 89:6)

### Chapter 90

#### From Everlasting to Everlasting


**v1** Lord, You have been our dwelling placethrough all generations.
**v2** Before the mountains were bornor You brought forth the earth and the world, from everlasting to everlasting You are God.

**v3** You return man to dust, saying, "Return, O sons of mortals."
**v4** For in Your sight a thousand yearsare but a day that passes, [^1] or a watch of the night.
**v5** You sweep them away in their sleep; they are like the new grass of the morning—
**v6** in the morning it springs up new, but by evening it fades and withers.

**v7** For we are consumed by Your angerand terrified by Your wrath.
**v8** You have set our iniquities before You, our secret sins in the light of Your presence.
**v9** For all our days decline in Your fury; we finish our years with a sigh.
**v10** The length of our days is seventy years—or eighty if we are strong—yet their pride is but labor and sorrow, for they quickly pass, and we fly away.

**v11** Who knows the power of Your anger?Your wrath matches the fear You are due.
**v12** So teach us to number our days, that we may present a heart of wisdom.

**v13** Return, O LORD! How long will it be?Have compassion on Your servants.
**v14** Satisfy us in the morning with Your loving devotion, that we may sing for joy and be glad all our days.
**v15** Make us glad for as many days as You have afflicted us, for as many years as we have seen evil.

**v16** May Your work be shown to Your servants, and Your splendor to their children.
**v17** May the favor [^2] of the Lord our God rest upon us; establish for us the work of our hands—yes, establish the work of our hands!
[^1]: See 2 Peter 3:8. ( 90:4)
[^2]: Or beauty ( 90:17)

### Chapter 91

#### You Are My Refuge and My Fortress
**v1** He who dwells in the shelter of the Most Highwill abide in the shadow of the Almighty. [^1]
**v2** I will say to the LORD, "You are my refuge and my fortress, my God, in whom I trust."

**v3** Surely He will deliver youfrom the snare of the fowler, and from the deadly plague.
**v4** He will cover you with His feathers; under His wings you will find refuge; His faithfulness is a shield and rampart.
**v5** You will not fear the terror of the night, nor the arrow that flies by day,
**v6** nor the pestilence that stalks in the darkness, nor the calamity that destroys at noon.
**v7** Though a thousand may fall at your side, and ten thousand at your right hand, no harm will come near you.
**v8** You will only see it with your eyesand witness the punishment of the wicked.

**v9** Because you have made the LORD your dwelling—my refuge, the Most High—
**v10** no evil will befall you, no plague will approach your tent.
**v11** For He will command His angels concerning youto guard you in all your ways.
**v12** They will lift you up in their hands, so that you will not strike your foot against a stone. [^2]
**v13** You will tread on the lion and cobra; you will trample the young lion and serpent.

**v14** "Because he loves Me, I will deliver him; because he knows My name, I will protect him.
**v15** When he calls out to Me, I will answer him; I will be with him in trouble.I will deliver him and honor him.
**v16** With long life I will satisfy himand show him My salvation."
[^1]: Hebrew Shaddai ( 91:1)
[^2]: Cited in Matthew 4:6 and Luke 4:10–11 ( 91:12)

### Chapter 92

#### How Great Are Your Works!

**v1** It is good to praise the LORD, and to sing praises to Your name, O Most High,
**v2** to proclaim Your loving devotion in the morningand Your faithfulness at night
**v3** with the ten-stringed harpand the melody of the lyre.

**v4** For You, O LORD, have made me glad by Your deeds; I sing for joy at the works of Your hands.
**v5** How great are Your works, O LORD, how deep are Your thoughts!
**v6** A senseless man does not know, and a fool does not understand,
**v7** that though the wicked sprout like grass, and all evildoers flourish, they will be forever destroyed.

**v8** But You, O LORD, are exalted forever!

**v9** For surely Your enemies, O LORD, surely Your enemies will perish; all evildoers will be scattered.
**v10** But You have exalted my horn like that of a wild ox; with fine oil I have been anointed.
**v11** My eyes see the downfall of my enemies; my ears hear the wailing of my wicked foes. [^1]

**v12** The righteous will flourish like a palm tree, and grow like a cedar in Lebanon.
**v13** Planted in the house of the LORD, they will flourish in the courts of our God.
**v14** In old age they will still bear fruit; healthy and green they will remain,
**v15** to proclaim, "The LORD is upright; He is my Rock, and in Him there is no unrighteousness."
[^1]: Or my ears hear evildoers when they rise against me ( 92:11)

### Chapter 93

#### The LORD Reigns!
**v1** The LORD reigns! He is robed in majesty; the LORD has clothed and armed Himself with strength.The world indeed is firmly established; it cannot be moved.
**v2** Your throne was established long ago; You are from all eternity.

**v3** The floodwaters have risen, O LORD; the rivers have raised their voice; the seas lift up their pounding waves.
**v4** Above the roar of many waters—the mighty breakers of the sea—the LORD on high is majestic.

**v5** Your testimonies are fully confirmed; holiness adorns Your house, O LORD, for all the days to come.
### Chapter 94

#### The LORD Will Not Forget His People
**v1** O LORD, God of vengeance, O God of vengeance, shine forth.
**v2** Rise up, O Judge of the earth; render a reward to the proud.
**v3** How long will the wicked, O LORD, how long will the wicked exult?

**v4** They pour out arrogant words; all workers of iniquity boast.
**v5** They crush Your people, O LORD; they oppress Your heritage.
**v6** They kill the widow and the foreigner; they murder the fatherless.
**v7** They say, "The LORD does not see; the God of Jacob pays no heed."

**v8** Take notice, O senseless among the people!O fools, when will you be wise?
**v9** He who affixed the ear, can He not hear?He who formed the eye, can He not see?
**v10** He who admonishes the nations, does He not discipline?He who teaches man, does He lack knowledge?
**v11** The LORD knows the thoughts of man, that they are futile. [^1]

**v12** Blessed is the man You discipline, O LORD, and teach from Your law,
**v13** to grant him relief from days of trouble, until a pit is dug for the wicked.
**v14** For the LORD will not forsake His people; He will never abandon His heritage.
**v15** Surely judgment will again be righteous, and all the upright in heart will follow it.

**v16** Who will rise up for me against the wicked?Who will stand for me against the workers of iniquity?
**v17** Unless the LORD had been my helper, I would soon have dwelt in the abode of silence.
**v18** If I say, "My foot is slipping,"Your loving devotion, O LORD, supports me.
**v19** When anxiety overwhelms me, Your consolation delights my soul.

**v20** Can a corrupt throne be Your ally—one devising mischief by decree?
**v21** They band together against the righteousand condemn the innocent to death. [^2]
**v22** But the LORD has been my stronghold, and my God is my rock of refuge.
**v23** He will bring upon them their own iniquityand destroy them for their wickedness.The LORD our God will destroy them.
[^1]: Cited in 1 Corinthians 3:20 ( 94:11)
[^2]: Or condemn innocent blood ( 94:21)

### Chapter 95

#### Do Not Harden Your Hearts
**v1** Come, let us sing for joy to the LORD; let us shout to the Rock of our salvation!
**v2** Let us enter His presence with thanksgiving; let us make a joyful noise to Him in song.

**v3** For the LORD is a great God, a great King above all gods.
**v4** In His hand are the depths of the earth, and the mountain peaks belong to Him.
**v5** The sea is His, for He made it, and His hands formed the dry land.

**v6** O come, let us worship and bow down; let us kneel before the LORD our Maker.
**v7** For He is our God, and we are the people of His pasture, the sheep under His care.Today, if you hear His voice,
**v8** do not harden your heartsas you did at Meribah, [^1] in the day at Massah in the wilderness, [^2]
**v9** where your fathers tested and tried Me, though they had seen My work.
**v10** For forty years I was angry with that generation, and I said, "They are a people whose hearts go astray, [^3] and they have not known My ways."
**v11** So I swore on oath in My anger,"They shall never enter My rest."[^4]
[^1]: LXX as you did in the rebellion; Meribah means quarreling; see Exodus 17:7; cited in Hebrews 3:15 and Hebrews 4:7. ( 95:8)
[^2]: LXX in the day of testing in the wilderness; Massah means testing; see Exodus 17:7. ( 95:8)
[^3]: LXX They always go astray in the heart ( 95:10)
[^4]: Cited in Hebrews 3:7–11, Hebrews 4:3, and Hebrews 4:5 ( 95:11)

### Chapter 96

#### Sing to the LORD, All the Earth
**v1** Sing to the LORD a new song; sing to the LORD, all the earth.
**v2** Sing to the LORD, bless His name; proclaim His salvation day after day.
**v3** Declare His glory among the nations, His wonders among all peoples.

**v4** For great is the LORD, and greatly to be praised; He is to be feared above all gods.
**v5** For all the gods of the nations are idols, but it is the LORD who made the heavens.
**v6** Splendor and majesty are before Him; strength and beauty fill His sanctuary.

**v7** Ascribe to the LORD, O families of the nations, ascribe to the LORD glory and strength.
**v8** Ascribe to the LORD the glory due His name; bring an offering and enter His courts.
**v9** Worship the LORD in the splendor of His holiness; tremble before Him, all the earth.

**v10** Declare among the nations: "The LORD reigns!" The world is firmly established; it cannot be moved; He will judge the peoples with equity.

**v11** Let the heavens be gladand the earth rejoice; let the sea resound, and all that fills it.
**v12** Let the fields exult, and all that is in them.Then all the trees of the forestwill sing for joy
**v13** before the LORD, for He is coming—He is coming to judge the earth.He will judge the world in righteousnessand the peoples in His faithfulness.
### Chapter 97

#### Let the Earth Rejoice
**v1** The LORD reigns, let the earth rejoice; let the distant shores be glad.

**v2** Clouds and darkness surround Him; righteousness and justice are His throne's foundation.
**v3** Fire goes before Himand consumes His foes on every side.
**v4** His lightning illuminates the world; the earth sees and trembles.
**v5** The mountains melt like waxat the presence of the LORD, before the Lord of all the earth.
**v6** The heavens proclaim His righteousness; all the peoples see His glory.

**v7** All worshipers of images are put to shame—those who boast in idols.Worship Him, all you gods!
**v8** Zion hears and rejoices, and the towns of Judah exultbecause of Your judgments, O LORD.
**v9** For You, O LORD, are Most High over all the earth; You are exalted far above all gods.

**v10** Hate evil, O you who love the LORD!He preserves the souls of His saints; He delivers them from the hand of the wicked.
**v11** Light shines [^1] on the righteous, gladness on the upright in heart.
**v12** Rejoice in the LORD, you righteous ones, and praise His holy name.
[^1]: One Hebrew manuscript, LXX, Syriac, and Vulgate; most Hebrew manuscripts Light is sown ( 97:11)

### Chapter 98

#### Sing to the LORD a New Song

**v1** Sing to the LORD a new song, for He has done wonders; His right hand and holy armhave gained Him the victory.
**v2** The LORD has proclaimed His salvationand revealed His righteousness to the nations.
**v3** He has remembered His love and faithfulnessto the house of Israel; all the ends of the earthhave seen the salvation of our God.

**v4** Make a joyful noise to the LORD, all the earth; break forth—let your cry ring out, and sing praises!
**v5** Sing praises to the LORD with the lyre, in melodious song with the harp.
**v6** With trumpets and the blast of the ram's hornshout for joy before the LORD, the King.

**v7** Let the sea resound, and all that fills it, the world, and all who dwell in it.
**v8** Let the rivers clap their hands, let the mountains sing together for joy
**v9** before the LORD, for He comes to judge the earth.He will judge the world with righteousnessand the peoples with equity.
### Chapter 99

#### The LORD Reigns!
**v1** The LORD reigns; let the nations tremble!He is enthroned above the cherubim; let the earth quake!
**v2** Great is the LORD in Zion; He is exalted above all the peoples.
**v3** Let them praise Your great and awesome name—He is holy! [^1]

**v4** The mighty King loves justice. [^2] You have established equity; You have exercised justiceand righteousness in Jacob.
**v5** Exalt the LORD our God, and worship at His footstool; He is holy!

**v6** Moses and Aaron were among His priests; Samuel was among those who called on His name.They called to the LORD and He answered.
**v7** He spoke to them from the pillar of cloud; they kept His decrees and the statutes He gave them.
**v8** O LORD our God, You answered them.You were a forgiving God to them, yet an avenger of their misdeeds.

**v9** Exalt the LORD our Godand worship at His holy mountain, for the LORD our God is holy.
[^1]: Or it is holy! ( 99:3)
[^2]: Or The might of the King loves justice. ( 99:4)

### Chapter 100

#### Make a Joyful Noise

**v1** Make a joyful noise to the LORD, all the earth.

**v2** Serve the LORD with gladness; come into His presence with joyful songs.
**v3** Know that the LORD is God.It is He who made us, and we are His; [^1] we are His people, and the sheep of His pasture.
**v4** Enter His gates with thanksgivingand His courts with praise; give thanks to Him and bless His name.

**v5** For the LORD is good, and His loving devotion endures forever; His faithfulness continues to all generations.
[^1]: Or and not we ourselves ( 100:3)

### Chapter 101

#### I Will Set No Worthless Thing before My Eyes
**v1** I will sing of Your loving devotion and justice; to You, O LORD, I will sing praises.

**v2** I will ponder the way that is blameless—when will You come to me?I will walk in my housewith integrity of heart.
**v3** I will set no worthless thingbefore my eyes.I hate the work of those who fall away; it shall not cling to me.
**v4** A perverse heart shall depart from me; I will know nothing of evil.

**v5** Whoever slanders his neighbor in secret, I will put to silence; the one with haughty eyes and a proud heart, I will not endure.
**v6** My eyes favor the faithful of the land, that they may dwell with me; he who walks in the way of integrityshall minister to me.

**v7** No one who practices deceitshall dwell in my house; no one who tells liesshall stand in my presence.
**v8** Every morning I will remove all the wicked of the land, that I may cut off every evildoer from the city of the LORD.
### Chapter 102

#### The Prayer of the Afflicted

**v1** Hear my prayer, O LORD; let my cry for help come before You.
**v2** Do not hide Your face from mein my day of distress.Incline Your ear to me; answer me quickly when I call.

**v3** For my days vanish like smoke, and my bones burn like glowing embers.
**v4** My heart is afflicted, and withered like grass; I even forget to eat my bread.
**v5** Through my loud groaningmy skin hangs on my bones.
**v6** I am like a desert owl, like an owl among the ruins.
**v7** I lie awake; I am like a lone bird on a housetop.

**v8** All day long my enemies taunt me; they ridicule me and curse me.
**v9** For I have eaten ashes like breadand mixed my drink with tears
**v10** because of Your indignation and wrath, for You have picked me up and cast me aside.
**v11** My days are like lengthening shadows, and I wither away like grass.

**v12** But You, O LORD, sit enthroned forever; Your renown endures to all generations.
**v13** You will rise up and have compassion on Zion, for it is time to show her favor—the appointed time has come.
**v14** For Your servants delight in her stonesand take pity on her dust.

**v15** So the nations will fear the name of the LORD, and all the kings of the earth will fear Your glory.
**v16** For the LORD will rebuild Zion; He has appeared in His glory.
**v17** He will turn toward the prayer of the destitute; He will not despise their prayer.

**v18** Let this be written for the generation to come, so that a people not yet created may praise the LORD.
**v19** For He looked down from the heights of His sanctuary; the LORD gazed out from heaven to earth
**v20** to hear a prisoner's groaning, to release those condemned to death,
**v21** that they may proclaim the name of the LORD in Zionand praise Him in Jerusalem,
**v22** when peoples and kingdoms assembleto serve the LORD.

**v23** He has broken my strength on the way; He has cut short my days.
**v24** I say: "O my God, do not take me in the midst of my days!Your years go on through all generations.
**v25** In the beginning You laid the foundations of the earth, and the heavens are the work of Your hands.
**v26** They will perish, but You remain; they will all wear out like a garment.Like clothing You will change them, and they will be passed on.
**v27** But You remain the same, and Your years will never end. [^1]
**v28** The children of Your servants will dwell securely, and their descendants will be established before You."
[^1]: Cited in Hebrews 1:10–12 ( 102:27)

### Chapter 103

#### Bless the LORD, O My Soul

**v1** Bless the LORD, O my soul; all that is within me, bless His holy name.
**v2** Bless the LORD, O my soul, and do not forget all His kind deeds—
**v3** He who forgives all your iniquitiesand heals all your diseases,
**v4** who redeems your life from the Pitand crowns you with loving devotion and compassion,
**v5** who satisfies you with good things, so that your youth is renewed like the eagle's.

**v6** The LORD executes righteousnessand justice for all the oppressed.
**v7** He made known His ways to Moses, His deeds to the people of Israel.
**v8** The LORD is compassionate and gracious, slow to anger, abounding in loving devotion.
**v9** He will not always accuse us, nor harbor His anger forever.
**v10** He has not dealt with us according to our sinsor repaid us according to our iniquities.

**v11** For as high as the heavens are above the earth, so great is His loving devotion for those who fear Him.
**v12** As far as the east is from the west, so far has He removed our transgressions from us.
**v13** As a father has compassion on his children, so the LORD has compassion on those who fear Him.
**v14** For He knows our frame; He is mindful that we are dust.

**v15** As for man, his days are like grass—he blooms like a flower of the field;
**v16** when the wind passes over, it vanishes, and its place remembers it no more.
**v17** But from everlasting to everlastingthe loving devotion of the LORDextends to those who fear Him, and His righteousness to their children's children—
**v18** to those who keep His covenantand remember to obey His precepts.
**v19** The LORD has established His throne in heaven, and His kingdom rules over all.

**v20** Bless the LORD, all His angels mighty in strengthwho carry out His word, who hearken to the voice of His command.
**v21** Bless the LORD, all His hosts, you servants who do His will.
**v22** Bless the LORD, all His worksin all places of His dominion.Bless the LORD, O my soul!
### Chapter 104

#### How Many Are Your Works, O LORD!
**v1** Bless the LORD, O my soul!O LORD my God, You are very great; You are clothed with splendor and majesty.
**v2** He wraps Himself in light as with a garment; He stretches out the heavens like a tent,
**v3** laying the beams of His chambersin the waters above, making the clouds His chariot, walking on the wings of the wind.
**v4** He makes the winds His messengers, flames of fire His servants. [^1]

**v5** He set the earth on its foundations, never to be moved.
**v6** You covered it with the deep like a garment; the waters stood above the mountains.
**v7** At Your rebuke the waters fled; at the sound of Your thunder they hurried away—
**v8** the mountains rose and the valleys sankto the place You assigned for them—
**v9** You set a boundary they cannot cross, that they may never again cover the earth.

**v10** He sends forth springs in the valleys; they flow between the mountains.
**v11** They give drink to every beast of the field; the wild donkeys quench their thirst.
**v12** The birds of the air nest beside the springs; they sing among the branches.
**v13** He waters the mountains from His chambers; the earth is satisfied by the fruit of His works.

**v14** He makes the grass grow for the livestockand provides crops for man to cultivate, bringing forth food from the earth:
**v15** wine that gladdens the heart of man, oil that makes his face to shine, and bread that sustains his heart.
**v16** The trees of the LORD have their fill, the cedars of Lebanon that He planted,
**v17** where the birds build their nests; the stork makes her home in the cypresses. [^2]
**v18** The high mountains are for the wild goats, the cliffs a refuge for the rock badgers. [^3]

**v19** He made the moon to mark the seasons; the sun knows when to set.
**v20** You bring darkness, and it becomes night, when all the beasts of the forest prowl.
**v21** The young lions roar for their preyand seek their food from God.
**v22** The sun rises, and they withdraw; they lie down in their dens.
**v23** Man goes forth to his workand to his labor until evening.

**v24** How many are Your works, O LORD!In wisdom You have made them all; the earth is full of Your creatures.
**v25** Here is the sea, vast and wide, teeming with creatures beyond number, living things both great and small.
**v26** There the ships pass, and Leviathan, which You formed to frolic there.

**v27** All creatures look to Youto give them their food in due season.
**v28** When You give it to them, they gather it up; when You open Your hand, they are satisfied with good things.
**v29** When You hide Your face, they are terrified; when You take away their breath, they die and return to dust.
**v30** When You send Your Spirit, [^4] they are created, and You renewthe face of the earth.

**v31** May the glory of the LORD endure forever; may the LORD rejoice in His works.
**v32** He looks on the earth, and it trembles; He touches the mountains, and they smolder.
**v33** I will sing to the LORD all my life; I will sing praise to my God while I have my being.
**v34** May my meditation be pleasing to Him, for I rejoice in the LORD.
**v35** May sinners vanish from the earthand the wicked be no more.Bless the LORD, O my soul.Hallelujah! [^5]
[^1]: LXX He makes His angels winds, His servants flames of fire. Cited in Hebrews 1:7 ( 104:4)
[^2]: Or pines or junipers or firs ( 104:17)
[^3]: Or the coneys or the hyraxes ( 104:18)
[^4]: Or breath ( 104:30)
[^5]: Or Hallelu YAH, meaning Praise the LORD ( 104:35)

### Chapter 105

#### Tell of His Wonders
**v1** Give thanks to the LORD, call upon His name; make known His deeds among the nations.
**v2** Sing to Him, sing praises to Him; tell of all His wonders.
**v3** Glory in His holy name; let the hearts of those who seek the LORD rejoice.
**v4** Seek out the LORD and His strength; seek His face always.
**v5** Remember the wonders He has done, His marvels, and the judgments He has pronounced,
**v6** O offspring of His servant Abraham, O sons of Jacob, His chosen ones.

**v7** He is the LORD our God; His judgments carry throughout the earth.
**v8** He remembers His covenant forever, the word He ordained for a thousand generations—
**v9** the covenant He made with Abraham, and the oath He swore to Isaac.
**v10** He confirmed it to Jacob as a decree, to Israel as an everlasting covenant:
**v11** "I will give you the land of Canaanas the portion of your inheritance."

**v12** When they were few in number, few indeed, and strangers in the land,
**v13** they wandered from nation to nation, from one kingdom to another.
**v14** He let no man oppress them; He rebuked kings on their behalf:
**v15** "Do not touch My anointed ones!Do no harm to My prophets!"

**v16** He called down famine on the landand cut off all their supplies [^1] of food.
**v17** He sent a man before them—Joseph, sold as a slave.
**v18** They bruised his feet with shacklesand placed his neck in irons,
**v19** until his prediction came trueand the word of the LORD proved him right.
**v20** The king sent and released him; the ruler of peoples set him free.
**v21** He made him master of his household, ruler over all his substance,
**v22** to instruct [^2] his princes as he pleasedand teach his elders wisdom.

**v23** Then Israel entered Egypt; Jacob dwelt in the land of Ham.
**v24** And the LORD made His people very fruitful, more numerous than their foes,
**v25** whose hearts He turned to hate His people, to conspire against His servants.
**v26** He sent Moses His servant, and Aaron, whom He had chosen.
**v27** They performed His miraculous signs among them, and wonders in the land of Ham.
**v28** He sent darkness, and it became dark—yet they defied His words. [^3]

**v29** He turned their waters to bloodand caused their fish to die.
**v30** Their land teemed with frogs, even in their royal chambers.
**v31** He spoke, and insects swarmed—gnats throughout their country.
**v32** He gave them hail for rain, with lightning throughout their land.
**v33** He struck their vines and fig treesand shattered the trees of their country.
**v34** He spoke, and the locusts came—young locusts without number.
**v35** They devoured every plant in their landand consumed the produce of their soil.
**v36** Then He struck all the firstborn in their land, the firstfruits of all their vigor.

**v37** He brought Israel out with silver and gold, and none among His tribes stumbled.
**v38** Egypt was glad when they departed, for the dread of Israel had fallen on them.
**v39** He spread a cloud as a coveringand a fire to light up the night.
**v40** They asked, and He brought quailand satisfied them with the bread of heaven.
**v41** He opened a rock, and water gushed out; it flowed like a river in the desert.
**v42** For He remembered His holy promiseto Abraham His servant.
**v43** He brought forth His people with rejoicing, His chosen with shouts of joy.
**v44** He gave them the lands of the nations, that they might inherit the fruit of others' labor,
**v45** that they might keep His statutesand obey His laws.Hallelujah! [^4]
[^1]: Hebrew staff ( 105:16)
[^2]: LXX and Syriac; MT to bind ( 105:22)
[^3]: LXX and Syriac; Hebrew for had they not defied His words? ( 105:28)
[^4]: Or Hallelu YAH, meaning Praise the LORD ( 105:45)

### Chapter 106

#### Give Thanks to the LORD, for He Is Good
**v1** Hallelujah! [^1] Give thanks to the LORD, for He is good; His loving devotion endures forever.
**v2** Who can describe the mighty acts of the LORDor fully proclaim His praise?
**v3** Blessed are those who uphold justice, who practice righteousness at all times.

**v4** Remember me, O LORD, in Your favor to Your people; visit me with Your salvation,
**v5** that I may see the prosperity of Your chosen ones, and rejoice in the gladness of Your nation, and give glory with Your inheritance.

**v6** We have sinned like our fathers; we have done wrong and acted wickedly.
**v7** Our fathers in Egypt did not grasp Your wondersor remember Your abundant kindness; but they rebelled by the sea, there at the Red Sea. [^2]
**v8** Yet He saved them for the sake of His name, to make His power known.
**v9** He rebuked the Red Sea, and it dried up; He led them through the depths as through a desert.
**v10** He saved them from the hand that hated them; He redeemed them from the hand of the enemy.
**v11** The waters covered their foes; not one of them remained.
**v12** Then they believed His promisesand sang His praise.

**v13** Yet they soon forgot His worksand failed to wait for His counsel.
**v14** They craved intensely in the wildernessand tested God in the desert.
**v15** So He granted their request, but sent a wasting disease upon them.

**v16** In the camp they envied Moses, as well as Aaron, the holy one of the LORD.
**v17** The earth opened up and swallowed Dathan; it covered the assembly of Abiram.
**v18** Then fire blazed through their company; flames consumed the wicked.

**v19** At Horeb [^3] they made a calfand worshiped a molten image.
**v20** They exchanged their Glory [^4] for the image of a grass-eating ox.
**v21** They forgot God their Savior, who did great things in Egypt,
**v22** wondrous works in the land of Ham, and awesome deeds by the Red Sea.
**v23** So He said He would destroy them—had not Moses His chosen onestood before Him in the breachto divert His wrath from destroying them.

**v24** They despised the pleasant land; they did not believe His promise.
**v25** They grumbled in their tentsand did not listen to the voice of the LORD.
**v26** So He raised His hand and sworeto cast them down in the wilderness,
**v27** to disperse [^5] their offspring among the nationsand scatter them throughout the lands.

**v28** They yoked themselves to Baal of Peorand ate sacrifices offered to lifeless gods.
**v29** So they provoked the LORD to anger with their deeds, and a plague broke out among them.
**v30** But Phinehas stood and intervened, and the plague was restrained.
**v31** It was credited to him as righteousnessfor endless generations to come.

**v32** At the waters of Meribah [^6] they angered the LORD, and trouble came to Moses because of them.
**v33** For they rebelled against His Spirit, [^7] and Moses spoke rashly with his lips.

**v34** They did not destroy the peoplesas the LORD had commanded them,
**v35** but they mingled with the nationsand adopted their customs.
**v36** They worshiped their idols, which became a snare to them.
**v37** They sacrificed their sonsand their daughters to demons.
**v38** They shed innocent blood—the blood of their sons and daughters, whom they sacrificed to the idols of Canaan, and the land was polluted with blood.
**v39** They defiled themselves by their actionsand prostituted themselves by their deeds.

**v40** So the anger of the LORD burned against His people, and He abhorred His own inheritance.
**v41** He delivered them into the hand of the nations, and those who hated them ruled over them.
**v42** Their enemies oppressed themand subdued them under their hand.
**v43** Many times He rescued them, but they were bent on rebellionand sank down in their iniquity.

**v44** Nevertheless He heard their cry; He took note of their distress.
**v45** And He remembered His covenant with them, and relented by the abundance of His loving devotion.
**v46** He made them objects of compassionto all who held them captive.

**v47** Save us, O LORD our God, and gather us from the nations, that we may give thanks to Your holy name, that we may glory in Your praise.

**v48** Blessed be the LORD, the God of Israel, from everlasting to everlasting.Let all the people say, "Amen!" Hallelujah!
[^1]: Or Hallelu YAH, meaning Praise the LORD; also in verse 48 ( 106:1)
[^2]: Or the Sea of Reeds; also in verses 9 and 22 ( 106:7)
[^3]: That is, Mount Sinai, or possibly a mountain in the range containing Mount Sinai ( 106:19)
[^4]: Or their glorious God ( 106:20)
[^5]: Or cast down or cause to fall ( 106:27)
[^6]: Meribah means quarreling; see Exodus 17:7. ( 106:32)
[^7]: Or they provoked His Spirit ( 106:33)

### Chapter 107

#### Thanksgiving for Deliverance
**v1** Give thanks to the LORD, for He is good; His loving devotion endures forever.
**v2** Let the redeemed of the LORD say so, whom He has redeemed from the hand of the enemy
**v3** and gathered from the lands, from east and west, from north and south. [^1]

**v4** Some wandered in desert wastelands, finding no path to a city in which to dwell.
**v5** They were hungry and thirsty; their soul fainted within them.
**v6** Then they cried out to the LORD in their trouble, and He delivered them from their distress.
**v7** He led them on a straight pathto reach a city where they could live.
**v8** Let them give thanks to the LORD for His loving devotionand His wonders to the sons of men.
**v9** For He satisfies the thirstyand fills the hungry with good things.

**v10** Some sat in darkness and in the shadow of death, prisoners in affliction and chains,
**v11** because they rebelled against the words of Godand despised the counsel of the Most High.
**v12** He humbled their hearts with hard labor; they stumbled, and there was no one to help.
**v13** Then they cried out to the LORD in their trouble, and He saved them from their distress.
**v14** He brought them out of darkness and the shadow of deathand broke away their chains.
**v15** Let them give thanks to the LORD for His loving devotionand His wonders to the sons of men.
**v16** For He has broken down the gates of bronzeand cut through the bars of iron.

**v17** Fools, in their rebellious ways, and through their iniquities, suffered affliction.
**v18** They loathed all foodand drew near to the gates of death.
**v19** Then they cried out to the LORD in their trouble, and He saved them from their distress.
**v20** He sent forth His word and healed them; He rescued them from the Pit.
**v21** Let them give thanks to the LORD for His loving devotionand His wonders to the sons of men.
**v22** Let them offer sacrifices of thanksgivingand declare His works with rejoicing.

**v23** Others went out to sea in ships, conducting trade on the mighty waters.
**v24** They saw the works of the LORD, and His wonders in the deep.
**v25** For He spoke and raised a tempestthat lifted the waves of the sea.
**v26** They mounted up to the heavens, then sunk to the depths; their courage melted in their anguish.
**v27** They reeled and staggered like drunkards, and all their skill was useless. [^2]

**v28** Then they cried out to the LORD in their trouble, and He brought them out of their distress.
**v29** He calmed the storm to a whisper, and the waves of the sea [^3] were hushed.
**v30** They rejoiced in the silence, and He guided them to the harbor they desired.
**v31** Let them give thanks to the LORD for His loving devotionand His wonders to the sons of men.
**v32** Let them exalt Him in the assembly of the peopleand praise Him in the council of the elders.

**v33** He turns rivers into deserts, springs of water into thirsty ground,
**v34** and fruitful land into fields of salt, because of the wickedness of its dwellers.
**v35** He turns a desert into pools of waterand a dry land into flowing springs.
**v36** He causes the hungry to settle there, that they may establish a city in which to dwell.
**v37** They sow fields and plant vineyardsthat yield a fruitful harvest.
**v38** He blesses them, and they multiply greatly; He does not let their herds diminish.

**v39** When they are decreased and humbledby oppression, evil, and sorrow,
**v40** He pours out contempt on the noblesand makes them wander in a trackless wasteland.
**v41** But He lifts the needy from afflictionand increases their families like flocks.
**v42** The upright see and rejoice, and all iniquity shuts its mouth.

**v43** Let him who is wise pay heed to these thingsand consider the loving devotion of the LORD.
[^1]: Hebrew north and the sea ( 107:3)
[^2]: Or and all their wisdom was swallowed up or and they were at their wits' end ( 107:27)
[^3]: DSS; MT their waves ( 107:29)

### Chapter 108

#### Israel's Kingdom Blessing

**v1** My heart is steadfast, O God; I will sing and make music with all my being. [^1]
**v2** Awake, O harp and lyre!I will awaken the dawn.
**v3** I will praise You, O LORD, among the nations; I will sing Your praises among the peoples.
**v4** For Your loving devotion extends beyond the heavens, and Your faithfulness reaches to the clouds.
**v5** Be exalted, O God, above the heavens; may Your glory cover all the earth.
**v6** Respond and save us with Your right hand, that Your beloved may be delivered.

**v7** God has spoken from His sanctuary: [^2]"I will triumph!I will parcel out Shechemand apportion the Valley of Succoth.
**v8** Gilead is Mine, and Manasseh is Mine; Ephraim is My helmet, Judah is My scepter.
**v9** Moab is My washbasin; upon Edom I toss My sandal; over Philistia I shout in triumph."

**v10** Who will bring me to the fortified city?Who will lead me to Edom?
**v11** Have You not rejected us, O God?Will You no longer march out, O God, with our armies?
**v12** Give us aid against the enemy, for the help of man is worthless.
**v13** With God we will perform with valor, and He will trample our enemies.
[^1]: Or with my glory ( 108:1)
[^2]: Or in His holiness ( 108:7)

### Chapter 109

#### The Song of the Slandered

**v1** O God of my praise, be not silent.
**v2** For wicked and deceitful mouths open against me; they speak against me with lying tongues.
**v3** They surround me with hateful wordsand attack me without cause.
**v4** In return for my love they accuse me, but I am a man of prayer.
**v5** They repay me evil for good, and hatred for my love.

**v6** Set over him a wicked man; let an accuser stand at his right hand.
**v7** When he is tried, let him be found guilty, and may his prayer be regarded as sin.
**v8** May his days be few; may another take his position. [^1]
**v9** May his children be fatherlessand his wife a widow.
**v10** May his children wander as beggars, seeking sustenance [^2] far from their ruined homes.
**v11** May the creditor seize all he owns, and strangers plunder the fruits of his labor.
**v12** May there be no one to extend kindness to him, and no one to favor his fatherless children.
**v13** May his descendants be cut off; may their name be blotted out from the next generation.
**v14** May the iniquity of his fathers be remembered before the LORD, and the sin of his mother never be blotted out.
**v15** May their sins always remain before the LORD, that He may cut off their memory from the earth.

**v16** For he never thought to show kindness, but pursued the poor and needy and brokenhearted, even to their death.
**v17** The cursing that he loved, may it fall on him; the blessing in which he refused to delight, may it be far from him.
**v18** The cursing that he wore like a coat, may it soak into his body like water, and into his bones like oil.
**v19** May it be like a robe wrapped about him, like a belt tied forever around him.
**v20** May this be the LORD's reward to my accusers, to those who speak evil against me.

**v21** But You, O GOD, the Lord, deal kindly with me for the sake of Your name; deliver me by the goodness of Your loving devotion.
**v22** For I am poor and needy; my heart is wounded within me.
**v23** I am fading away like a lengthening shadow; I am shaken off like a locust.
**v24** My knees are weak from fasting, and my body grows lean and gaunt.
**v25** I am an object of scorn to my accusers; when they see me, they shake their heads.

**v26** Help me, O LORD my God; save me according to Your loving devotion.
**v27** Let them know that this is Your hand, that You, O LORD, have done it.
**v28** Though they curse, You will bless.When they rise up, they will be put to shame, but Your servant will rejoice.
**v29** May my accusers be clothed with disgrace; may they wear their shame like a robe.
**v30** With my mouth I will thank the LORD profusely; I will praise Him in the presence of many.
**v31** For He stands at the right hand of the needy one, to save him from the condemners of his soul.
[^1]: Cited in Acts 1:20 ( 109:8)
[^2]: Hebrew; LXX may they be driven ( 109:10)

### Chapter 110

#### God's Faithful Messiah

**v1** The LORD said to my Lord: "Sit at My right handuntil I make Your enemiesa footstool for Your feet."[^1]

**v2** The LORD extends Your mighty scepter from Zion: "Rule in the midst of Your enemies."
**v3** Your people shall be willingon Your day of battle.Arrayed in holy splendor, from the womb of the dawn, to You belongs the dew of Your youth.

**v4** The LORD has swornand will not change His mind: "You are a priest foreverin the order of Melchizedek."[^2]

**v5** The Lord is at Your right hand; He will crush kings in the day of His wrath.
**v6** He will judge the nations, heaping up the dead; He will crush the leaders far and wide.
**v7** He will drink from the brook by the road; therefore He will lift up His head.
[^1]: Cited in Matthew 22:44, Mark 12:36, Luke 20:42–43, Acts 2:34–35, and Hebrews 1:13 ( 110:1)
[^2]: Cited in Hebrews 5:6, Hebrews 7:17, and Hebrews 7:21 ( 110:4)

### Chapter 111

#### Majestic Is His Work
**v1** Hallelujah! [^1] I will give thanks to the LORD with all my heartin the council of the upright and in the assembly.

**v2** Great are the works of the LORD; they are pondered by all who delight in them.
**v3** Splendid and majestic is His work; His righteousness endures forever.
**v4** He has caused His wonders to be remembered; the LORD is gracious and compassionate.
**v5** He provides food for those who fear Him; He remembers His covenant forever.

**v6** He has shown His people the power of His worksby giving them the inheritance of the nations.
**v7** The works of His hands are truth and justice; all His precepts are trustworthy.
**v8** They are upheld forever and ever, enacted in truth and uprightness.
**v9** He has sent redemption to His people; He has ordained His covenant forever; holy and awesome is His name.

**v10** The fear of the LORD is the beginning of wisdom; all who follow His precepts gain rich understanding.His praise endures forever!
[^1]: Or Hallelu YAH, meaning Praise the LORD. This psalm is an acrostic poem, each line beginning with the successive letters of the Hebrew alphabet. ( 111:1)

### Chapter 112

#### The Blessed Fear of the LORD
**v1** Hallelujah! [^1] Blessed is the man who fears the LORD, who greatly delights in His commandments.
**v2** His descendants will be mighty in the land; the generation of the upright will be blessed.
**v3** Wealth and riches are in his house, and his righteousness endures forever.
**v4** Light dawns in the darkness for the upright—for the gracious, compassionate, and righteous.

**v5** It is well with the man who is generous and lends freely, whose affairs are guided by justice.
**v6** Surely he will never be shaken; the righteous man will be remembered forever.
**v7** He does not fear bad news; his heart is steadfast, trusting in the LORD.
**v8** His heart is assured; he does not fear, until he looks in triumph on his foes.
**v9** He has scattered abroad his gifts to the poor; his righteousness endures forever; [^2] his horn will be lifted high in honor.

**v10** The wicked man will see and be grieved; he will gnash his teeth and waste away; the desires of the wicked will perish.
[^1]: Or Hallelu YAH, meaning Praise the LORD. This psalm is an acrostic poem, each line beginning with the successive letters of the Hebrew alphabet. ( 112:1)
[^2]: Cited in 2 Corinthians 9:9 ( 112:9)

### Chapter 113

#### The LORD Exalts the Humble
**v1** Hallelujah! [^1] Give praise, O servants of the LORD; praise the name of the LORD.
**v2** Blessed be the name of the LORDboth now and forevermore.
**v3** From where the sun rises to where it sets, the name of the LORD is praised.

**v4** The LORD is exalted over all the nations, His glory above the heavens.
**v5** Who is like the LORD our God, the One enthroned on high?
**v6** He humbles Himself to beholdthe heavens and the earth.

**v7** He raises the poor from the dustand lifts the needy from the dump
**v8** to seat them with nobles, with the princes of His people.
**v9** He settles the barren woman in her homeas a joyful mother to her children.Hallelujah!
[^1]: Or Hallelu YAH, meaning Praise the LORD; also in verse 9 ( 113:1)

### Chapter 114

#### A Psalm of Exodus
**v1** When Israel departed from Egypt, the house of Jacob from a people of foreign tongue,
**v2** Judah became God's sanctuary, Israel His dominion.

**v3** The sea observed and fled; the Jordan turned back;
**v4** the mountains skipped like rams, the hills like lambs.
**v5** Why was it, O sea, that you fled, O Jordan, that you turned back,
**v6** O mountains, that you skipped like rams, O hills, like lambs?

**v7** Tremble, O earth, at the presence of the Lord, at the presence of the God of Jacob,
**v8** who turned the rock into a pool, the flint into a fountain of water!
### Chapter 115

#### To Your Name Be the Glory
**v1** Not to us, O LORD, not to us, but to Your name be the glory, because of Your loving devotion, because of Your faithfulness.

**v2** Why should the nations say,"Where is their God?"

**v3** Our God is in heaven; He does as He pleases.

**v4** Their idols are silver and gold, made by the hands of men.
**v5** They have mouths, but cannot speak; they have eyes, but cannot see;
**v6** they have ears, but cannot hear; they have noses, but cannot smell;
**v7** they have hands, but cannot feel; they have feet, but cannot walk; they cannot even clear their throats. [^1]
**v8** Those who make them become like them, as do all who trust in them.

**v9** O Israel, [^2] trust in the LORD!He is their help and shield.
**v10** O house of Aaron, trust in the LORD!He is their help and shield.
**v11** You who fear the LORD, trust in the LORD!He is their help and shield.
**v12** The LORD is mindful of us; He will bless us.He will bless the house of Israel; He will bless the house of Aaron;
**v13** He will bless those who fear the LORD—small and great alike.

**v14** May the LORD give you increase, both you and your children.
**v15** May you be blessed by the LORD, the Maker of heaven and earth.

**v16** The highest heavens belong to the LORD, but the earth He has given to mankind.
**v17** It is not the dead who praise the LORD, nor any who descend into silence.
**v18** But it is we who will bless the LORD, both now and forevermore.Hallelujah! [^3]
[^1]: Literally they cannot utter with their throat ( 115:7)
[^2]: MT; many Hebrew manuscripts, LXX, and Syriac O house of Israel ( 115:9)
[^3]: Or Hallelu YAH, meaning Praise the LORD ( 115:18)

### Chapter 116

#### The LORD Has Heard My Voice
**v1** I love the LORD, for He has heard my voice—my appeal for mercy.
**v2** Because He has inclined His ear to me, I will call on Him as long as I live.

**v3** The ropes of death entangled me; the anguish of Sheol overcame me; I was confronted by trouble and sorrow.
**v4** Then I called on the name of the LORD: "O LORD, deliver my soul!"

**v5** The LORD is gracious and righteous; our God is full of compassion.
**v6** The LORD preserves the simplehearted; I was helpless, and He saved me.
**v7** Return to your rest, O my soul, for the LORD has been good to you.
**v8** For You have delivered my soul from death, my eyes from tears, my feet from stumbling.

**v9** I will walk before the LORDin the land of the living.
**v10** I believed, therefore I said, [^1]"I am greatly afflicted."
**v11** In my alarm I said,"All men are liars!"

**v12** How can I repay the LORDfor all His goodness to me?
**v13** I will lift the cup of salvationand call on the name of the LORD.
**v14** I will fulfill my vows to the LORDin the presence of all His people.

**v15** Precious in the sight of the LORDis the death of His saints.
**v16** Truly, O LORD, I am Your servant; I am Your servant, the son of Your maidservant; You have broken my bonds.

**v17** I will offer to You a sacrifice of thanksgivingand call on the name of the LORD.
**v18** I will fulfill my vows to the LORDin the presence of all His people,
**v19** in the courts of the LORD's house, in your midst, O Jerusalem.Hallelujah! [^2]
[^1]: LXX therefore I have spoken; cited in 2 Corinthians 4:13 ( 116:10)
[^2]: Or Hallelu YAH, meaning Praise the LORD ( 116:19)

### Chapter 117

#### Extol Him, All You Peoples
**v1** Praise the LORD, all you nations!Extol Him, all you peoples! [^1]
**v2** For great is His loving devotion toward us, and the faithfulness of the LORD endures forever.Hallelujah! [^2]
[^1]: Cited in Romans 15:11 ( 117:1)
[^2]: Or Hallelu YAH, meaning Praise the LORD ( 117:2)

### Chapter 118

#### The LORD Is on My Side
**v1** Give thanks to the LORD, for He is good; His loving devotion endures forever.
**v2** Let Israel [^1] say,"His loving devotion endures forever."
**v3** Let the house of Aaron say,"His loving devotion endures forever."
**v4** Let those who fear the LORD say,"His loving devotion endures forever."

**v5** In my distress I called to the LORD, and He answered and set me free.
**v6** The LORD is on my side; [^2] I will not be afraid.What can man do to me? [^3]
**v7** The LORD is on my side; He is my helper.Therefore I will look in triumph on those who hate me.
**v8** It is better to take refuge in the LORDthan to trust in man.
**v9** It is better to take refuge in the LORDthan to trust in princes.

**v10** All the nations surrounded me, but in the name of the LORD I cut them off.
**v11** They surrounded me on every side, but in the name of the LORD I cut them off.
**v12** They swarmed around me like bees, but they were extinguished like burning thorns; in the name of the LORD I cut them off.
**v13** I was pushed so hard I was falling, but the LORD helped me.
**v14** The LORD is my strength and my song, and He has become my salvation.

**v15** Shouts of joy and salvation resound in the tents of the righteous: "The right hand of the LORD performs with valor!
**v16** The right hand of the LORD is exalted!The right hand of the LORD performs with valor!"
**v17** I will not die, but I will liveand proclaim what the LORD has done.
**v18** The LORD disciplined me severely, but He has not given me over to death.

**v19** Open to me the gates of righteousness, that I may enter and give thanks to the LORD.
**v20** This is the gate of the LORD; the righteous shall enter through it.
**v21** I will give You thanks, for You have answered me, and You have become my salvation.
**v22** The stone the builders rejectedhas become the cornerstone. [^4]
**v23** This is from the LORD, and it is marvelous in our eyes. [^5]
**v24** This is the day that the LORD has made; we will rejoice and be glad in it.

**v25** O LORD, save us, we pray. [^6] We beseech You, O LORD, cause us to prosper!

**v26** Blessed is he who comes in the name of the LORD. [^7] From the house of the LORD we bless you.
**v27** The LORD is God; He has made His light to shine upon us.Bind the festal sacrifice with cordsto the horns of the altar. [^8]
**v28** You are my God, and I will give You thanks.You are my God, and I will exalt You.
**v29** Give thanks to the LORD, for He is good; His loving devotion endures forever.
[^1]: LXX the house of Israel ( 118:2)
[^2]: Or The LORD is with me; also in verse 7; LXX The Lord is my helper ( 118:6)
[^3]: Cited in Hebrews 13:6 ( 118:6)
[^4]: Hebrew the head of the corner; cited in Matthew 21:42, Mark 12:10, Luke 20:17, Acts 4:11, and 1 Peter 2:7 ( 118:22)
[^5]: Cited in Matthew 21:42 and Mark 12:11 ( 118:23)
[^6]: Hebrew hosia-na, meaning save, we pray or save now; see Matthew 21:9, Matthew 21:15, Mark 11:9, and John 12:13. ( 118:25)
[^7]: Cited in Matthew 21:9, Matthew 23:39, Mark 11:9, Luke 13:35, Luke 19:38, and John 12:13 ( 118:26)
[^8]: Or Join in the festal procession with boughs in hand, up to the horns of the altar. ( 118:27)

### Chapter 119

#### Your Word Is a Lamp to My Feet
**v1** Blessed [^1] are those whose way is blameless, who walk in the Law of the LORD.
**v2** Blessed are those who keep His testimoniesand seek Him with all their heart.
**v3** They do no iniquity; they walk in His ways.
**v4** You have ordained Your precepts, that we should keep them diligently.
**v5** Oh, that my ways were committedto keeping Your statutes!
**v6** Then I would not be ashamedwhen I consider all Your commandments.
**v7** I will praise You with an upright heartwhen I learn Your righteous judgments.
**v8** I will keep Your statutes; do not utterly forsake me.


**v9** How can a young man keep his way pure?By guarding it according to Your word.
**v10** With all my heart I have sought You; do not let me stray from Your commandments.
**v11** I have hidden Your word in my heartthat I might not sin against You.
**v12** Blessed are You, O LORD; teach me Your statutes.
**v13** With my lips I proclaimall the judgments of Your mouth.
**v14** I rejoice in the way of Your testimoniesas much as in all riches.
**v15** I will meditate on Your preceptsand regard Your ways.
**v16** I will delight in Your statutes; I will not forget Your word.


**v17** Deal bountifully with Your servant, that I may live and keep Your word.
**v18** Open my eyes that I may seewondrous things from Your law.
**v19** I am a stranger on the earth; do not hide Your commandments from me.
**v20** My soul is consumed with longingfor Your judgments at all times.
**v21** You rebuke the arrogant—the cursed who stray from Your commandments.
**v22** Remove my scorn and contempt, for I have kept Your testimonies.
**v23** Though rulers sit and slander me, Your servant meditates on Your statutes.
**v24** Your testimonies are indeed my delight; they are my counselors.


**v25** My soul cleaves to the dust; revive me according to Your word.
**v26** I recounted my ways, and You answered me; teach me Your statutes.
**v27** Make clear to me the way of Your precepts; then I will meditate on Your wonders.
**v28** My soul melts with sorrow; strengthen me according to Your word.
**v29** Remove me from the path of deceitand graciously grant me Your law.
**v30** I have chosen the way of truth; I have set Your ordinances before me.
**v31** I cling to Your testimonies, O LORD; let me not be put to shame.
**v32** I run in the path of Your commandments, for You will enlarge my heart.


**v33** Teach me, O LORD, the way of Your statutes, and I will keep them to the end. [^2]
**v34** Give me understanding that I may obey Your law, and follow it with all my heart.
**v35** Direct me in the path of Your commandments, for there I find delight.
**v36** Turn my heart to Your testimoniesand not to covetous gain.
**v37** Turn my eyes away from worthless things; revive me with Your word. [^3]
**v38** Establish Your word to Your servant, to produce reverence for You.
**v39** Turn away the disgrace I dread, for Your judgments are good.
**v40** How I long for Your precepts!Revive me in Your righteousness.


**v41** May Your loving devotion come to me, O LORD, Your salvation, according to Your promise.
**v42** Then I can answer him who taunts, for I trust in Your word.
**v43** Never take Your word of truth from my mouth, for I hope in Your judgments.
**v44** I will always obey Your law, forever and ever.
**v45** And I will walk in freedom, for I have sought Your precepts.
**v46** I will speak of Your testimonies before kings, and I will not be ashamed.
**v47** I delight in Your commandmentsbecause I love them.
**v48** I lift up my hands to Your commandments, which I love, and I meditate on Your statutes.


**v49** Remember Your word to Your servant, upon which You have given me hope.
**v50** This is my comfort in affliction, that Your promise has given me life.
**v51** The arrogant utterly deride me, but I do not turn from Your law.
**v52** I remember Your judgments of old, O LORD, and in them I find comfort.
**v53** Rage has taken hold of mebecause of the wicked who reject Your law.
**v54** Your statutes are songs to mein the house of my pilgrimage.
**v55** In the night, O LORD, I remember Your name, that I may keep Your law.
**v56** This is my practice, for I obey Your precepts.


**v57** The LORD is my portion; I have promised to keep Your words.
**v58** I have sought Your face with all my heart; be gracious to me according to Your promise.
**v59** I considered my waysand turned my steps to Your testimonies.
**v60** I hurried without hesitatingto keep Your commandments.
**v61** Though the ropes of the wicked bind me, I do not forget Your law.
**v62** At midnight I rise to give You thanksfor Your righteous judgments.
**v63** I am a friend to all who fear You, and to those who keep Your precepts.
**v64** The earth is filled with Your loving devotion, O LORD; teach me Your statutes.


**v65** You are good to Your servant, O LORD, according to Your word.
**v66** Teach me good judgment and knowledge, for I believe in Your commandments.
**v67** Before I was afflicted, I went astray; but now I keep Your word.
**v68** You are good, and You do what is good; teach me Your statutes.
**v69** Though the arrogant have smeared me with lies, I keep Your precepts with all my heart.
**v70** Their hearts are callous and insensitive, [^4] but I delight in Your law.
**v71** It was good for me to be afflicted, that I might learn Your statutes.
**v72** The law from Your mouth is more precious to methan thousands of pieces of gold and silver.


**v73** Your hands have made me and fashioned me; give me understanding to learn Your commandments.
**v74** May those who fear You see me and rejoice, for I have hoped in Your word.
**v75** I know, O LORD, that Your judgments are righteous, and that in faithfulness You have afflicted me.
**v76** May Your loving devotion comfort me, I pray, according to Your promise to Your servant.
**v77** May Your compassion come to me, that I may live, for Your law is my delight.
**v78** May the arrogant be put to shame for subverting me with a lie; I will meditate on Your precepts.
**v79** May those who fear You turn to me, those who know Your testimonies.
**v80** May my heart be blameless in Your statutes, that I may not be put to shame.


**v81** My soul faints for Your salvation; I wait for Your word.
**v82** My eyes fail, looking for Your promise; I ask, "When will You comfort me?"
**v83** Though I am like a wineskin dried up by smoke, I do not forget Your statutes.
**v84** How many days must Your servant wait? [^5] When will You execute judgment on my persecutors?
**v85** The arrogant have dug pits for mein violation of Your law.
**v86** All Your commandments are faithful; I am persecuted without cause—help me!
**v87** They almost wiped me from the earth, but I have not forsaken Your precepts.
**v88** Revive me according to Your loving devotion, that I may obey the testimony of Your mouth.


**v89** Your word, O LORD, is everlasting; it is firmly fixed in the heavens.
**v90** Your faithfulness continues through all generations; You established the earth, and it endures.
**v91** Your ordinances stand to this day, [^6] for all things are servants to You.
**v92** If Your law had not been my delight, then I would have perished in my affliction.
**v93** I will never forget Your precepts, for by them You have revived me.
**v94** I am Yours; save me, for I have sought Your precepts.
**v95** The wicked wait to destroy me, but I will ponder Your testimonies.
**v96** I have seen a limit to all perfection, but Your commandment is without limit.


**v97** Oh, how I love Your law!All day long it is my meditation.
**v98** Your commandments make me wiser than my enemies, for they are always with me.
**v99** I have more insight than all my teachers, for Your testimonies are my meditation.
**v100** I discern more than the elders, for I obey Your precepts.
**v101** I have kept my feet from every evil path, that I may keep Your word.
**v102** I have not departed from Your ordinances, for You Yourself have taught me.
**v103** How sweet are Your words to my taste—sweeter than honey in my mouth!
**v104** I gain understanding from Your precepts; therefore I hate every false way.


**v105** Your word is a lamp to my feetand a light to my path.
**v106** I have sworn and confirmedthat I will keep Your righteous judgments.
**v107** I am severely afflicted, O LORD; revive me through Your word.
**v108** Accept the freewill offerings of my mouth, O LORD, and teach me Your judgments.
**v109** I constantly take my life in my hands, yet I do not forget Your law.
**v110** The wicked have set a snare for me, but I have not strayed from Your precepts.
**v111** Your testimonies are my heritage forever, for they are the joy of my heart.
**v112** I have inclined my heart to perform Your statutes, even to the very end.


**v113** The double-minded I despise, but Your law I love.
**v114** You are my hiding place and my shield; I put my hope in Your word.
**v115** Depart from me, you evildoers, that I may obey the commandments of my God.
**v116** Sustain me as You promised, that I may live; let me not be ashamed of my hope.
**v117** Uphold me, and I will be saved, that I may always regard Your statutes.
**v118** You reject all who stray from Your statutes, for their deceitfulness is in vain.
**v119** All the wicked on earth You discard like dross; therefore I love Your testimonies.
**v120** My flesh trembles in awe of You; I stand in fear of Your judgments.


**v121** I have done what is just and right; do not leave me to my oppressors.
**v122** Ensure Your servant's well-being; do not let the arrogant oppress me.
**v123** My eyes fail, looking for Your salvation, and for Your righteous promise.
**v124** Deal with Your servant according to Your loving devotion, and teach me Your statutes.
**v125** I am Your servant; give me understanding, that I may know Your testimonies.
**v126** It is time for the LORD to act, for they have broken Your law.
**v127** Therefore I love Your commandments more than gold, even the purest gold.
**v128** Therefore I admire all Your preceptsand hate every false way.


**v129** Wonderful are Your testimonies; therefore I obey them.
**v130** The unfolding of Your words gives light; it informs the simple.
**v131** I open my mouth and pant, longing for Your commandments.
**v132** Turn to me and show me mercy, as You do to those who love Your name.
**v133** Order my steps in Your word; let no sin rule over me.
**v134** Redeem me from the oppression of man, that I may keep Your precepts.
**v135** Make Your face shine upon Your servant, and teach me Your statutes.
**v136** My eyes shed streams of tearsbecause Your law is not obeyed.


**v137** Righteous are You, O LORD, and upright are Your judgments.
**v138** The testimonies You have laid down are righteousand altogether faithful.
**v139** My zeal has consumed mebecause my foes forget Your words.
**v140** Your promise is completely pure; therefore Your servant loves it.
**v141** I am lowly and despised, but I do not forget Your precepts.
**v142** Your righteousness is everlastingand Your law is true.
**v143** Trouble and distress have found me, but Your commandments are my delight.
**v144** Your testimonies are righteous forever.Give me understanding, that I may live.


**v145** I call with all my heart; answer me, O LORD!I will obey Your statutes.
**v146** I call to You; save me, that I may keep Your testimonies.
**v147** I rise before dawn and cry for help; in Your word I have put my hope.
**v148** My eyes anticipate the watches of night, that I may meditate on Your word.
**v149** Hear my voice, O LORD, according to Your loving devotion; give me life according to Your justice.
**v150** Those who follow after wickedness draw near; they are far from Your law.
**v151** You are near, O LORD, and all Your commandments are true.
**v152** Long ago I learned from Your testimoniesthat You have established them forever.


**v153** Look upon my affliction and rescue me, for I have not forgotten Your law.
**v154** Defend my cause and redeem me; revive me according to Your word.
**v155** Salvation is far from the wickedbecause they do not seek Your statutes.
**v156** Great are Your mercies, O LORD; revive me according to Your ordinances.
**v157** Though my persecutors and foes are many, I have not turned from Your testimonies.
**v158** I look on the faithless with loathingbecause they do not keep Your word.
**v159** Consider how I love Your precepts, O LORD; give me life according to Your loving devotion.
**v160** The entirety of Your word is truth, and all Your righteous judgments endure forever.


**v161** Rulers persecute me without cause, but my heart fears only Your word.
**v162** I rejoice in Your promiselike one who finds great spoil.
**v163** I hate and abhor falsehood, but Your law I love.
**v164** Seven times a day I praise Youfor Your righteous judgments.
**v165** Abundant peace belongs to those who love Your law; nothing can make them stumble.
**v166** I wait for Your salvation, O LORD, and I carry out Your commandments.
**v167** I obey Your testimoniesand love them greatly.
**v168** I obey Your precepts and Your testimonies, for all my ways are before You.


**v169** May my cry come before You, O LORD; give me understanding according to Your word.
**v170** May my plea come before You; rescue me according to Your promise.
**v171** My lips pour forth praise, for You teach me Your statutes.
**v172** My tongue sings of Your word, for all Your commandments are righteous.
**v173** May Your hand be ready to help me, for I have chosen Your precepts.
**v174** I long for Your salvation, O LORD, and Your law is my delight.
**v175** Let me live to praise You; may Your judgments sustain me.
**v176** I have strayed like a lost sheep; seek Your servant, for I have not forgotten Your commandments.
