[^1]: This psalm is an acrostic poem of twenty-two stanzas, following the letters of the Hebrew alphabet; within a stanza, each verse begins with the same Hebrew letter. ( 119:1)
[^2]: Or keep them as my reward ( 119:33)
[^3]: Two MT manuscripts and DSS; most MT manuscripts in Your way ( 119:37)
[^4]: Or fat ( 119:70)
[^5]: Or How many are the days of Your servant? ( 119:84)
[^6]: Or They stand this day according to Your ordinances ( 119:91)

### Chapter 120

#### In My Distress I Cried to the LORD

**v1** In my distress I cried to the LORD, and He answered me.
**v2** Deliver my soul, O LORD, from lying lips and a deceitful tongue.

**v3** What will He do to you, and what will be added to you, O deceitful tongue?
**v4** Sharp arrows will come from the warrior, with burning coals of the broom tree!

**v5** Woe to me that I dwell in Meshech, that I live among the tents of Kedar!
**v6** Too long have I dweltamong those who hate peace.
**v7** I am in favor of peace; but when I speak, they want war.
### Chapter 121

#### I Lift Up My Eyes to the Hills

**v1** I lift up my eyes to the hills.From where does my help come?
**v2** My help comes from the LORD, the Maker of heaven and earth.

**v3** He will not allow your foot to slip; your Protector will not slumber.
**v4** Behold, the Protector of Israelwill neither slumber nor sleep.

**v5** The LORD is your keeper; the LORD is the shade on your right hand.
**v6** The sun will not strike you by day, nor the moon by night.

**v7** The LORD will guard you from all evil; He will preserve your soul.
**v8** The LORD will watch over your coming and going, both now and forevermore.
### Chapter 122

#### Pray for the Peace of Jerusalem

**v1** I was glad when they said to me,"Let us go to the house of the LORD."
**v2** Our feet are standing in your gates, O Jerusalem.

**v3** Jerusalem is built upas a city united together,
**v4** where the tribes go up, the tribes of the LORD, as a testimony for Israel, to give thanks to the name of the LORD.
**v5** For there the thrones of judgment stand, the thrones of the house of David.

**v6** Pray for the peace of Jerusalem: "May those who love you prosper. [^1]
**v7** May there be peace within your walls, and prosperity [^2] inside your fortresses."
**v8** For the sake of my brothers and friends, I will say, "Peace be within you."
**v9** For the sake of the house of the LORD our God, I will seek your prosperity.
[^1]: Or be secure ( 122:6)
[^2]: Or security ( 122:7)

### Chapter 123

#### I Lift Up My Eyes to You

**v1** I lift up my eyes to You, the One enthroned in heaven.
**v2** As the eyes of servantslook to the hand of their master, as the eyes of a maidservantlook to the hand of her mistress, so our eyes are on the LORD our Goduntil He shows us mercy.

**v3** Have mercy on us, O LORD, have mercy, for we have endured much contempt.
**v4** We have endured much scorn from the arrogant, much contempt from the proud.
### Chapter 124

#### Our Help Is in the Name of the LORD

**v1** If the LORD had not been on our side—let Israel now declare—
**v2** if the LORD had not been on our sidewhen men attacked us,
**v3** when their anger flared against us, then they would have swallowed us alive,
**v4** then the floods would have engulfed us, then the torrent would have overwhelmed us,
**v5** then the raging waterswould have swept us away.

**v6** Blessed be the LORD, who has not given us as prey to their teeth.
**v7** We have escaped like a bird from the snare of the fowler; the net is torn, and we have slipped away.
**v8** Our help is in the name of the LORD, the Maker of heaven and earth.
### Chapter 125

#### The LORD Surrounds His People

**v1** Those who trust in the LORD are like Mount Zion.It cannot be moved; it abides forever.
**v2** As the mountains surround Jerusalem, so the LORD surrounds His people, both now and forevermore.

**v3** For the scepter of the wicked will not restupon the land allotted to the righteous, so that the righteous will not put forththeir hands to injustice.

**v4** Do good, O LORD, to those who are good, and to the upright in heart.
**v5** But those who turn to crooked waysthe LORD will banish with the evildoers.Peace be upon Israel.
### Chapter 126

#### Zion's Captives Restored

**v1** When the LORD restored the captives of Zion, [^1] we were like dreamers. [^2]
**v2** Then our mouths were filled with laughter, our tongues with shouts of joy.Then it was said among the nations,"The LORD has done great things for them."
**v3** The LORD has done great things for us; we are filled with joy.

**v4** Restore our captives, [^3] O LORD, like streams in the Negev.
**v5** Those who sow in tearswill reap with shouts of joy.
**v6** He who goes out weeping, bearing a trail of seed, will surely return with shouts of joy, carrying sheaves of grain.
[^1]: Or brought back the captives to Zion or restored the fortunes of Zion ( 126:1)
[^2]: Or like those restored to health ( 126:1)
[^3]: Or Restore our fortunes ( 126:4)

### Chapter 127

#### Children Are a Heritage from the LORD

**v1** Unless the LORD builds the house, its builders labor in vain; unless the LORD protects the city, its watchmen stand guard in vain.
**v2** In vain you rise earlyand stay up late, toiling for bread to eat—for He gives sleep to His beloved.

**v3** Children are indeed a heritage from the LORD, and the fruit of the womb is His reward.
**v4** Like arrows in the hand of a warrior, so are children born in one's youth.
**v5** Blessed is the manwhose quiver is full of them.He will not be put to shamewhen he confronts the enemies at the gate.
### Chapter 128

#### The Blessed Fear of the LORD

**v1** Blessed are all who fear the LORD, who walk in His ways!
**v2** For when you eat the fruit of your labor, blessings and prosperity will be yours.
**v3** Your wife will be like a fruitful vineflourishing within your house, your sons like olive shootssitting around your table.
**v4** In this way indeed shall blessing cometo the man who fears the LORD.

**v5** May the LORD bless you from Zion, that you may see the prosperity of Jerusalemall the days of your life,
**v6** that you may seeyour children's children.Peace be upon Israel!
### Chapter 129

#### The Cords of the Wicked

**v1** Many a time they have persecuted me from my youth—let Israel now declare—
**v2** many a time they have persecuted me from my youth, but they have not prevailed against me.
**v3** The plowmen plowed over my back; they made their furrows long.
**v4** The LORD is righteous; He has cut me from the cords of the wicked.

**v5** May all who hate Zionbe turned back in shame.
**v6** May they be like grass on the rooftops, which withers before it can grow,
**v7** unable to fill the hands of the reaper, or the arms of the binder of sheaves.
**v8** May none who pass by say to them,"The blessing of the LORD be on you; we bless you in the name of the LORD."
### Chapter 130

#### Out of the Depths

**v1** Out of the depths I cry to You, O LORD!
**v2** O Lord, hear my voice; let Your ears be attentive to my plea for mercy.

**v3** If You, O LORD, kept track of iniquities, then who, O Lord, could stand?
**v4** But with You there is forgiveness, so that You may be feared.

**v5** I wait for the LORD; my soul does wait, and in His word I put my hope.
**v6** My soul waits for the Lordmore than watchmen wait for the morning—more than watchmen wait for the morning.

**v7** O Israel, put your hope in the LORD, for with the LORD is loving devotion, and with Him is redemption in abundance.
**v8** And He will redeem Israelfrom all iniquity.
### Chapter 131

#### I Have Stilled My Soul

**v1** My heart is not proud, O LORD, my eyes are not haughty.I do not aspire to great thingsor matters too lofty for me.
**v2** Surely I have stilled and quieted my soul; like a weaned child with his mother, like a weaned child is my soul within me.

**v3** O Israel, put your hope in the LORD, both now and forevermore.
### Chapter 132

#### The LORD Has Chosen Zion

**v1** O LORD, remember on behalf of Davidall the hardships he endured,
**v2** how he swore an oath to the LORD, and vowed to the Mighty One of Jacob:
**v3** "I will not enter my houseor get into my bed,
**v4** I will not give sleep to my eyesor slumber to my eyelids,
**v5** until I find a place for the LORD, a dwelling for the Mighty One of Jacob. [^1]"

**v6** We heard that the ark was in Ephrathah; [^2] we found it in the fields of Jaar.
**v7** Let us go to His dwelling place; let us worship at His footstool.
**v8** Arise, O LORD, to Your resting place, You and the ark of Your strength.
**v9** May Your priests be clothed with righteousness, and Your saints shout for joy.
**v10** For the sake of Your servant David, do not reject Your anointed one.

**v11** The LORD swore an oath to David, a promise He will not revoke: "One of your descendants I will place on your throne. [^3]
**v12** If your sons keep My covenantand the testimony I will teach them, then their sons will also sit on your throneforever and ever."

**v13** For the LORD has chosen Zion; He has desired it for His home:
**v14** "This is My resting place forever and ever; here I will dwell, for I have desired this home.
**v15** I will bless her with abundant provisions; I will satisfy her poor with bread.
**v16** I will clothe her priests with salvation, and her saints will sing out in joy.
**v17** There I will make a horn grow for David; I have prepared a lamp for My anointed one.
**v18** I will clothe his enemies with shame, but the crown upon him will gleam."
[^1]: LXX for the God of Jacob; see Acts 7:46. ( 132:5)
[^2]: Literally Behold, we heard of it in Ephrathah ( 132:6)
[^3]: Literally "From the fruit of your body I will set (one) on your throne. Cited in Acts 2:30 ( 132:11)

### Chapter 133

#### How Pleasant to Live in Harmony!

**v1** Behold, how good and pleasant it iswhen brothers live together in harmony!
**v2** It is like fine oil on the head, running down on the beard, running down Aaron's beardover the collar of his robes.
**v3** It is like the dew of Hermonfalling on the mountains of Zion.For there the LORD has bestowed the blessingof life forevermore.
### Chapter 134

#### Bless the LORD, All You Servants

**v1** Come, bless the LORD, all you servants of the LORDwho serve by nightin the house of the LORD!
**v2** Lift up your hands to the sanctuaryand bless the LORD!

**v3** May the LORD, the Maker of heaven and earth, bless you from Zion.
### Chapter 135

#### Give Praise, O Servants of the LORD
**v1** Hallelujah! [^1] Praise the name of the LORD.Give praise, O servants of the LORD,
**v2** who stand in the house of the LORD, in the courts of the house of our God.
**v3** Hallelujah, for the LORD is good; sing praises to His name, for it is lovely.
**v4** For the LORD has chosen Jacob as His own, Israel as His treasured possession.

**v5** For I know that the LORD is great; our Lord is above all gods.
**v6** The LORD does all that pleases Himin the heavens and on the earth, in the seas and in all their depths.
**v7** He causes the clouds to risefrom the ends of the earth.He generates the lightning with the rainand brings forth the wind from His storehouses.

**v8** He struck down the firstborn of Egypt, of both man and beast.
**v9** He sent signs and wonders into your midst, O Egypt, against Pharaoh and all his servants.
**v10** He struck down many nationsand slaughtered mighty kings:
**v11** Sihon king of the Amorites, Og king of Bashan, and all the kings of Canaan.
**v12** He gave their land as an inheritance, as a heritage to His people Israel.

**v13** Your name, O LORD, endures forever, Your renown, O LORD, through all generations.
**v14** For the LORD will vindicate His people [^2] and will have compassion on His servants.

**v15** The idols of the nations are silver and gold, made by the hands of men.
**v16** They have mouths, but cannot speak; they have eyes, but cannot see;
**v17** they have ears, but cannot hear; nor is there breath in their mouths.
**v18** Those who make them become like them, as do all who trust in them.

**v19** O house of Israel, bless the LORD; O house of Aaron, bless the LORD;
**v20** O house of Levi, bless the LORD; you who fear the LORD, bless the LORD!
**v21** Blessed be the LORD from Zion—He who dwells in Jerusalem.Hallelujah!
[^1]: Or Hallelu YAH, meaning Praise the LORD; also in verses 3 and 21 ( 135:1)
[^2]: Or will judge His people; see also LXX; cited in Hebrews 10:30. ( 135:14)

### Chapter 136

#### His Loving Devotion Endures Forever
**v1** Give thanks to the LORD, for He is good.His loving devotion endures forever.
**v2** Give thanks to the God of gods.His loving devotion endures forever.
**v3** Give thanks to the Lord of lords.His loving devotion endures forever.
**v4** He alone does great wonders.His loving devotion endures forever.
**v5** By His insight He made the heavens.His loving devotion endures forever.
**v6** He spread out the earth upon the waters.His loving devotion endures forever.
**v7** He made the great lights—His loving devotion endures forever.
**v8** the sun to rule the day, His loving devotion endures forever.
**v9** the moon and stars to govern the night.His loving devotion endures forever.
**v10** He struck down the firstborn of Egypt His loving devotion endures forever.
**v11** and brought Israel out from among them His loving devotion endures forever.
**v12** with a mighty hand and an outstretched arm.His loving devotion endures forever.
**v13** He divided the Red Sea [^1] in two His loving devotion endures forever.
**v14** and led Israel through the midst, His loving devotion endures forever.
**v15** but swept [^2] Pharaoh and his army into the Red Sea.His loving devotion endures forever.
**v16** He led His people through the wilderness.His loving devotion endures forever.
**v17** He struck down great kings His loving devotion endures forever.
**v18** and slaughtered mighty kings—His loving devotion endures forever.
**v19** Sihon king of the Amorites His loving devotion endures forever.
**v20** and Og king of Bashan—His loving devotion endures forever.
**v21** and He gave their land as an inheritance, His loving devotion endures forever.
**v22** a heritage to His servant Israel.His loving devotion endures forever.
**v23** He remembered us in our low estate His loving devotion endures forever.
**v24** and freed us from our enemies.His loving devotion endures forever.
**v25** He gives food to every creature.His loving devotion endures forever.
**v26** Give thanks to the God of heaven!His loving devotion endures forever.
[^1]: Or the Sea of Reeds; also in verse 15 ( 136:13)
[^2]: Hebrew shook off ( 136:15)

### Chapter 137

#### By the Rivers of Babylon
**v1** By the rivers of Babylon we sat and weptwhen we remembered Zion.
**v2** There on the willows [^1] we hung our harps,
**v3** for there our captors requested a song; our tormentors demanded songs of joy: "Sing us a song of Zion."

**v4** How can we sing a song of the LORDin a foreign land?
**v5** If I forget you, O Jerusalem, may my right hand cease to function.
**v6** May my tongue cling to the roof of my mouthif I do not remember you, if I do not exalt Jerusalemas my greatest joy!

**v7** Remember, O LORD, the sons of Edom on the day Jerusalem fell: "Destroy it," they said,"tear it down to its foundations!"

**v8** O Daughter of Babylon, doomed to destruction, blessed is he who repays youas you have done to us.
**v9** Blessed is he who seizes your infantsand dashes them against the rocks.
[^1]: Or poplars ( 137:2)

### Chapter 138

#### A Thankful Heart

**v1** I give You thanks with all my heart; before the gods I sing Your praises.
**v2** I bow down toward Your holy templeand give thanks to Your namefor Your loving devotion and Your faithfulness; You have exalted Your nameand Your word above all else.
**v3** On the day I called, You answered me; You emboldened me and strengthened my soul. [^1]

**v4** All the kings of the earth will give You thanks, O LORD, when they hear the words of Your mouth.
**v5** They will sing of the ways of the LORD, for the glory of the LORD is great.
**v6** Though the LORD is on high, He attends to the lowly; but the proud He knows from afar.

**v7** If I walk in the midst of trouble, You preserve me from the anger of my foes; You extend Your hand, and Your right hand saves me.
**v8** The LORD will fulfill His purpose for me.O LORD, Your loving devotion endures forever—do not abandon the works of Your hands.
[^1]: Or You emboldened me with strength in my soul ( 138:3)

### Chapter 139

#### You Have Searched Me and Known Me

**v1** O LORD, You have searched meand known me.
**v2** You know when I sit and when I rise; You understand my thoughts from afar.
**v3** You search out my path and my lying down; You are aware of all my ways.
**v4** Even before a word is on my tongue, You know all about it, O LORD.
**v5** You hem me in behind and before; You have laid Your hand upon me.
**v6** Such knowledge is too wonderful for me, too lofty for me to attain.

**v7** Where can I go to escape Your Spirit?Where can I flee from Your presence?
**v8** If I ascend to the heavens, You are there; if I make my bed in Sheol, You are there.
**v9** If I rise on the wings of the dawn, if I settle by the farthest sea,
**v10** even there Your hand will guide me; Your right hand will hold me fast.
**v11** If I say, "Surely the darkness will hide me, and the light become night around me"—
**v12** even the darkness is not dark to You, but the night shines like the day, for darkness is as light to You.

**v13** For You formed my inmost being; [^1] You knit me together in my mother's womb.
**v14** I praise You, for I am fearfully and wonderfully made.Marvelous are Your works, and I know this very well.
**v15** My frame was not hidden from Youwhen I was made in secret, when I was woven togetherin the depths of the earth.
**v16** Your eyes saw my unformed body; all my days were written in Your bookand ordained for mebefore one of them came to be.

**v17** How precious to me are Your thoughts, [^2] O God, how vast is their sum!
**v18** If I were to count them, they would outnumber the grains of sand; and when I awake, I am still with You.

**v19** O God, that You would slay the wicked—away from me, you bloodthirsty men—
**v20** who speak of You deceitfully; Your enemies take Your name in vain. [^3]
**v21** Do I not hate those who hate You, O LORD, and detest those who rise against You?
**v22** I hate them with perfect hatred; I count them as my enemies.

**v23** Search me, O God, and know my heart; test me and know my concerns.
**v24** See if there is any offensive way in me; lead me in the way everlasting.
[^1]: Hebrew my kidneys ( 139:13)
[^2]: Or How amazing are Your thoughts concerning me ( 139:17)
[^3]: Hebrew Your enemies take in vain or Your enemies bear up in vain; LXX Your enemies take Your cities in vain ( 139:20)

### Chapter 140

#### Rescue Me from Evil Men

**v1** Rescue me, O LORD, from evil men.Protect me from men of violence,
**v2** who devise evil in their heartsand stir up war all day long.
**v3** They sharpen their tongues like snakes; the venom of vipers is on their lips. [^1] Selah
**v4** Guard me, O LORD, from the hands of the wicked.Keep me safe from men of violencewho scheme to make me stumble.
**v5** The proud hide a snare for me; the cords of their net are spread along the path, and lures are set out for me.Selah
**v6** I say to the LORD, "You are my God." Hear, O LORD, my cry for help.
**v7** O GOD the Lord, the strength of my salvation, You shield my head in the day of battle.
**v8** Grant not, O LORD, the desires of the wicked; do not promote their evil plans, lest they be exalted.Selah
**v9** May the heads of those who surround mebe covered in the trouble their lips have caused.
**v10** May burning coals fall on them; may they be thrown into the fire, into the miry pits, never to rise again.
**v11** May no slanderer be established in the land; may calamity hunt down the man of violence.

**v12** I know that the LORD upholds justice for the poorand defends the cause of the needy.
**v13** Surely the righteous will praise Your name; the upright will dwell in Your presence.
[^1]: Cited in Romans 3:13 ( 140:3)

### Chapter 141

#### Come Quickly to Me

**v1** I call upon You, O LORD; come quickly to me.Hear my voice when I call to You.
**v2** May my prayer be set before You like incense; my uplifted hands, like the evening offering.

**v3** Set a guard, O LORD, over my mouth; keep watch at the door of my lips.
**v4** Do not let my heart be drawn to any evil thingor take part in works of wickednesswith men who do iniquity; let me not feast on their delicacies.

**v5** Let the righteous man strike me; let his rebuke be an act of loving devotion.It is oil for my head; let me not refuse it.For my prayer is ever against the deeds of the wicked.
**v6** When their rulers are thrown down from the cliffs, the people will listen to my words, for they are pleasant.
**v7** As when one plows and breaks up the soil, so our bones have been scattered at the mouth of Sheol.

**v8** But my eyes are fixed on You, O GOD the Lord.In You I seek refuge; do not leave my soul defenseless. [^1]
**v9** Keep me from the snares they have laid for me, and from the lures of evildoers.
**v10** Let the wicked fall into their own nets, while I pass by in safety.
[^1]: Or do not pour out my life or do not give me over to death ( 141:8)

### Chapter 142

#### I Lift My Voice to the LORD

**v1** I cry aloud to the LORD; I lift my voice to the LORD for mercy.
**v2** I pour out my complaint before Him; I reveal my trouble to Him.

**v3** Although my spirit grows faint within me, You know my way.Along the path I travelthey have hidden a snare for me.
**v4** Look to my right and see; no one attends to me.There is no refuge for me; no one cares for my soul.

**v5** I cry to You, O LORD: "You are my refuge, my portion in the land of the living."

**v6** Listen to my cry, for I am brought quite low.Rescue me from my pursuers, for they are too strong for me.
**v7** Free my soul from prison, that I may praise Your name.The righteous will gather around mebecause of Your goodness to me.
[^1]: Maskil is probably a musical or liturgical term; used for Psalms 32, 42, 44–45, 52–55, 74, 78, 88–89, and 142. ( 142:0)

### Chapter 143

#### I Stretch Out My Hands to You

**v1** O LORD, hear my prayer.In Your faithfulness, give ear to my plea; in Your righteousness, answer me.
**v2** Do not bring Your servant into judgment, for no one alive is righteous before You.

**v3** For the enemy has pursued my soul, crushing my life to the ground, making me dwell in darknesslike those long since dead.
**v4** My spirit grows faint within me; my heart is dismayed inside me.

**v5** I remember the days of old; I meditate on all Your works; I consider the work of Your hands.
**v6** I stretch out my hands to You; my soul thirsts for You like a parched land.Selah
**v7** Answer me quickly, O LORD; my spirit fails.Do not hide Your face from me, or I will be like those who descend to the Pit.
**v8** Let me hear Your loving devotion in the morning, for I have put my trust in You.Teach me the way I should walk, for to You I lift up my soul.
**v9** Deliver me from my enemies, O LORD; I flee to You for refuge. [^1]
**v10** Teach me to do Your will, for You are my God.May Your good Spirit lead meon level ground.

**v11** For the sake of Your name, O LORD, revive me.In Your righteousness, bring my soul out of trouble.
**v12** And in Your loving devotion, cut off my enemies.Destroy all who afflict me, for I am Your servant.
[^1]: LXX and one Hebrew manuscript; most Hebrew manuscripts in You I take cover ( 143:9)

### Chapter 144

#### Blessed Be the LORD, My Rock

**v1** Blessed be the LORD, my Rock, who trains my hands for war, my fingers for battle.
**v2** He is my steadfast love and my fortress, my stronghold and my deliverer.He is my shield, in whom I take refuge, who subdues peoples [^1] under me.

**v3** O LORD, what is man, that You regard him, the son of man that You think of him?
**v4** Man is like a breath; his days are like a passing shadow.

**v5** Part Your heavens, O LORD, and come down; touch the mountains, that they may smoke.
**v6** Flash forth Your lightning and scatter them; shoot Your arrows and rout them.
**v7** Reach down from on high; set me free and rescue mefrom the deep waters, from the grasp of foreigners,
**v8** whose mouths speak falsehood, whose right hands are deceitful.

**v9** I will sing to You a new song, O God; on a harp of ten strings I will make music to You—
**v10** to Him who gives victory to kings, who frees His servant David from the deadly sword.
**v11** Set me free and rescue mefrom the grasp of foreigners, whose mouths speak falsehood, whose right hands are deceitful.

**v12** Then our sons will be like plantsnurtured in their youth, our daughters like corner pillarscarved to adorn a palace.
**v13** Our storehouses will be full, supplying all manner of produce; our flocks will bring forth thousands, tens of thousands in our fields.
**v14** Our oxen will bear great loads. [^2] There will be no breach in the walls, no going into captivity, and no cry of lament in our streets.

**v15** Blessed are the people of whom this is so; blessed are the people whose God is the LORD.
[^1]: Many Hebrew manuscripts, DSS, Syriac; most Hebrew manuscripts subdues my people ( 144:2)
[^2]: Or Our chieftains will be firmly established ( 144:14)

### Chapter 145

#### I Will Exalt You, My God and King

**v1** I will exalt You, my God and King; I will bless Your name forever and ever.
**v2** Every day I will bless You, and I will praise Your name forever and ever.

**v3** Great is the LORD and greatly to be praised; His greatness is unsearchable.
**v4** One generation will commend Your works to the next, and will proclaim Your mighty acts—
**v5** the glorious splendor of Your majesty.And I will meditate on Your wondrous works.
**v6** They will proclaim the power of Your awesome deeds, and I will declare Your greatness.
**v7** They will extol the fame of Your abundant goodnessand sing joyfully of Your righteousness.

**v8** The LORD is gracious and compassionate, slow to anger and abounding in loving devotion.
**v9** The LORD is good to all; His compassion rests on all He has made.
**v10** All You have made will give You thanks, O LORD, and Your saints will bless You.
**v11** They will tell of the glory of Your kingdomand speak of Your might,
**v12** to make known to men Your mighty actsand the glorious splendor of Your kingdom.
**v13** Your kingdom is an everlasting kingdom, and Your dominion endures through all generations.The LORD is faithful in all His wordsand kind in all His actions. [^2]

**v14** The LORD upholds all who falland lifts up all who are bowed down.
**v15** The eyes of all look to You, and You give them their food in season.
**v16** You open Your handand satisfy the desire of every living thing.

**v17** The LORD is righteous in all His waysand kind in all His deeds.
**v18** The LORD is near to all who call on Him, to all who call out to Him in truth.
**v19** He fulfills the desires of those who fear Him; He hears their cry and saves them.
**v20** The LORD preserves all who love Him, but all the wicked He will destroy.
**v21** My mouth will declare the praise of the LORD; let every creature bless His holy nameforever and ever.
[^1]: This psalm is an acrostic poem, each verse beginning with the successive letters of the Hebrew alphabet. ( 145:0)
[^2]: The final two lines are supplied by one MT manuscript, LXX, Syriac, and DSS. ( 145:13)

### Chapter 146

#### Praise the LORD, O My Soul
**v1** Hallelujah! [^1] Praise the LORD, O my soul.

**v2** I will praise the LORD all my life; I will sing praises to my God while I have my being.

**v3** Put not your trust in princes, in mortal man, who cannot save.
**v4** When his spirit departs, he returns to the ground; on that very day his plans perish.

**v5** Blessed is he whose help is the God of Jacob, whose hope is in the LORD his God,
**v6** the Maker of heaven and earth, the sea, and everything in them.He remains faithful forever.
**v7** He executes justice for the oppressedand gives food to the hungry.The LORD sets the prisoners free,
**v8** the LORD opens the eyes of the blind, the LORD lifts those who are weighed down, the LORD loves the righteous.
**v9** The LORD protects foreigners; He sustains the fatherless and the widow, but the ways of the wicked He frustrates.

**v10** The LORD reigns forever, your God, O Zion, for all generations.Hallelujah!
[^1]: Or Hallelu YAH, meaning Praise the LORD; also in verse 10 ( 146:1)

### Chapter 147

#### It Is Good to Sing Praises
**v1** Hallelujah! [^1] How good it is to sing praises to our God, how pleasant and lovely to praise Him!

**v2** The LORD builds up Jerusalem; He gathers the exiles of Israel.
**v3** He heals the brokenheartedand binds up their wounds.
**v4** He determines the number of the stars; He calls them each by name.
**v5** Great is our Lord, and mighty in power; His understanding has no limit.
**v6** The LORD sustains the humble, but casts the wicked to the ground.

**v7** Sing to the LORD with thanksgiving; make music on the harp to our God,
**v8** who covers the sky with clouds, who prepares rain for the earth, who makes grass to grow on the hills.
**v9** He provides food for the animals, and for the young ravens when they call.

**v10** He does not delight in the strength of the horse; He takes no pleasure in the legs of a man.
**v11** The LORD is pleased with those who fear Him, who hope in His loving devotion.

**v12** Exalt the LORD, O Jerusalem; praise your God, O Zion!
**v13** For He strengthens the bars of your gatesand blesses the children within you.
**v14** He makes peace at your borders; He fills you with the finest wheat.

**v15** He sends forth His command to the earth; His word runs swiftly.
**v16** He spreads the snow like wool; He scatters the frost like ashes;
**v17** He casts forth His hail like pebbles. [^2] Who can withstand His icy blast?
**v18** He sends forth His word and melts them; He unleashes His winds, and the waters flow.

**v19** He declares His word to Jacob, His statutes and judgments to Israel.
**v20** He has done this for no other nation; they do not know His judgments. [^3] Hallelujah!
[^1]: Or Hallelu YAH, meaning Praise the LORD; also in verse 20 ( 147:1)
[^2]: Or like crumbs or like morsels ( 147:17)
[^3]: MT; DSS and LXX He has not made known to them His judgments ( 147:20)

### Chapter 148

#### Praise the LORD from the Heavens
**v1** Hallelujah! [^1] Praise the LORD from the heavens; praise Him in the highest places. [^2]
**v2** Praise Him, all His angels; praise Him, all His heavenly hosts.
**v3** Praise Him, O sun and moon; praise Him, all you shining stars.
**v4** Praise Him, O highest heavens, and you waters above the skies.
**v5** Let them praise the name of the LORD, for He gave the command and they were created.
**v6** He established them forever and ever; He issued a decree that will never pass away.

**v7** Praise the LORD from the earth, all great sea creatures and ocean depths,
**v8** lightning and hail, snow and clouds, powerful wind fulfilling His word,
**v9** mountains and all hills, fruit trees and all cedars,
**v10** wild animals and all cattle, crawling creatures and flying birds,
**v11** kings of the earth and all peoples, princes and all rulers of the earth,
**v12** young men and maidens, old and young together.

**v13** Let them praise the name of the LORD, for His name alone is exalted; His splendor is above the earth and the heavens.
**v14** He has raised up a horn for His people, the praise of all His saints, of Israel, a people near to Him.Hallelujah!
[^1]: Or Hallelu YAH, meaning Praise the LORD; also in verse 14 ( 148:1)
[^2]: See Matthew 21:9, Mark 11:10, and Luke 19:38. ( 148:1)

### Chapter 149

#### Sing to the LORD a New Song
**v1** Hallelujah! [^1] Sing to the LORD a new song—His praise in the assembly of the godly.
**v2** Let Israel rejoice in their Maker; let the children of Zion rejoice in their King.
**v3** Let them praise His name with dancing, and make music to Him with tambourine and harp.
**v4** For the LORD takes pleasure in His people; He adorns the afflicted with salvation.
**v5** Let the saints exult in glory; let them shout for joy upon their beds.

**v6** May the high praises of God be in their mouths, and a double-edged sword in their hands,
**v7** to inflict vengeance on the nationsand punishment on the peoples,
**v8** to bind their kings with chainsand their nobles with shackles of iron,
**v9** to execute the judgment written against them.This honor is for all His saints.Hallelujah!
[^1]: Or Hallelu YAH, meaning Praise the LORD; also in verse 9 ( 149:1)

### Chapter 150

#### Let Everything That Has Breath Praise the LORD
**v1** Hallelujah! [^1] Praise God in His sanctuary.Praise Him in His mighty heavens. [^2]
**v2** Praise Him for His mighty acts; praise Him for His excellent greatness.

**v3** Praise Him with the sound of the horn; praise Him with the harp and lyre.
**v4** Praise Him with tambourine and dancing; praise Him with strings and flute.
**v5** Praise Him with clashing cymbals; praise Him with resounding cymbals.

**v6** Let everything that has breath praise the LORD!Hallelujah!
[^1]: Or Hallelu YAH, meaning Praise the LORD; also in verse 6 ( 150:1)
[^2]: Or in the expanse of His might or in the firmament of His might; see also Genesis 1:6–8. ( 150:1)

## Proverbs

### Chapter 1

#### The Beginning of Knowledge
**v1** These are the proverbs of Solomon son of David, king of Israel,
**v2** for gaining wisdom and discipline, for comprehending words of insight,
**v3** and for receiving instruction in wise livingand in righteousness, justice, and equity.
**v4** To impart prudence to the simple [^1] and knowledge and discretion to the young,
**v5** let the wise listen and gain instruction, and the discerning acquire wise counsel
**v6** by understanding the proverbs and parables, the sayings and riddles of the wise.

**v7** The fear of the LORD is the beginning of knowledge, but fools [^2] despise wisdom and discipline.
#### The Enticement of Sin

**v8** Listen, my son, to your father's instruction, and do not forsake the teaching of your mother.
**v9** For they are a garland of grace on your headand a pendant around your neck.

**v10** My son, if sinners entice you, do not yield to them.
**v11** If they say, "Come along, let us lie in wait for blood, let us ambush the innocent without cause,
**v12** let us swallow them alive like Sheol, and whole like those descending into the Pit.
**v13** We will find all manner of precious goods; we will fill our houses with plunder.
**v14** Throw in your lot with us; let us all share one purse"—
**v15** my son, do not walk the road with themor set foot upon their path.
**v16** For their feet run to evil, and they are swift to shed blood.
**v17** How futile it is to spread the netwhere any bird can see it!
**v18** But they lie in wait for their own blood; they ambush their own lives.
**v19** Such is the fate of all who are greedy, whose unjust gain takes the lives of its possessors.
#### Wisdom Calls Aloud

**v20** Wisdom calls out in the street, she lifts her voice in the square;
**v21** in the main concourse [^3] she cries aloud, at the city gates she makes her speech:

**v22** "How long, O simple ones, will you love your simple ways?How long will scoffers delight in their scornand fools hate knowledge?
**v23** If you had repented at my rebuke, then surely I would have poured out my spirit on you; I would have made my words known to you.
**v24** Because you refused my call, and no one took my outstretched hand,
**v25** because you neglected all my counsel, and wanted none of my correction,
**v26** in turn I will mock your calamity; I will sneer when terror strikes you,
**v27** when your dread comes like a storm, and your destruction like a whirlwind, when distress and anguish overwhelm you.

**v28** Then they will call on me, but I will not answer; they will earnestly seek me, but will not find me.
**v29** For they hated knowledgeand chose not to fear the LORD.
**v30** They accepted none of my counsel; they despised all my reproof.
**v31** So they will eat the fruit of their own way, and be filled with their own devices.
**v32** For the waywardness of the simple will slay them, and the complacency of fools will destroy them.
**v33** But whoever listens to me will dwell in safety, secure from the fear of evil."
[^1]: The Hebrew word rendered simple in Proverbs refers to one who is naive, without moral direction, or inclined to evil. ( 1:4)
[^2]: The Hebrew words rendered as fool in Proverbs denote one who is morally deficient. ( 1:7)
[^3]: Or from the top of the wall ( 1:21)

### Chapter 2

#### The Benefits of Wisdom
**v1** My son, if you accept my wordsand hide my commandments within you,
**v2** if you incline your ear to wisdomand direct your heart to understanding,
**v3** if you truly call out to insightand lift your voice to understanding,
**v4** if you seek it like silverand search it out like hidden treasure,
**v5** then you will discern the fear of the LORDand discover the knowledge of God.

**v6** For the LORD gives wisdom; from His mouth come knowledge and understanding.
**v7** He stores up sound wisdom for the upright; He is a shield to those who walk with integrity,
**v8** to guard the paths of justiceand protect the way of His saints.

**v9** Then you will discern righteousnessand justice and equity—every good path.
**v10** For wisdom will enter your heart, and knowledge will delight your soul.
**v11** Discretion will watch over you, and understanding will guard you,
**v12** to deliver you from the way of evil, from the man who speaks perversity,
**v13** from those who leave the straight pathsto walk in the ways of darkness,
**v14** from those who enjoy doing eviland rejoice in the twistedness of evil,
**v15** whose paths are crookedand whose ways are devious.

**v16** It will rescue you from the forbidden woman, [^1] from the stranger [^2] with seductive words
**v17** who abandons the partner of her youthand forgets the covenant of her God.
**v18** For her house sinks down to death, and her tracks to the departed spirits. [^3]
**v19** None who go to her returnor negotiate the paths of life.

**v20** So you will follow in the ways of the good, and keep to the paths of the righteous.
**v21** For the upright will inhabit the land, and the blameless will remain in it;
**v22** but the wicked will be cut off from the land, and the unfaithful will be uprooted.
[^1]: Or wayward wife ( 2:16)
[^2]: Or adulteress ( 2:16)
[^3]: Hebrew to the Rephaim ( 2:18)

### Chapter 3

#### Trust in the LORD with All Your Heart
**v1** My son, do not forget my teaching, but let your heart keep my commandments;
**v2** for they will add length to your days, years and peace to your life.
**v3** Never let loving devotion [^1] or faithfulness leave you; bind them around your neck, write them on the tablet of your heart.
**v4** Then you will find favor and high regardin the sight of God and man.

**v5** Trust in the LORD with all your heart, and lean not on your own understanding;
**v6** in all your ways acknowledge Him, and He will make your paths straight.
**v7** Be not wise in your own eyes; fear the LORD and turn away from evil.
**v8** This will bring healing to your body [^2] and refreshment [^3] to your bones.

**v9** Honor the LORD with your wealthand with the firstfruits of all your crops;
**v10** then your barns will be filled with plenty, and your vats will overflow with new wine.

**v11** My son, do not reject the discipline of the LORD, and do not loathe His rebuke; [^4]
**v12** for the LORD disciplines the one He loves, as does a father the son in whom he delights. [^5]
#### The Blessings of Wisdom

**v13** Blessed is the man who finds wisdom, the man who acquires understanding,
**v14** for she is more profitable than silver, and her gain is better than fine gold.
**v15** She is more precious than rubies; nothing you desire compares with her.
**v16** Long life is in her right hand; in her left hand are riches and honor.
**v17** All her ways are pleasant, and all her paths are peaceful.
**v18** She is a tree of life to those who embrace her, and those who lay hold of her are blessed.

**v19** The LORD founded the earth by wisdomand established the heavens by understanding.
**v20** By His knowledge the watery depths were broken open, and the clouds dripped with dew.

**v21** My son, do not lose sight of this:Preserve sound judgment and discernment.
**v22** They will be life to your souland adornment to your neck.
**v23** Then you will go on your way in safety, and your foot will not stumble.
**v24** When you lie down, you will not be afraid; when you rest, your sleep will be sweet.
**v25** Do not fear sudden dangeror the ruin that overtakes the wicked,
**v26** for the LORD will be your confidenceand will keep your foot from the snare.

**v27** Do not withhold good from the deserving [^6] when it is within your power to act.
**v28** Do not tell your neighbor,"Come back tomorrow and I will provide"—when you already have the means.
**v29** Do not devise evil against your neighbor, for he trustfully dwells beside you.
**v30** Do not accuse a man without cause, when he has done you no harm.

**v31** Do not envy a violent manor choose any of his ways;
**v32** for the LORD detests the perverse, but He is a friend to the upright.
**v33** The curse of the LORD is on the house of the wicked, but He blesses the home of the righteous.
**v34** He mocks the mockers, but gives grace to the humble. [^7]
**v35** The wise will inherit honor, but fools are held up to shame.
[^1]: Forms of the Hebrew chesed are translated here and in most cases throughout the Scriptures as loving devotion; the range of meaning includes love, goodness, kindness, faithfulness, and mercy, as well as loyalty to a covenant. ( 3:3)
[^2]: Hebrew navel ( 3:8)
[^3]: Or medicine ( 3:8)
[^4]: LXX and do not lose heart when He rebukes; cited in Hebrews 12:5 ( 3:11)
[^5]: LXX and He flogs every son He receives; cited in Hebrews 12:6 ( 3:12)
[^6]: Or from its owners ( 3:27)
[^7]: LXX The Lord opposes the proud, but gives grace to the humble; cited in James 4:6 and 1 Peter 5:5 ( 3:34)

### Chapter 4

#### A Father's Instruction
**v1** Listen, my sons, to a father's instruction; pay attention and gain understanding.
**v2** For I give you sound teaching; do not abandon my directive.
**v3** When I was a son to my father, tender and the only child of my mother,
**v4** he taught me and said,"Let your heart lay hold of my words; keep my commands and you will live.
**v5** Get wisdom, get understanding; do not forget my words or turn from them.
**v6** Do not forsake wisdom, and she will preserve you; love her, and she will guard you.
**v7** Wisdom is supreme; so acquire wisdom.And whatever you may acquire, [^1] gain understanding.
**v8** Prize her, and she will exalt you; if you embrace her, she will honor you.
**v9** She will set a garland of grace on your head; she will present you with a crown of beauty."

**v10** Listen, my son, and receive my words, and the years of your life will be many.
**v11** I will guide you in the way of wisdom; I will lead you on straight paths.
**v12** When you walk, your steps will not be impeded; when you run, you will not stumble.
**v13** Hold on to instruction; do not let go.Guard it, for it is your life.
**v14** Do not set foot on the path of the wickedor walk in the way of evildoers.
**v15** Avoid it; do not travel on it.Turn from it and pass on by.
**v16** For they cannot sleepunless they do evil; they are deprived of slumberuntil they make someone fall.
**v17** For they eat the bread of wickednessand drink the wine of violence.
**v18** The path of the righteous is like the first gleam of dawn, shining brighter and brighter until midday.
**v19** But the way of the wicked is like the darkest gloom; they do not know what makes them stumble.

**v20** My son, pay attention to my words; incline your ear to my sayings.
**v21** Do not lose sight of them; keep them within your heart.
**v22** For they are life to those who find them, and health to the whole body.
**v23** Guard your heart with all diligence, for from it flow springs of life.
**v24** Put away deception from your mouth; keep your lips from perverse speech.
**v25** Let your eyes look forward; fix your gaze straight ahead.
**v26** Make a level path for your feet, [^2] and all your ways will be sure.
**v27** Do not swerve to the right or to the left; turn your feet away from evil.
[^1]: Or And whatever else you acquire ( 4:7)
[^2]: Or Ponder the path for your feet; LXX Make straight paths for your feet; cited in Hebrews 12:13 ( 4:26)

### Chapter 5

#### Avoiding Immorality
**v1** My son, pay attention to my wisdom; incline your ear to my insight,
**v2** that you may maintain discretionand your lips may preserve knowledge.
**v3** Though the lips of the forbidden woman [^1] drip honeyand her speech [^2] is smoother than oil,
**v4** in the end she is bitter as wormwood, sharp as a double-edged sword.
**v5** Her feet go down to death; her steps lead straight to Sheol. [^3]
**v6** She does not consider the path of life; she does not know that her ways are unstable.

**v7** So now, my sons, listen to me, and do not turn aside from the words of my mouth.
**v8** Keep your path far from her; do not go near the door of her house,
**v9** lest you concede your vigor to others, and your years to one who is cruel;
**v10** lest strangers feast on your wealth, and your labors enrich the house of a foreigner.
**v11** At the end of your life you will groanwhen your flesh and your body are spent,
**v12** and you will say, "How I hated discipline, and my heart despised reproof!
**v13** I did not listen to the voice of my teachersor incline my ear to my mentors.
**v14** I am on the brink of utter ruinin the midst of the whole assembly."

**v15** Drink water from your own cistern, and running water from your own well.
**v16** Why should your springs flow in the streets, your streams of water in the public squares?
**v17** Let them be yours alone, never to be shared with strangers.
**v18** May your fountain be blessed, and may you rejoice in the wife of your youth:
**v19** A loving doe, a graceful fawn—may her breasts satisfy you always; may you be captivated [^4] by her love forever.
**v20** Why be captivated, my son, by an adulteress, or embrace the bosom of a stranger? [^5]
**v21** For a man's ways are before the eyes of the LORD, and the LORD examines [^6] all his paths.
**v22** The iniquities of a wicked man entrap him; the cords of his sin entangle him.
**v23** He dies for lack of discipline, led astray by his own great folly.
[^1]: Or the adulteress ( 5:3)
[^2]: Or her palate ( 5:3)
[^3]: Or lay hold of Sheol ( 5:5)
[^4]: Or be led astray; also in verse 20 ( 5:19)
[^5]: Or a foreign woman or another man's wife ( 5:20)
[^6]: Or ponders or makes level ( 5:21)

### Chapter 6

#### Warnings against Foolishness
**v1** My son, if you have put up security for your neighbor, if you have struck hands in pledge with a stranger,
**v2** if you have been trapped by the words of your lips, ensnared by the words of your mouth,
**v3** then do this, my son, to free yourself, for you have fallen into your neighbor's hands:Go, humble yourself, [^1] and press your plea with your neighbor.
**v4** Allow no sleep to your eyesor slumber to your eyelids.
**v5** Free yourself, like a gazelle from the hand of the hunter, [^2] like a bird from the snare of the fowler.

**v6** Walk in the manner of the ant, O slacker; observe its ways and become wise.
**v7** Without a commander, without an overseer or ruler,
**v8** it prepares its provisions in summer; it gathers its food at harvest.
**v9** How long will you lie there, O slacker?When will you get up from your sleep?
**v10** A little sleep, a little slumber, a little folding of the hands to rest,
**v11** and poverty will come upon you like a robber, and need like a bandit.

**v12** A worthless person, a wicked man, walks with a perverse mouth,
**v13** winking his eyes, speaking with his feet, and pointing with his fingers.
**v14** With deceit in his heart he devises evil; he continually sows discord.
**v15** Therefore calamity will come upon him suddenly; in an instant he will be shattered beyond recovery.

**v16** There are six things that the LORD hates, seven that are detestable to Him:

**v17** haughty eyes, a lying tongue, hands that shed innocent blood,

**v18** a heart that devises wicked schemes, feet that run swiftly to evil,

**v19** a false witness who gives false testimony, and one who stirs up discord among brothers.
#### Warnings against Adultery

**v20** My son, keep your father's commandment, and do not forsake your mother's teaching.
**v21** Bind them always upon your heart; tie them around your neck.
**v22** When you walk, they will guide you; when you lie down, they will watch over you; when you awake, they will speak to you.
**v23** For this commandment is a lamp, this teaching is a light, and the reproofs of discipline are the way to life,
**v24** to keep you from the evil woman, from the smooth tongue of the adulteress. [^3]

**v25** Do not lust in your heart for her beautyor let her captivate you with her eyes. [^4]
**v26** For the levy of the prostitute is poverty, [^5] and the adulteress preys upon your very life.
**v27** Can a man embrace fireand his clothes not be burned?
**v28** Can a man walk on hot coalswithout scorching his feet?
**v29** So is he who sleeps with another man's wife; no one who touches her will go unpunished.

**v30** Men do not despise the thiefif he steals to satisfy his hunger.
**v31** Yet if caught, he must pay sevenfold; he must give up all the wealth of his house.
**v32** He who commits adultery lacks judgment; whoever does so destroys himself.
**v33** Wounds and dishonor will befall him, and his reproach will never be wiped away.
**v34** For jealousy enrages a husband, and he will show no mercy in the day of vengeance.
**v35** He will not be appeased by any ransom, or persuaded by lavish gifts.
[^1]: Or hasten ( 6:3)
[^2]: Hebrew does not include of the hunter. ( 6:5)
[^3]: Or the stranger ( 6:24)
[^4]: Or eyelids or eyelashes ( 6:25)
[^5]: Literally a crust of bread ( 6:26)

### Chapter 7

#### Warnings about the Adulteress
**v1** My son, keep my wordsand treasure my commandments within you.
**v2** Keep my commandments and live; guard my teachings as the apple [^1] of your eye.
**v3** Tie them to your fingers; write them on the tablet of your heart.
**v4** Say to wisdom, "You are my sister,"and call understanding your kinsman,
**v5** that they may keep you from the adulteress, from the stranger with seductive words.

**v6** For at the window of my house I looked through the lattice.
**v7** I saw among the simple, I noticed among the youths, a young man lacking judgment,
**v8** crossing the street near her corner, strolling down the road to her house,
**v9** at twilight, as the day was fadinginto the dark of the night.

**v10** Then a woman came out to meet him, with the attire of a harlot and cunning of heart.
**v11** She is loud and defiant; her feet do not remain at home.
**v12** Now in the street, now in the squares, she lurks at every corner.
**v13** She seizes him and kisses him; she brazenly says to him:

**v14** "I have made my peace offerings; today I have paid my vows.
**v15** So I came out to meet you; I sought you, and I have found you.
**v16** I have decked my bed with coverings, with colored linen from Egypt.
**v17** I have perfumed my bed with myrrh, with aloes, and with cinnamon.
**v18** Come, let us take our fill of love till morning.Let us delight in loving caresses!
**v19** For my husband is not at home; he has gone on a long journey.
**v20** He took with him a bag of moneyand will not return till the moon is full."

**v21** With her great persuasion she entices him; with her flattering lips she lures him.
**v22** He follows her on impulse, like an ox going to the slaughter, like a deer bounding into a trap, [^2]
**v23** until an arrow pierces his liver, like a bird darting into a snare—not knowing it will cost him his life.

**v24** Now, my sons, listen to me, and attend to the words of my mouth.
**v25** Do not let your heart turn aside to her ways; do not stray into her paths.
**v26** For she has brought many down to death; her slain are many in number.
**v27** Her house is the road to Sheol, descending to the chambers of death.
[^1]: Literally the pupil ( 7:2)
[^2]: Probable reading (see LXX, Vulgate, Syriac); Hebrew like fetters to discipline a fool ( 7:22)

### Chapter 8

#### The Excellence of Wisdom
**v1** Does not wisdom call out, and understanding raise her voice?
**v2** On the heights overlooking the road, at the crossroads she takes her stand.
**v3** Beside the gates to the city, at the entrances she cries out:

**v4** "To you, O men, I call out, and my cry is to the sons of men.
**v5** O simple ones, learn to be shrewd; O fools, gain understanding. [^1]
**v6** Listen, for I speak of noble things, and the opening of my lips will reveal right.

**v7** For my mouth will speak the truth, and wickedness is detestable to my lips.
**v8** All the words of my mouth are righteous; none are crooked or perverse.
**v9** They are all plain to the discerning, and upright to those who find knowledge.
**v10** Receive my instruction instead of silver, and knowledge rather than pure gold.
**v11** For wisdom is more precious than rubies, and nothing you desire compares with her.

**v12** I, wisdom, dwell together with prudence, and I find knowledge and discretion.
**v13** To fear the LORD is to hate evil; I hate arrogant pride, evil conduct, and perverse speech.
**v14** Counsel and sound judgment are mine; I have insight and strength.
**v15** By me kings reign, and rulers enact just laws;
**v16** By me princes rule, and all nobles who govern justly. [^2]

**v17** I love those who love me, and those who seek me early shall find me.
**v18** With me are riches and honor, enduring wealth and righteousness.
**v19** My fruit is better than gold, pure gold, and my harvest surpasses choice silver.
**v20** I walk in the way of righteousness, along the paths of justice,
**v21** bestowing wealth on those who love meand making their treasuries full.

**v22** The LORD created me as His first course, [^3] before His works of old.
**v23** From everlasting I was established, from the beginning, before the earth began.
**v24** When there were no watery depths, I was brought forth, when no springs were overflowing with water.
**v25** Before the mountains were settled, before the hills, I was brought forth,
**v26** before He made the land or fields, or any of the dust of the earth.

**v27** I was there when He established the heavens, when He inscribed a circle on the face of the deep,
**v28** when He established the clouds above, when the fountains of the deep gushed forth,
**v29** when He set a boundary for the sea, so that the waters would not surpass His command, when He marked out the foundations of the earth.
**v30** Then I was a skilled craftsman at His side, and His delight [^4] day by day, rejoicing always in His presence.
**v31** I was rejoicing in His whole world, delighting together in the sons of men.

**v32** Now therefore, my sons, listen to me, for blessed are those who keep my ways.
**v33** Listen to instruction and be wise; do not ignore it.
**v34** Blessed is the man who listens to me, watching daily at my doors, waiting at the posts of my doorway.
**v35** For whoever finds me finds lifeand obtains the favor of the LORD.
**v36** But he who fails to find me harms himself; all who hate me love death."
[^1]: Or instruct your minds ( 8:5)
[^2]: Some Hebrew manuscripts and LXX who govern the earth ( 8:16)
[^3]: Or The LORD possessed me at the beginning of His way ( 8:22)
[^4]: Or filled with His delight ( 8:30)

### Chapter 9

#### The Way of Wisdom
**v1** Wisdom has built her house; she has carved out [^1] her seven pillars.
**v2** She has prepared her meat and mixed her wine; she has also set her table.
**v3** She has sent out her maidservants; she calls out from the heights of the city.
**v4** "Whoever is simple, let him turn in here!"she says to him who lacks judgment.
**v5** "Come, eat my breadand drink the wine I have mixed.
**v6** Leave your folly behind, and you will live; walk in the way of understanding."

**v7** He who corrects a mocker brings shame on himself; he who rebukes a wicked man taints himself.
**v8** Do not rebuke a mocker, or he will hate you; rebuke a wise man, and he will love you.
**v9** Instruct a wise man, and he will be wiser still; teach a righteous man, and he will increase his learning.

**v10** The fear of the LORD is the beginning of wisdom, and knowledge of the Holy One is understanding.
**v11** For through wisdom [^2] your days will be multiplied, and years will be added to your life.
**v12** If you are wise, you are wise to your own advantage; but if you scoff, you alone will bear the consequences.
#### The Way of Folly

**v13** The woman named Folly is loud; she is naive and knows nothing.
**v14** She sits at the door of her house, on a seat in the heights of the city,
**v15** calling out to those who pass by, who make their paths straight.
**v16** "Whoever is simple, let him turn in here!"she says to him who lacks judgment.
**v17** "Stolen water is sweet, and bread eaten in secret is tasty!"
**v18** But they do not know that the dead [^3] are there, that her guests are in the depths of Sheol.
[^1]: Hebrew; LXX, Syriac, and Aramaic Targum has set up ( 9:1)
[^2]: LXX, Syriac, and Aramaic Targum; Hebrew through me ( 9:11)
[^3]: Hebrew the Rephaim ( 9:18)

### Chapter 10

#### Solomon's Proverbs: The Wise Son
**v1** The proverbs of Solomon:A wise son brings joy to his father, but a foolish son grief to his mother.

**v2** Ill-gotten treasures profit nothing, but righteousness brings deliverance from death.

**v3** The LORD does not let the righteous go hungry, but He denies the craving of the wicked.

**v4** Idle hands make one poor, but diligent hands bring wealth.

**v5** He who gathers in summer is a wise son, but he who sleeps during harvest is a disgraceful son.

**v6** Blessings are on the head of the righteous, but the mouth of the wicked conceals violence. [^1]

**v7** The memory of the righteous is a blessing, but the name of the wicked will rot.

**v8** A wise heart will receive commandments, but foolish lips will come to ruin.

**v9** He who walks in integrity walks securely, but he who perverts his ways will be found out.

**v10** He who winks the eye causes grief, and foolish lips will come to ruin. [^2]

**v11** The mouth of the righteous is a fountain of life, but the mouth of the wicked conceals violence.

**v12** Hatred stirs up dissension, but love covers all transgressions. [^3]

**v13** Wisdom is found on the lips of the discerning, but a rod is for the back of him who lacks judgment.

**v14** The wise store up knowledge, but the mouth of the fool invites destruction.

**v15** The wealth of the rich man is his fortified city, but poverty is the ruin of the poor.

**v16** The labor of the righteous leads to life, but the gain of the wicked brings punishment.

**v17** Whoever heeds instruction is on the path to life, but he who ignores reproof goes astray.

**v18** The one who conceals hatred has lying lips, and whoever spreads slander is a fool.

**v19** When words are many, sin is unavoidable, but he who restrains his lips is wise.

**v20** The tongue of the righteous is choice silver, but the heart of the wicked has little worth.

**v21** The lips of the righteous feed many, but fools die for lack of judgment.

**v22** The blessing of the LORD enriches, and He adds no sorrow to it.

**v23** The fool delights in shameful conduct, but a man of understanding has wisdom.

**v24** What the wicked man dreads will overtake him, but the desire of the righteous will be granted.

**v25** When the whirlwind passes, the wicked are no more, but the righteous are secure forever.

**v26** Like vinegar to the teeth and smoke to the eyes, so is the slacker to those who send him.

**v27** The fear of the LORD prolongs life, but the years of the wicked will be cut short.

**v28** The hope of the righteous is joy, but the expectations of the wicked will perish.

**v29** The way of the LORD is a refuge to the upright, but destruction awaits those who do evil.

**v30** The righteous will never be shaken, but the wicked will not inhabit the land.

**v31** The mouth of the righteous brings forth wisdom, but a perverse tongue will be cut out.

**v32** The lips of the righteous know what is fitting, but the mouth of the wicked is perverse.
[^1]: Or but violence covers the mouth of the wicked; also in verse 11 ( 10:6)
[^2]: Or babbling fools will fall ( 10:10)
[^3]: See 1 Peter 4:8 ( 10:12)

### Chapter 11

#### Dishonest Scales
**v1** Dishonest scales are an abomination to the LORD, but an accurate weight is His delight.

**v2** When pride comes, disgrace follows, but with humility comes wisdom.

**v3** The integrity of the upright guides them, but the perversity of the faithless destroys them.

**v4** Riches are worthless in the day of wrath, but righteousness brings deliverance from death.

**v5** The righteousness of the blameless directs their path, but the wicked fall by their own wickedness.

**v6** The righteousness of the upright delivers them, but the faithless are trapped by their own desires.

**v7** When the wicked man dies, his hope perishes, and the hope of his strength vanishes.

**v8** The righteous man is delivered from trouble; in his place the wicked man goes in.

**v9** With his mouth the ungodly man destroys his neighbor, but through knowledge the righteous are rescued.

**v10** When the righteous thrive, the city rejoices, and when the wicked perish, there are shouts of joy.

**v11** By the blessing of the upright a city is built up, but by the mouth of the wicked it is torn down.

**v12** Whoever shows contempt for his neighbor lacks judgment, but a man of understanding remains silent.

**v13** A gossip reveals a secret, but a trustworthy person keeps a confidence.

**v14** For lack of guidance, a nation falls, but with many counselors comes deliverance.

**v15** He who puts up security for a stranger will surely suffer, but the one who hates indebtedness is secure.

**v16** A gracious woman attains honor, but ruthless men gain only wealth.

**v17** A kind man benefits himself, but a cruel man brings trouble on himself.

**v18** The wicked man earns an empty wage, but he who sows righteousness reaps a true reward.

**v19** Genuine righteousness leads to life, but the pursuit of evil brings death.

**v20** The perverse in heart are an abomination to the LORD, but the blameless in their walk are His delight.

**v21** Be assured that the wicked will not go unpunished, but the offspring of the righteous will escape.

**v22** Like a gold ring in a pig's snoutis a beautiful woman who lacks discretion.

**v23** The desire of the righteous leads only to good, but the hope of the wicked brings wrath.

**v24** One gives freely, yet gains even more; another withholds what is right, only to become poor.

**v25** A generous soul will prosper, and he who refreshes others will himself be refreshed.

**v26** The people will curse the hoarder of grain, but blessing will crown the one who sells it.

**v27** He who searches out good finds favor, but evil will come to him who seeks it.

**v28** He who trusts in his riches will fall, but the righteous will thrive like foliage.

**v29** He who brings trouble on his house will inherit the wind, and the fool will be servant to the wise of heart.

**v30** The fruit of the righteous is a tree of life, and he who wins souls is wise.

**v31** If the righteous receive their due on earth, how much more the ungodly and the sinner! [^1]
[^1]: LXX If it is hard for the righteous to be saved, what will become of the ungodly and the sinner? Cited in 1 Peter 4:18 ( 11:31)

### Chapter 12

#### Loving Discipline and Knowledge
**v1** Whoever loves discipline loves knowledge, but he who hates correction is stupid.

**v2** The good man obtains favor from the LORD, but the LORD condemns a man who devises evil.

**v3** A man cannot be established through wickedness, but the righteous cannot be uprooted.

**v4** A wife of noble character is her husband's crown, but she who causes shame is like decay in his bones.

**v5** The plans of the righteous are just, but the counsel of the wicked leads to deceit.

**v6** The words of the wicked lie in wait for blood, but the speech of the upright rescues them.

**v7** The wicked are overthrown and perish, but the house of the righteous will stand.

**v8** A man is praised according to his wisdom, but a twisted mind is despised.

**v9** Better to be lightly esteemed yet have a servant, than to be self-important but lack food.

**v10** A righteous man regards the life of his animal, but the tender mercies of the wicked are only cruelty.

**v11** The one who works his land will have plenty of food, but whoever chases fantasies lacks judgment.

**v12** The wicked desire the plunder of evil men, but the root of the righteous flourishes.

**v13** An evil man is trapped by his rebellious speech, but a righteous man escapes from trouble.

**v14** By fruitful speech a man is filled with good things, and the work of his hands returns to him.

**v15** The way of a fool is right in his own eyes, but a wise man listens to counsel.

**v16** A fool's anger is known at once, but a prudent man overlooks an insult.

**v17** He who speaks the truth declares what is right, but a false witness speaks deceit.

**v18** Speaking rashly is like a piercing sword, but the tongue of the wise brings healing.

**v19** Truthful lips endure forever, but a lying tongue lasts only a moment.

**v20** Deceit is in the hearts of those who devise evil, but the counselors of peace have joy.

**v21** No harm befalls the righteous, but the wicked are filled with trouble.

**v22** Lying lips are detestable to the LORD, but those who deal faithfully are His delight.

**v23** A shrewd man keeps his knowledge to himself, but a foolish heart proclaims its folly.

**v24** The hand of the diligent will rule, but laziness ends in forced labor.

**v25** Anxiety weighs down the heart of a man, but a good word cheers it up.

**v26** A righteous man is cautious in friendship, but the ways of the wicked lead them astray.

**v27** A lazy man does not roast his game, but a diligent man prizes his possession.

**v28** There is life in the path of righteousness, but another path leads to death.
### Chapter 13

#### A Father's Discipline
**v1** A wise son heeds his father's discipline, but a mocker does not listen to rebuke.

**v2** From the fruit of his lips a man enjoys good things, but the desire of the faithless is violence.

**v3** He who guards his mouth protects his life, but the one who opens his lips invites his own ruin.

**v4** The slacker craves yet has nothing, but the soul of the diligent is fully satisfied.

**v5** The righteous hate falsehood, but the wicked bring shame and disgrace.

**v6** Righteousness guards the man of integrity, but wickedness undermines the sinner.

**v7** One pretends to be rich, but has nothing; another pretends to be poor, yet has great wealth.

**v8** Riches may ransom a man's life, but a poor man hears no threat.

**v9** The light of the righteous shines brightly, but the lamp of the wicked is extinguished.

**v10** Arrogance leads only to strife, but wisdom is with the well-advised.

**v11** Dishonest wealth will dwindle, but what is earned through hard work will be multiplied.

**v12** Hope deferred makes the heart sick, but desire fulfilled is a tree of life.

**v13** He who despises instruction will pay the penalty, but the one who respects a command will be rewarded.

**v14** The teaching [^1] of the wise is a fountain of life, turning one from the snares of death.

**v15** Good understanding wins favor, but the way of the faithless is difficult.

**v16** Every prudent man acts with knowledge, but a fool displays his folly.

**v17** A wicked messenger falls into trouble, but a faithful envoy brings healing.

**v18** Poverty and shame come to him who ignores discipline, but whoever heeds correction is honored.

**v19** Desire fulfilled is sweet to the soul, but turning from evil is detestable to fools.

**v20** He who walks with the wise will become wise, but the companion of fools will be destroyed.

**v21** Disaster pursues sinners, but prosperity is the reward of the righteous.

**v22** A good man leaves an inheritance to his children's children, but the sinner's wealth is passed to the righteous.

**v23** Abundant food is in the fallow ground of the poor, but without justice it is swept away.

**v24** He who spares the rod hates his son, but he who loves him disciplines him diligently.

**v25** A righteous man eats to his heart's content, but the stomach of the wicked is empty.
[^1]: Or law ( 13:14)

### Chapter 14

#### The Wise Woman
**v1** Every wise woman builds her house, but a foolish one tears it down with her own hands.

**v2** He who walks in uprightness fears the LORD, but the one who is devious in his ways despises Him.

**v3** The proud speech of a fool brings a rod to his back, but the lips of the wise protect them.

**v4** Where there are no oxen, the manger is empty, but an abundant harvest comes through the strength of the ox.

**v5** An honest witness does not deceive, but a dishonest witness pours forth lies.

**v6** A mocker seeks wisdom and finds none, but knowledge comes easily to the discerning.

**v7** Stay away from a foolish man; you will gain no knowledge from his speech.

**v8** The wisdom of the prudent is to discern his way, but the folly of fools deceives them.

**v9** Fools mock the making of amends, but goodwill is found among the upright.

**v10** The heart knows its own bitterness, and no stranger shares in its joy.

**v11** The house of the wicked will be destroyed, but the tent of the upright will flourish.

**v12** There is a way that seems right to a man, but its end is the way of death.

**v13** Even in laughter the heart may ache, and joy may end in sorrow.

**v14** The backslider in heart receives the fill of his own ways, but a good man is rewarded for his ways.

**v15** The simple man believes every word, but the prudent man watches his steps.

**v16** A wise man fears [^1] and turns from evil, but a fool is careless and reckless.

**v17** A quick-tempered man acts foolishly, and a devious man is hated.

**v18** The simple inherit folly, but the prudent are crowned with knowledge.

**v19** The evil bow before the good, and the wicked at the gates of the righteous.

**v20** The poor man is hated even by his neighbor, but many are those who love the rich.

**v21** He who despises his neighbor sins, but blessed is he who shows kindness to the poor.

**v22** Do not those who contrive evil go astray?But those who plan goodness find [^2] loving devotion and faithfulness.

**v23** There is profit in all labor, but mere talk leads only to poverty.

**v24** The crown of the wise is their wealth, but the effort of fools is folly.

**v25** A truthful witness saves lives, but one who utters lies is deceitful.

**v26** He who fears the LORD is secure in confidence, and his children shall have a place of refuge.

**v27** The fear of the LORD is a fountain of life, turning a man from the snares of death.

**v28** A large population is a king's splendor, but a lack of subjects is a prince's ruin.

**v29** A patient man has great understanding, but a quick-tempered man promotes folly.

**v30** A tranquil heart is life to the body, but envy rots the bones.

**v31** Whoever oppresses the poor taunts their Maker, but whoever is kind to the needy honors Him.

**v32** The wicked man is thrown down by his own sin, but the righteous man has a refuge even in death.

**v33** Wisdom rests in the heart of the discerning; even among fools she is known. [^3]

**v34** Righteousness exalts a nation, but sin is a disgrace to any people.

**v35** A king delights in a wise servant, but his anger falls on the shameful.
[^1]: Or fears the LORD ( 14:16)
[^2]: Or show ( 14:22)
[^3]: Hebrew; LXX and Syriac but among fools she is not known ( 14:33)

### Chapter 15

#### A Gentle Answer Turns Away Wrath
**v1** A gentle answer turns away wrath, but a harsh word stirs up anger.

**v2** The tongue of the wise commends knowledge, but the mouth of the fool spouts folly.

**v3** The eyes of the LORD are in every place, observing the evil and the good.

**v4** A soothing tongue is a tree of life, but a perverse tongue crushes the spirit.

**v5** A fool rejects his father's discipline, but whoever heeds correction is prudent.

**v6** The house of the righteous has great treasure, but the income of the wicked is trouble.

**v7** The lips of the wise spread knowledge, but not so the hearts of fools.

**v8** The sacrifice of the wicked is detestable to the LORD, but the prayer of the upright is His delight.

**v9** The LORD detests the way of the wicked, but He loves those who pursue righteousness.

**v10** Discipline is harsh for him who leaves the path; he who hates correction will die.

**v11** Sheol and Abaddon [^1] lie open before the LORD—how much more the hearts of men!

**v12** A mocker does not love to be reproved, nor will he consult the wise.

**v13** A joyful heart makes a cheerful countenance, but sorrow of the heart crushes the spirit.

**v14** A discerning heart seeks knowledge, but the mouth of a fool feeds on folly.

**v15** All the days of the oppressed are bad, but a cheerful heart has a continual feast.

**v16** Better a little with the fear of the LORDthan great treasure with turmoil.

**v17** Better a dish of vegetables where there is lovethan a fattened ox with hatred.

**v18** A hot-tempered man stirs up strife, but he who is slow to anger calms dispute.

**v19** The way of the slacker is like a hedge of thorns, but the path of the upright is a highway.

**v20** A wise son brings joy to his father, but a foolish man despises his mother.

**v21** Folly is joy to one who lacks judgment, but a man of understanding walks a straight path.

**v22** Plans fail for lack of counsel, but with many advisers they succeed.

**v23** A man takes joy in a fitting reply—and how good is a timely word!

**v24** The path of life leads upward for the wise, that he may avoid going down to Sheol.

**v25** The LORD tears down the house of the proud, but He protects the boundaries of the widow.

**v26** The LORD detests the thoughts of the wicked, but the words of the pure are pleasant to Him.

**v27** He who is greedy for unjust gain brings trouble on his household, but he who hates bribes will live.

**v28** The heart of the righteous ponders how to answer, but the mouth of the wicked blurts out evil.

**v29** The LORD is far from the wicked, but He hears the prayer of the righteous.

**v30** The light of the eyes cheers the heart, and good news nourishes the bones.

**v31** He who listens to life-giving reproofwill dwell among the wise.

**v32** He who ignores discipline despises himself, but whoever heeds correction gains understanding.

**v33** The fear of the LORD is the instruction of wisdom, and humility comes before honor.
[^1]: Or Death and Destruction ( 15:11)

### Chapter 16

#### The Reply of the Tongue Is from the LORD
**v1** The plans of the heart belong to man, but the reply of the tongue is from the LORD.

**v2** All a man's ways are pure in his own eyes, but his motives are weighed out by the LORD.

**v3** Commit your works to the LORDand your plans will be achieved.

**v4** The LORD has made everything for His purpose—even the wicked for the day of disaster.

**v5** Everyone who is proud in heart is detestable to the LORD; be assured that he will not go unpunished.

**v6** By loving devotion and faithfulness iniquity is atoned for, and by the fear of the LORD one turns aside from evil.

**v7** When a man's ways please the LORD, He makes even the man's enemies live at peace with him.

**v8** Better a little with righteousnessthan great gain with injustice.

**v9** A man's heart plans his course, but the LORD determines his steps.

**v10** A divine verdict is on the lips of a king; his mouth must not betray justice.

**v11** Honest scales and balances are from the LORD; all the weights in the bag are His concern.

**v12** Wicked behavior is detestable for kings, for a throne is established through righteousness.

**v13** Righteous lips are a king's delight, and he who speaks honestly is beloved.

**v14** The wrath of a king is a messenger of death, but a wise man will pacify it.

**v15** When a king's face brightens, there is life; his favor is like a rain cloud in spring.

**v16** How much better to acquire wisdom than gold!To gain understanding is more desirable than silver.

**v17** The highway of the upright leads away from evil; he who guards his way protects his life.

**v18** Pride goes before destruction, and a haughty spirit before a fall.

**v19** It is better to be lowly in spirit among the humblethan to divide the spoil with the proud.

**v20** Whoever heeds instruction will find success, [^1] and blessed is he who trusts in the LORD.

**v21** The wise in heart are called discerning, and pleasant speech promotes instruction.

**v22** Understanding is a fountain of life to its possessor, but the discipline of fools is folly.

**v23** The heart of the wise man instructs his mouthand adds persuasiveness to his lips.

**v24** Pleasant words are a honeycomb, sweet to the soul and healing to the bones.

**v25** There is a way that seems right to a man, but its end is the way of death.

**v26** A worker's appetite works for himbecause his hunger drives him onward.

**v27** A worthless man digs up evil, and his speech [^2] is like a scorching fire.

**v28** A perverse man spreads dissension, and a gossip divides close friends.

**v29** A violent man entices his neighborand leads him down a path that is not good.

**v30** He who winks his eye devises perversity; he who purses his lips is bent on evil.

**v31** Gray hair is a crown of glory; it is attained along the path of righteousness.

**v32** He who is slow to anger is better than a warrior, and he who controls his temper is greater than one who captures a city.

**v33** The lot is cast into the lap, but its every decision is from the LORD.
[^1]: Or Whoever speaks prudently will find what is good ( 16:20)
[^2]: Or and what is on his lips ( 16:27)

### Chapter 17

#### Better a Dry Morsel in Quietness
**v1** Better a dry morsel in quietnessthan a house full of feasting [^1] with strife.

**v2** A wise servant will rule over a disgraceful sonand share his inheritance as one of the brothers.

**v3** A crucible for silver and a furnace for gold, but the LORD is the tester of hearts.

**v4** A wicked man listens to evil lips; a liar gives ear to a destructive tongue.

**v5** He who mocks the poor insults their Maker; whoever gloats over calamity will not go unpunished.

**v6** Grandchildren are the crown of the aged, and the glory of a son is his father.

**v7** Eloquent words are unfit for a fool; how much worse are lying lips to a ruler!

**v8** A bribe is a charm to its giver; wherever he turns, he succeeds.

**v9** Whoever conceals an offense promotes love, but he who brings it up separates friends.
